# nucl-ex [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [First measurements of deuteron production spectra in p+p collisions at beam momentum of 158 GeV/c at NA61/SHINE](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22545)
*Anirvan Shukla*

Main category: nucl-ex

TL;DR: NA61/SHINE实验首次测量了158 GeV/c质子-质子非弹性碰撞中氘核的双微分产生谱，为宇宙反核子背景建模提供关键数据，以支持暗物质探测研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探测宇宙反核子（cosmic antinuclei）是识别暗物质（dark matter）的突破性方法，而宇宙反核子的主要背景源是宇宙射线质子与星际氢气的相互作用。深入了解质子-质子相互作用中氘核的产生机制是建模宇宙反核子产生的关键第一步。

Method: 使用位于CERN超级质子同步加速器（Super Proton Synchrotron, SPS）的NA61/SHINE谱仪，在入射动量158 GeV/c（$\sqrt{s}$ = 17.3 GeV）条件下测量质子-质子非弹性碰撞（inelastic p+p interactions）中氘核的产生。测量了作为快度（rapidity）和横向动量（transverse momentum）函数的双微分谱。

Result: 首次获得了与宇宙射线研究相关的能量下氘核的微分产生测量结果，并将双微分谱与热模型（thermal model）和聚结模型（coalescence model）的预测进行了比较。

Conclusion: 这些测量对于改进对宇宙（反）核子产生的理解至关重要，为建模宇宙反核子产生提供了必要的基础数据，有助于区分暗物质信号与背景。

Abstract: The NA61/SHINE spectrometer at the CERN Super Proton Synchrotron (SPS) scans particle production in collisions of nuclei with various sizes at a set of energies covering the SPS energy range towards various physics goals.
  This paper presents the first differential production measurements of deuterons at energies relevant for cosmic-ray studies, produced in inelastic p+p interactions at incident projectile momentum of 158 GeV/c ($\sqrt{s}$ = 17.3 GeV). The double-differential spectra are presented as functions of rapidity and transverse momentum and are compared to predictions of the thermal and coalescence models.
  These measurements are essential for improving our understanding of cosmic (anti)nuclei production, as detecting cosmic antinuclei can be a breakthrough approach to identifying dark matter. The primary source of cosmic antinuclei background is interactions between cosmic-ray protons and interstellar hydrogen gas. Gaining a deeper insight into the deuteron production mechanism in p+p interactions is an essential first step in modeling cosmic antinuclei production.

</details>


<div id='nucl-th'></div>

# nucl-th [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [Hall Viscosity in the Quark-Gluon Plasma](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23498)
*Sukrut Mondkar,Giorgio Torrieri,Matthias Kaminski,René Meyer*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了非中心重离子碰撞中产生的夸克胶子等离子体（QGP）的霍尔粘度（Hall viscosity）。在强磁场或涡旋存在下，旋转对称性从O(3)破缺到O(2)，导致出现两个独立的霍尔粘度分量。研究发现霍尔粘度在量级上与零磁场下的剪切粘度相当，并对流动和事件平面关联产生可观测效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究非中心重离子碰撞中产生的夸克胶子等离子体（quark gluon plasma, QGP）的霍尔粘度特性。在强磁场或涡旋（vorticity）存在下，旋转对称性破缺为理解QGP的输运性质提供了新的物理视角。

Method: 通过将动力学理论（kinetic-theory）机制扩展到三维空间，推导相应的本构关系（constitutive relations）。同时采用全息（holographic）方法进行估计，并在实际QGP条件下提供参数化估计。

Result: 发现存在两个独立的霍尔粘度分量，分别对应于与对称性破缺方向垂直和平行的剪切形变。动力学理论和全息估计均表明，霍尔粘度的量级与零磁场下的剪切粘度相当。霍尔粘性应力在流体动力学初始化时可能与标准粘性修正相当。

Conclusion: 霍尔粘度在QGP中具有显著物理效应，其量级与剪切粘度相当。研究识别了霍尔粘性应力在流动（flow）和事件平面关联（event-plane correlations）中的可观测后果，为实验探测提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We study the Hall viscosity of the quark gluon plasma (QGP) created in non-central heavy-ion collisions. In the presence of a strong magnetic field or vorticity, rotational symmetry is broken from O(3) to O(2), allowing for two independent Hall viscosities associated with shear deformations transverse and parallel to the symmetry-breaking direction. We find the corresponding constitutive relations by extending the kinetic-theory mechanism to three spatial dimensions and provide parametric estimates of the Hall viscosities under realistic QGP conditions. Both kinetic-theory and holographic estimates indicate that Hall viscosities are comparable in magnitude to the shear viscosity at zero magnetic field. We further show that Hall viscous stresses at hydrodynamic initialization can be as large as standard viscous corrections and identify observable consequences in flow and event-plane correlations.

</details>


<div id='hep-ex'></div>

# hep-ex [[Back]](#toc)

### [3] [Probing unexplored spin-dependent dark matter-proton coupling with few-photoelectron threshold in COSINE-100](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22411)
*W. K. Kim,N. Carlin,J. Y. Cho,S. J. Cho,S. Choi,A. C. Ezeribe,L. E. França,R. F. Muhdi,O. Gileva,C. Ha,I. S. Hahn,E. J. Jeon,H. W. Joo,W. G. Kang,M. Kauer,B. H. Kim,D. Y. Kim,H. J. Kim,J. Kim,K. W. Kim,S. H. Kim,S. K. Kim,Y. D. Kim,Y. H. Kim,B. R. Ko,Y. J. Ko,B. C. Koh,D. H. Lee,E. K. Lee,H. Lee,H. S. Lee,H. Y. Lee,I. S. Lee,J. Lee,J. Y. Lee,M. H. Lee,S. H. Lee,S. H. Lee,Y. J. Lee,D. S. Leonard,N. T. Luan,V. H. A. Machado,B. B. Manzato,R. H. Maruyama,S. L. Olsen,H. K. Park,H. S. Park,J. C. Park,J. S. Park,K. S. Park,K. Park,S. D. Park,R. L. C. Pitta,H. Prihtiadi,C. Rott,K. A. Shin,D. F. F. S. Cavalcante,M. K. Son,N. J. C. Spooner,L. T. Truc,L. Yang,G. H. Yu*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: COSINE-100实验通过多层感知机事件选择和噪声抑制技术，将探测阈值降至3-4个孤立光电子，在低质量暗物质参数空间设定了世界领先的约束限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在探索低质量暗物质与质子的自旋相关散射截面，特别是在先前未研究的少光电子区域，该区域光电倍增管噪声和磷光效应显著。

Method: 采用多层感知机（multi-layer perceptron）进行专门的事件选择，结合稳健的噪声抑制技术，将探测阈值降至3-4个孤立光电子。使用现象学背景模型（phenomenological background model）搜索标准晕模型（Standard Halo Model）预期的年度调制信号，并纳入米格达尔效应（Migdal effect）扩展灵敏度。

Result: 数据中未观察到统计显著的年度调制信号。在1.75-2.25 GeV/c²质量范围内设定了90%置信水平上限，成为该区域最严格的自旋相关暗物质-质子散射截面约束。通过米格达尔效应，在15-58 MeV/c²亚GeV/c²区域设定了世界领先的限制。

Conclusion: 研究证明了NaI(Tl)靶材料在探索先前未开发的暗物质参数空间区域的能力，特别是在低质量暗物质探测方面取得了重要进展。

Abstract: We report new constraints on the spin-dependent scattering cross section between low-mass dark matter and protons using data collected by the COSINE-100 experiment. By implementing a specialized event selection process using a multi-layer perceptron and robust noise mitigation, this analysis pioneers a detection threshold of 3 and 4 isolated peaks, corresponding to the reconstructed photoelectrons, which is significantly lower than the 8 photoelectron threshold used in previous analyses. In this unstudied few-photoelectron regime, where PMT-induced noise and phosphorescence are prevalent, we utilize a phenomenological background model to search for the annual modulation signal expected from the Standard Halo Model. No statistically significant annual modulation is observed in our data. We derive new 90% confidence level upper limits for the spin-dependent DM-proton cross section, establishing the world's most stringent constraints in the 1.75-2.25 GeV/c$^2$ mass range. Furthermore, by incorporating the Migdal effect, we extend the experimental sensitivity to the sub-GeV/c$^2$ regime, setting world-leading limits in the 15-58 MeV/c$^2$ range. These results demonstrate the capability of NaI(Tl) target materials to probe previously unexplored regions of the dark matter parameter space.

</details>


### [4] [Measurement and interpretation of inclusive $Wγ$ production in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}=13$ TeV using the ATLAS detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22478)
*ATLAS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文报告了ATLAS实验在13 TeV质子-质子对撞中测量W玻色子与光子联合产生微分截面的研究，使用140 fb⁻¹数据，通过16个可观测量探测Wγ系统性质，并用于约束有效场论中的维六算符。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究W玻色子与光子联合产生过程旨在探测标准模型（Standard Model）中的三重规范耦合（triple gauge coupling），特别是WWγ耦合的结构。该测量可用于检验辐射振幅零点效应（radiation amplitude zero effect）、W玻色子极化（polarisation）以及质子部分子分布函数（parton distribution functions）。

Method: 分析使用ATLAS实验在√s=13 TeV收集的质子-质子对撞数据，对应积分亮度140 fb⁻¹。测量在Wγ→ℓνγ衰变道（ℓ=e,μ）中进行，定义了16个微分截面可观测量。数据经过探测器效率（detector inefficiency）和分辨率（resolution）修正，并与SHERPA、MADGRAPH5_aMC@NLO和GENEVA的理论预测进行比较。

Result: 微分截面测量精度足以区分不同先进理论预测。研究发现了基于神经网络输出的探测器修正可观测量对CP-odd算符特别敏感。在有效场论（effective field theory）框架下，对𝒪_W、𝒪_HWB、𝒪_Ŵ和𝒪_HŴB算符的威尔逊系数（Wilson coefficients）给出了约束，其中𝒪_HŴB算符的灵敏度相比先前其他末态测量提高了2.5倍。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了Wγ联合产生过程的精确微分截面测量，可用于探测标准模型三重规范耦合和检验超出标准模型物理。基于神经网络的可观测量显著增强了对CP-odd维六算符的探测灵敏度，为有效场论分析提供了重要约束。

Abstract: Differential cross-section measurements are presented for the production of a $W$ boson in association with a photon. The analysis is performed using proton--proton collision data collected by the ATLAS experiment at $\sqrt{s}= 13$ TeV, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 140~fb$^{-1}$. The differential cross sections are measured in the $Wγ\rightarrow \ell νγ$ decay channel ($\ell=e,μ$) as a function of 16 observables. Collectively, these observables probe the kinematic properties of the $Wγ$ system, the radiation amplitude zero effect predicted for the $Wγ$ final state, the polarisation of the $W$ boson, the charge conjugation and parity structure of the $WWγ$ triple gauge coupling, and the parton distribution functions of the proton. The data are corrected for the effects of detector inefficiency and resolution and are sufficiently precise that they can be used to distinguish between different state-of-the-art theoretical predictions provided by SHERPA, MADGRAPH5_aMC@NLO, and GENEVA. The differential cross sections are used to search for anomalous weak-boson self-interactions induced by dimension-six operators within an effective field theory. For CP-odd operators, dedicated detector-corrected observables based on the outputs of neural networks are found to be particularly sensitive to the interference between the Standard Model and dimension-six scattering amplitudes. Constraints are placed on the Wilson coefficients of the $\mathcal {o}_{W}$, $\mathcal{o}_{HWB}$, $\mathcal{o}_{\tilde{W}}$ and $\mathcal{o}_{H{\tilde{W}B}}$ operators in the effective field theory. The sensitivity to the $\mathcal{o}_{H{\tilde{W}B}}$ operator is improved by a factor of 2.5 compared to previous measurements in other final states.

</details>


### [5] [First search for sterile neutrino oscillation leading to $ν_μ$ disappearance in the Booster Neutrino Beam at ICARUS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22557)
*ICARUS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: ICARUS探测器在费米实验室Booster中微子束（BNB）中搜索μ子中微子消失现象，在600米基线距离上未发现统计显著的中微子振荡证据，并给出了在3+1 sterile中微子模型参数空间的排除限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在利用ICARUS探测器在Booster中微子束（BNB）中搜索μ子中微子消失现象，以检验sterile中微子（sterile neutrino）存在的可能性。这是ICARUS首次暴露于BNB束流下进行的中微子振荡分析。

Method: 研究选取了2022-2023年（ICARUS Run 2）的数据，选择通过带电电流相互作用（charged current interaction）与氩核相互作用、且末态仅包含一个μ子和至少一个质子（1μNp）的μ子中微子事例。使用基于模拟的预期进行比较，并在3+1 sterile中微子模型的二中微子近似框架下进行拟合。

Result: 在ICARUS距离BNB靶600米的基线距离上，未发现统计显著的μ子中微子消失现象。研究给出了在Δm²₄₁ - sin²2θₘₘ参数空间中90%置信水平（C.L.）的排除轮廓。分析受到系统不确定性的限制，主要来自通量模型和中微子相互作用模型的大未约束不确定性。

Conclusion: 这是ICARUS首次在BNB束流下进行的中微子振荡分析，未发现sterile中微子存在的证据。未来ICARUS与SBND探测器（距离靶110米）的联合分析将显著约束系统不确定性，实现世界领先的双探测器分析。

Abstract: We present a search for muon neutrino disappearance in the Booster Neutrino Beam (BNB) at Fermilab using the ICARUS detector. Neutrino interactions identified as muon neutrinos interacting with argon nuclei via the charged current interaction and having only a muon and at least one proton in the final state (1$μ$Np) have been selected from data collected in 2022-2023 (ICARUS Run 2) and compared with a simulation-based expectation. In the context of a fit to a two-neutrino approximation of the sterile 3+1 model, including the impact of systematic uncertainty from the flux, neutrino interaction, and detector models, we find no statistically significant muon neutrino disappearance at the ICARUS baseline of 600 meters from the BNB target. Corresponding 90% C.L. exclusion contours in $Δm^2_{41}$ - sin$^22θ_{μμ}$ space are presented. This is the first oscillation analysis produced by ICARUS exposed to the BNB. We note that the analysis is systematics limited due to large unconstrained uncertainties from the flux and interaction models. In future joint analyses, data from ICARUS and the SBND detector, exposed to the BNB at 110 meters from target, will be combined to provide significant constraint of these uncertainties, enabling a robust, world-leading two-detector analysis.

</details>

*BESIII Collaboration,M. Ablikim,M. N. Achasov,P. Adlarson,X. C. Ai,R. Aliberti,A. Amoroso,Q. An,Y. Bai,O. Bakina,Y. Ban,H. -R. Bao,V. Batozskaya,K. Begzsuren,N. Berger,M. Berlowski,M. B. Bertani,D. Zhu,J. Zhu,K. Zhu,K. J. Zhu,K. S. Zhu,L. X. Zhu,Lin Zhu,S. H. Zhu,T. J. Zhu,W. D. Zhu,W. J. Zhu,W. Z. Zhu,Y. C. Zhu,Z. A. Zhu,X. Y. Zhuang,J. H. Zou*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: BESIII合作组利用20.3 fb⁻¹的正负电子对撞数据，首次在粲介子辐射衰变到轴矢量介子的过程中检验矢量介子主导机制，未观测到显著信号，并确定了分支比上限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在检验矢量介子主导（Vector Meson Dominance, VMD）机制在粲介子辐射衰变到轴矢量介子过程中的适用性。这是首次在该类衰变过程中对VMD机制进行实验验证。

Method: 利用BESIII探测器在BEPCII对撞机上收集的20.3 fb⁻¹正负电子对撞数据，质心能量为3.773 GeV。搜索了辐射衰变道D⁰→γK̄₁(1270)⁰和D⁺→γK₁(1270)⁺。

Result: 未观测到显著信号，在90%置信水平下确定了分支比上限：D⁰→γK̄₁(1270)⁰为7.7×10⁻⁴，D⁺→γK₁(1270)⁺为3.9×10⁻⁵。

Conclusion: 该研究首次在粲介子辐射衰变到轴矢量介子的过程中检验了矢量介子主导机制，为理解粲介子辐射衰变机制提供了重要实验约束。

Abstract: A search for the radiative decays $D^0\to γ\bar K_1(1270)^0$ and $D^+\to γK_1(1270)^+$ is conducted using $20.3~\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$ of $e^+e^-$ annihilation data collected at the center-of-mass energy $\sqrt{s}=3.773$ GeV by the BESIII detector operating at the BEPCII collider. No significant signals are observed, and upper limits on the branching fractions of $D^0\to γ\bar K_1(1270)^0$ and $D^+\to γK_1(1270)^+$ at 90\% confidence level are determined to be $7.7\times10^{-4}$ and $3.9\times10^{-5}$, respectively. This represents the first test of the Vector Meson Dominance mechanism in the radiative decays of charmed mesons to axial-vector mesons.

</details>

Zhuge,J. H. Zou,J. Zu*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: BESIII合作组利用(10087±44)×10⁶个J/ψ事例，首次对J/ψ→γηπ⁰衰变过程进行振幅分析，观测到多个中间过程贡献，首次发现J/ψ到同位旋三重态标量介子的辐射跃迁，并将分支比测量精度提高一倍以上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在首次对J/ψ→γηπ⁰衰变过程进行振幅分析，以深入理解该衰变机制中的中间过程贡献，特别是探索J/ψ到同位旋三重态标量介子的辐射跃迁过程。

Method: 利用BESIII探测器收集的(10087±44)×10⁶个J/ψ事例，采用振幅分析方法对J/ψ→γηπ⁰衰变过程进行分析，识别并量化不同中间过程的贡献。

Result: 分析发现衰变主要由J/ψ→π⁰b₀(→γη)、J/ψ→π⁰ρ(1450)⁰(→γη)和J/ψ→ηh₁(1170)(→γπ⁰)等中间过程主导；首次以超过5σ统计显著性观测到J/ψ→γa₀(980)⁰(→ηπ⁰)、J/ψ→γa₂(1320)⁰(→ηπ⁰)和J/ψ→γa₂(1700)⁰(→ηπ⁰)的贡献，构成J/ψ到同位旋三重态标量介子辐射跃迁的首个观测证据。

Conclusion: J/ψ→γηπ⁰的总分支比测量结果为(25.7±0.3±1.5)×10⁻⁶，与先前测量结果一致，但精度提高了一倍以上，为理解粲偶素衰变机制和标量介子性质提供了重要实验依据。

Abstract: Using $(10087 \pm 44)\times 10^{6}$ $\jpsi$ events collected with the BESIII detector, we perform the first amplitude analysis of the process $\jpsi\toγη\piz$. The decay is dominated by the intermediate processes $\jpsi\to\piz \bo \left( \toγη\right)$, $\jpsi\to\pizρ(1450)^0 \left( \toγη\right)$ and $\jpsi\toηh_1(1170) \left( \toγ\piz\right)$. Contributions from $\jpsi\toγa_0(980)^0(\toη\piz)$, $\jpsi\toγa_2(1320)^0(\toη\piz)$ and $\jpsi\toγa_2(1700)^0(\toη\piz)$ are observed with a statistical significance exceeding $5σ$, constituting the first observation of radiative transitions of $\jpsi$ to isospin-triplet scalar mesons. The total branching fraction of $\jpsi\toγη\piz$ is measured to be \num{25.7\pm0.3\pm1.5e-6}, where the first uncertainty is statistical and the second systematic. This result is consistent with the previous measurement, with the precision improved by more than a factor of two.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: keV质量范围的惰性中微子（sterile neutrinos）是标准模型（Standard Model）的有力扩展，也是可行的暗物质候选者。实验室实验可以通过探测β衰变电子能谱中的特征性扭折状畸变（kink-like distortion）来验证其存在。

Method: KATRIN实验在完成电子中微子质量测量后，将利用新开发的TRISTAN探测器阵列——一种针对高计数率和远低于端点能量（endpoint）的微分测量优化的硅漂移探测器阵列（silicon drift detector array），搜索keV尺度的惰性中微子。研究采用专门的模拟框架进行灵敏度预测。

Result: 通过模拟分析，KATRIN在4个月探测器有效时间内，对（4-13）keV质量范围的惰性中微子，具有探测$|U_{e4}|^2 \sim 10^{-6}$水平混合振幅的统计能力，显著超越了先前实验室搜索的范围。实验系统不确定性的主要影响使灵敏度在同一质量范围内降低了10-50倍。

Conclusion: KATRIN实验通过TRISTAN探测器阵列的部署，将显著扩展对keV尺度惰性中微子的探测能力，为暗物质候选者的实验室验证提供新的可能性，尽管系统不确定性对灵敏度有显著影响。

Abstract: Sterile neutrinos in the keV mass range are a well-motivated extension of the Standard Model and viable dark matter candidates. Their existence can be probed in laboratory experiments, as the admixture of a sterile state would induce a characteristic kink-like distortion in the $β$-decay electron energy spectrum. The KATRIN experiment is designed to measure the effective electron neutrino mass with sub-eV sensitivity by analyzing the endpoint region of the tritium $β$-decay spectrum. Following the completion of its neutrino mass program, KATRIN will extend its physics reach to the search for keV-scale sterile neutrinos. This effort will be enabled by the TRISTAN detector, a newly developed silicon drift detector array optimized for differential measurements at high rates and energies well below the endpoint. In this article, we present the projected sensitivity of KATRIN to keV-scale sterile neutrinos using a dedicated simulation framework. With four months of detector livetime, KATRIN has the statistical power to probe mixing amplitudes at the level of $|U_{e4}|^2 \sim 10^{-6}$ for sterile neutrino masses in the (4$-$13) keV range, significantly extending the reach of previous laboratory searches. The major experimental systematic uncertainties investigated in this work reduces the sensitivity by a factor of 10$-$50 over the same mass range.

### [9] [Contrastive Metric Learning for Point Cloud Segmentation in Highly Granular Detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23356)
*Max Marriott-Clarke,Lazar Novakovic,Elizabeth Ratzer,Robert J. Bainbridge,Loukas Gouskos,Benedikt Maier*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于监督对比度量学习（CML）的新型点云分割聚类方法，该方法在模拟高粒度量热器数据上相比对象凝聚（OC）方法表现出更优的性能，特别是在高多重性区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对高粒度量热器中高度重叠粒子簇射（particle showers）的分割问题，需要一种能够有效分离重叠簇射并提高重建效率的方法。传统对象中心化方法在处理此类复杂重叠场景时存在局限性。

Method: 该方法采用监督对比度量学习（supervised contrastive metric learning, CML）学习潜在表示，使属于同一对象的点嵌入相近，无关点相互分离。然后使用基于密度的读出（density-based readout）在学习的度量空间中重建聚类，实现表示学习与聚类形成的解耦。

Result: CML方法为电磁和强子粒子簇射产生了更稳定、可分离的嵌入几何结构，提高了局部邻域一致性，更可靠地分离了重叠簇射，并在外推到未见多重性和能量时表现出更好的泛化能力。这直接转化为更高的重建效率和纯度，特别是在高多重性区域，以及改进的能量分辨率。

Conclusion: 基于相似性的表示学习结合基于密度的聚合是高粒度探测器中点云分割的一种有前景的替代方案，相比对象中心化方法具有更强的鲁棒性，特别是在混合粒子环境中。

Abstract: We propose a novel clustering approach for point-cloud segmentation based on supervised contrastive metric learning (CML). Rather than predicting cluster assignments or object-centric variables, the method learns a latent representation in which points belonging to the same object are embedded nearby while unrelated points are separated. Clusters are then reconstructed using a density-based readout in the learned metric space, decoupling representation learning from cluster formation and enabling flexible inference. The approach is evaluated on simulated data from a highly granular calorimeter, where the task is to separate highly overlapping particle showers represented as sets of calorimeter hits. A direct comparison with object condensation (OC) is performed using identical graph neural network backbones and equal latent dimensionality, isolating the effect of the learning objective. The CML method produces a more stable and separable embedding geometry for both electromagnetic and hadronic particle showers, leading to improved local neighbourhood consistency, a more reliable separation of overlapping showers, and better generalization when extrapolating to unseen multiplicities and energies. This translates directly into higher reconstruction efficiency and purity, particularly in high-multiplicity regimes, as well as improved energy resolution. In mixed-particle environments, CML maintains strong performance, suggesting robust learning of the shower topology, while OC exhibits significant degradation. These results demonstrate that similarity-based representation learning combined with density-based aggregation is a promising alternative to object-centric approaches for point cloud segmentation in highly granular detectors.

</details>


### [10] [Resonant Parameters of Vector Charmonium-like States above 4.4 GeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23418)
*Chunhua Li,Wanting Liu,Linfa Tang,Ying Ding*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于分析BESIII实验测量的多个e⁺e⁻→强子过程的截面数据，这些数据包含对理解粲偶素共振态性质至关重要的信息。通过系统分析这些过程，可以揭示不同共振态在特定衰变道中的贡献模式。

Method: 采用χ²最小化拟合（χ²-minimized fit）方法，同时对BESIII实验测量的六个过程的截面数据进行拟合分析。分析基于四个粲偶素共振态结构：ψ(4230)、ψ(4500)、ψ(4660)和ψ(4710)。

Result: 获得了四个共振态的质量和宽度参数。研究发现e⁺e⁻→Dₛ⁺Dₛ₁*⁻(2536)、e⁺e⁻→Dₛ⁺Dₛ₂*⁻(2573)和e⁺e⁻→φχ_{c1,2}这三个过程主要来源于ψ(4660)和ψ(4710)的衰变贡献。

Conclusion: 研究通过系统分析多个强子产生过程，确定了四个粲偶素共振态的参数，并揭示了ψ(4660)和ψ(4710)在特定Dₛ介子和φχ_{c}衰变道中的主导作用，为理解这些共振态的性质提供了重要信息。

Abstract: We analysis the $\sqrt{s}$-dependent line shapes of the $e^+e^-\to D_s^{+}D_{s1}^{*-}(2536)$, $D_s^{+}D_{s2}^{*-}(2573)$, $φχ_{c1,2}$, $K^+K^-J/ψ$, $K_S^0 K_S^0 J/ψ$, and $K^+K^-ψ(2S)$ cross sections measured by the BESIII experiment using the four resonant structures $ψ(4230)$, $ψ(4500)$, $ψ(4660)$, and $ψ(4710)$, by performing a simultaneous $χ^2$-minimized fit. Their masses and widths are obtained. We find that the processes $e^+e^-\to D_s^{+}D_{s1}^{*-}(2536)$, $e^+e^-\to D_s^{+}D_{s2}^{*-}(2573)$, and $e^+e^-\to φχ_{c1,2}$ are all dominantly produced via the $ψ(4660)$ and $ψ(4710)$ decays.

### [11] [Search for new particles decaying into top quark-antiquark pairs in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23454)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该研究利用CMS探测器在13 TeV质心能量下收集的138 fb⁻¹质子-质子对撞数据，通过分析顶夸克-反顶夸克对衰变末态，对新型粒子进行搜索，并设定了迄今最严格的模型排除限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在搜索衰变到顶夸克-反顶夸克对（top quark-antiquark pairs）的新粒子，以探索超出标准模型（beyond the Standard Model）的物理现象，特别是通过分析不同轻子（lepton）末态来覆盖所有可能的衰变模式。

Method: 利用CMS探测器在2016-2018年间记录的13 TeV质子-质子对撞数据，对应138 fb⁻¹的积分亮度，分析了0、1和2个轻子的末态，全面覆盖顶夸克-反顶夸克对的所有衰变模式。

Result: 排除了相对宽度为1%、10%和30%的重Z'玻色子（heavy Z' bosons），质量范围分别为0.4-4.8、0.4-6.2和0.4-7.4 TeV；排除了Randall-Sundrum模型中的Kaluza-Klein胶子（Kaluza-Klein gluon）和暗物质媒介子（dark-matter mediator），质量范围分别为0.5-5.5和1.0-4.2 TeV；在双希格斯二重态模型（two-Higgs-doublet models）中，对质量为0.5-1.0 TeV、相对宽度为2.5%、10%和25%的标量和赝标量希格斯玻色子设定了耦合强度修正因子的上限。

Conclusion: 这些结果为所考虑模型在顶夸克-反顶夸克对末态中设定了迄今最严格的排除限，显著推进了对超出标准模型物理的探索，特别是在重粒子搜索和暗物质相关模型方面。

Abstract: A search for new particles decaying to top quark-antiquark pairs is performed using proton-proton collision data at a centre-of-mass energy of 13 TeV. The data set recorded with the CMS detector between 2016 and 2018 is used, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 138 fb$^{-1}$. Final states with 0, 1, and 2 leptons are analyzed, covering all decay modes of the top quark-antiquark pairs. Heavy Z' bosons with relative widths of 1, 10, and 30% are excluded for masses in the ranges 0.4$-$4.8, 0.4$-$6.2, and 0.4$-$7.4 TeV, respectively. A Kaluza$-$Klein gluon in the Randall$-$Sundrum model and a dark-matter mediator are excluded for masses between 0.5$-$5.5 and 1.0$-$4.2 TeV, respectively. These results set the most stringent limits to date for the considered models in the $\mathrm{t\bar{t}}$ final state. In addition, in the two-Higgs-doublet models, upper limits are set on the coupling strength modifier for scalar and pseudoscalar Higgs bosons with relative widths of 2.5, 10, and 25% in the mass range of 0.5$-$1.0 TeV.

### [12] [Multivariable Painleve'-II equation: connection formulas for asymptotic solutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22470)
*N. A. Sinitsyn*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文证明了一个包含对称性破缺项的广义Painlevé-II方程系统是可积的，并利用其Lax对通过渐近精确WKB方法关联不同无穷远处的渐近行为，应用包括二阶相变中不稳定真空衰变问题的精确标度分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索具有对称性破缺项的广义Painlevé-II方程系统的可积性，并建立其数学结构与物理应用之间的联系，特别是二阶相变中不稳定真空衰变等物理问题。

Method: 方法包括：证明广义Painlevé-II方程系统的可积性，构造其Lax对，采用渐近精确WKB方法分析不同无穷远处的渐近行为，并利用量子力学Demkov-Osherov模型的精确解作为分析基础。

Result: 主要结果包括：证明了具有对称性破缺项的广义Painlevé-II方程系统的可积性，建立了通过Lax对和WKB方法关联渐近行为的数学框架，并将该理论应用于二阶相变中不稳定真空衰变问题，获得了激发数目的精确标度行为，包括次要贡献。

Conclusion: 结论表明该广义Painlevé-II方程系统具有可积性，其数学框架能够精确描述物理系统的渐近行为，特别是在相变动力学中提供了包含次要贡献的精确标度关系，建立了可积系统理论与物理应用之间的重要联系。

Abstract: It is shown that a generalization of the Painlevé-II equation (P-II) to a system of coupled equations with symmetry breaking terms is integrable. A Lax pair for this system is used to relate the asymptotic behavior of the solutions at different infinities via an asymptotically exact WKB approach. The analysis relies on an exact solution of the quantum mechanical Demkov-Osherov model (DOM). An application to the problem of unstable vacuum decay during a second order phase transition provides precise scaling of the number of excitations, including subdominant contributions.

### [13] [Spectral topology and edge modes for one-dimensional non-Hermitian photonic crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22515)
*Junshan Lin,Hai Zhang*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过转移矩阵方法分析了非厄米光子晶体中的边缘模，建立了适用于连续波模型的新拓扑不变量，为理解非厄米系统中的趋肤效应提供了理论基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非厄米光子晶体中的光谱互易性破缺导致边缘模和趋肤效应，但离散晶格模型的Toeplitz矩阵谱理论无法应用于连续波模型，需要新的数学框架来描述连续介质中的波传播。

Method: 采用转移矩阵方法描述一维周期性介质中的波传播，并基于转移矩阵特征值引入新的谱拓扑不变量，该不变量等价于非厄米谱的绕数。

Result: 新拓扑不变量能够表征一维非厄米光子晶体中的边缘模，为连续波模型中的趋肤效应提供了理论基础，解决了有限维近似失效的问题。

Conclusion: 转移矩阵方法和基于其特征值的拓扑不变量为分析非厄米光子晶体中的边缘模和趋肤效应提供了有效的数学框架，扩展了非厄米拓扑物理的理论基础。

Abstract: This work investigates edge modes in non-Hermitian photonic crystals with broken spectral reciprocity. In such systems, the spectra of the underlying operators generally form closed loops over the complex plane with nontrivial spectral topology, which gives rise to the so-called skin effect characterized by edge modes localized at interfaces. For discrete lattice models, the skin effect can be understood through the spectral theory of Toeplitz matrices. However, this mathematical framework no longer applies to continuous wave models, where finite-dimensional approximations break down. In this work, we employ a transfer matrix approach to describe wave propagation in one-dimensional periodic media and introduce a new spectral topological invariant based on the eigenvalues of the transfer matrix. The new topological invariant is equivalent to the winding number of the non-Hermitian spectrum and it enables the characterization of edge modes in one-dimensional non-Hermitian photonic crystals. The mathematical theory provides the theoretical foundation for the skin effect in continuous wave models.

</details>


### [14] [Edge density expansions for the classical Gaussian and Laguerre ensembles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22974)
*Peter J. Forrester,Anas A. Rahman,Bo-Jian Shen*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该研究从微分方程视角重新审视了高斯和拉盖尔随机矩阵系综软边标度密度中的可积结构，并将类似分析扩展到硬边情形。研究揭示了这些渐近展开中的可积特征，并提供了高阶修正项的信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Bornemann近期研究揭示了高斯和拉盖尔随机矩阵系综软边渐近展开中隐藏的可积结构，涉及间距分布和特征值密度。本研究旨在从不同视角重新审视这些结果，并将类似分析扩展到硬边情形。

Method: 采用标量微分方程作为主要工具，该方程满足软边标度密度。与积分表示不同，这些微分方程在软边标度变量中分离了作为展开变量的函数$N$。研究还探讨了高斯系综中戴森指数$β=6$的类似特征。

Result: 对于拉盖尔系综硬边情形，给出了酉对称性下二阶修正以及正交和辛对称性下一阶修正的显式形式。在高斯系综中，戴森指数$β=6$展示了类似特征，表明经典$β$系综的渐近展开普遍具有可积特征。研究还证明了各种微分关系。

Conclusion: 微分方程方法为随机矩阵系综软边和硬边渐近展开提供了新的视角，揭示了其中隐藏的可积结构。该方法不仅补充了Bornemann的研究发现，还为经典$β$系综的普遍可积特征提供了证据。

Abstract: Recent work of Bornemann has uncovered hitherto hidden integrable structures relating to the asymptotic expansion of quantities at the soft edge of Gaussian and Laguerre random matrix ensembles. These quantities are spacing distributions and the eigenvalue density, and the findings cover the cases of the three symmetry classes orthogonal, unitary and symplectic. In this work we give a different viewpoint on these results in the case of the soft edge scaled density, and in the Laguerre case we initiate an analogous study at the hard edge. Our tool is the scalar differential equation satisfied by the latter, known from earlier work. Unlike integral representations, these differential equations in soft edge scaling variables isolate the function of $N$ which is the expansion variable. Moreover, they give information on the correction terms which supplements the findings from the work of Bornemann. In the case of the Gaussian ensemble, we can demonstrate analogous features for Dyson index $β= 6$, which suggests a broader class of models, namely the classical $β$ ensembles, with asymptotic expansions exhibiting integrable features. For the Laguerre ensembles at the hard edge, we give the explicit form of the correction at second order for unitary symmetry, and at first order in the orthogonal and symplectic cases. Various differential relations are demonstrated.

</details>

In the constant-gauge, invertible setting, the endpoint reduced $η$ contributions cancel, so the APS index vanishes. For smooth gauge families, the APS projector becomes discontinuous when a boundary mode crosses zero. We therefore introduce a regularized APS-type family of self-adjoint endpoint conditions that remains continuous across such crossings. This regularized family admits a real-symplectic boundary formulation within the standard spectral-flow/Maslov framework: for nondegenerate regularization, the zero-mode set coincides with the boundary-zero set, and transverse boundary zeros give isolated regular crossings.

### [17] [Interfacial instability as a trigger for dryout inception in two-phase CO2 flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23371)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究提出了两相环状流的数学模型，通过线性理论分析气液界面的稳定性。稳定性分析简化为求解耦合的四阶微分特征值问题，采用基于Chebyshev-τ方法的内部代码进行数值处理。

Result: 数值研究识别出导致界面不稳定的临界蒸汽干度值x_dry。该预测结果与两个独立实验活动收集的实验数据相符，验证了干涸起始由界面不稳定性控制的假设。

Conclusion: 研究证实了干涸起始由气液界面不稳定性触发的新假设，为高能粒子探测器微通道冷却系统的干涸现象提供了理论解释和预测方法。

Abstract: Progress in particle physic leads to increasing in detector luminosity and a consequent increasing overheating induced by Joule effect. An effective cooling strategy is the exploitation of CO\textsubscript{2} heat latency in phase-change. An additional challenge, relevant to detectors for High Energy Particles, is the consequent geometrical constrain due to the limited space avialable for the cooling system within the detector arrangement, leading to the implementation of cooling system by means of millichannels. In this context, at relative high vapour quality the liquid phase exhibits annular flow, anticipating the dryout. Dryout is a critical condition where the heat transfer coefficient dramatically drops and dangerous temperature levels can be reached, potentially leading to catastrophic consequences. Experimental evidences reveal that its behavior in two-phase annular flows differs from conventional refrigerants and the fundamental inception-mechanism is not yet understood. This study aims at investigating the key new idea whereby dryout inception is triggered by instability of the liquid-vapour interface. A mathematical model for two-phase annular flow is presented and the stability of the interface between the two fluids is studied through the linear theory. The stability analysis reduces to solving a coupled forth-order differential eigenvalue problem that is treated numerically with an in-house code based on the Chebyshev-$τ$ method. Numerical investigations identify a critical value for the vapour quality, named $x_{dry}$, that leads to interface instability. The resulting predictions on $x_{dry}$ are confirmed by experimental data collected from two independent experimental campaigns, validating the hypothesis that dryout inception is governed by interfacial instabilities.

### [19] [Spectral Structure of the Mixed Hessian of the Dispersionless Toda $τ$-Function](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23424)
*Oleg Alekseev*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文分析了s-重对称单调和多项式共形映射的色散less Toda τ-函数的混合Hessian矩阵。研究发现存在两个不同的阈值：解析阈值ζ_c和几何阈值ζ_univ>ζ_c，并证明首次谱不稳定性出现在ζ_c而非ζ_univ。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究s-重对称单调和多项式共形映射的色散less Toda τ-函数混合Hessian矩阵的谱特性，特别关注其在不同阈值下的行为差异。

Method: 分析混合Hessian矩阵在对称扇区中的行为，研究加权亚临界实现的特征值分布，并继续标量Gram函数超越ζ_c的解析延拓。

Result: 发现加权亚临界实现中仅有一个对数发散特征值，其余谱保持有界；标量Gram函数在ζ_c后仍具有广义超几何描述、Cauchy-Stieltjes表示，并在特定参数范围内可实现为有界Jacobi算子的Weyl函数。

Conclusion: 解析临界性（而非单叶性的丧失）被确定为Toda Hessian矩阵的首个谱阈值，标量量在ζ_univ处保持有限。

Abstract: We analyze the mixed Hessian of the dispersionless Toda $τ$-function for the $s$-fold symmetric one-harmonic polynomial conformal map. The inverse branch exhibits two distinct thresholds: an analytic threshold $ζ_c$, where the dominant square-root singularity reaches the circle of convergence, and a later geometric threshold $ζ_{\mathrm{univ}}>ζ_c$, where the map ceases to be univalent. We prove that the first spectral instability occurs already at $ζ_c$. In each symmetry sector, the weighted subcritical realization has exactly one logarithmically diverging eigenvalue, whereas the remaining spectrum stays bounded and, after removal of the singular direction, converges to that of a compact limiting remainder. We further continue the corresponding scalar Gram functions beyond $ζ_c$, showing that they admit a generalized hypergeometric description, a Cauchy--Stieltjes representation, and, for $1\le p\le s$, a realization as Weyl functions of bounded Jacobi operators. In particular, these scalar quantities remain finite at $ζ_{\mathrm{univ}}$. This identifies analytic criticality, rather than loss of univalence, as the first spectral threshold of the Toda Hessian.

### [20] [Exact density-functional theory as parallel ensemble variational hierarchies: from Lieb's formulation to Kohn-Sham theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23399)
*Nan Sheng*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 该论文对精确密度泛函理论（exact density-functional theory）进行了形式重组，区分了相互作用与非相互作用两种变分层次结构，并澄清了Kohn-Sham辅助构造与精确理论框架之间的区别。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精确密度泛函理论（exact DFT）通常被压缩为单一叙述，但实际包含相互作用与非相互作用两种平行的变分层次结构。本文旨在重构精确DFT以澄清这些常被模糊的区分，包括功能域与可表示性类别、非相互作用支撑势结构与Kohn-Sham辅助构造之间的差异。

Method: 通过重建精确DFT围绕平行结构，区分相互作用层次（基于Lieb的系综表述）与非相互作用层次（基于精确系综非相互作用理论），并将Kohn-Sham辅助密度泛函构造视为连接两者的桥梁。从这一视角重新审视交换关联结构。

Result: 提出了精确DFT的形式重组，将分数粒子数（fractional particle number）、分段线性（piecewise linearity）、单边化学势（one-sided chemical potentials）、导数不连续性（derivative discontinuity）、分数轨道占据（fractional orbital occupations）和Janak型关系纳入统一的变分框架。交换关联结构被重新解释为相互作用与非相互作用层次之间的界面量。

Conclusion: 该形式重组澄清了压缩表述中常被模糊的区分，包括功能域与可表示性类别、非相互作用支撑势结构与Kohn-Sham辅助构造、密度再现与谱解释之间的差异，为精确DFT提供了更清晰的理论框架。

Abstract: Exact ground-state density-functional theory contains two parallel variational structures that are often compressed into a single narrative: an interacting hierarchy rooted in Lieb's ensemble formulation and a noninteracting hierarchy rooted in exact ensemble noninteracting theory. We reconstruct exact DFT around this parallel structure and distinguish both exact frameworks from the Kohn-Sham auxiliary density-functional construction that links them on a common admissible density class. From this viewpoint, the Levy-Lieb constrained search, the Hohenberg-Kohn picture, and ordinary pure-state noninteracting or Kohn-Sham formulations appear as narrower specializations under additional restrictions. The same organization also places fractional particle number, piecewise linearity, one-sided chemical potentials, derivative discontinuity, fractional orbital occupations, and Janak-type relations within a single variational picture. Exchange-correlation structure is reconsidered from the same standpoint, where it appears as the interface quantity between the interacting and noninteracting hierarchies rather than merely as the unknown remainder of the Kohn-Sham decomposition. The result is a formal reorganization of exact DFT that clarifies distinctions often blurred in compressed expositions, including functional domain versus representability class, noninteracting supporting-potential structure versus Kohn-Sham auxiliary construction, and density reproduction versus spectral interpretation.

### [21] [A unified variational framework for the inverse Kohn-Sham problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23452)
*Nan Sheng*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 该论文为逆科恩-沈（inverse Kohn-Sham）问题建立了一个统一的变分框架，将现有的多种反演表述（如Wu-Yang、Zhao-Morrison-Parr等方法）纳入同一优化理论分类体系，揭示了它们之间的内在联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 逆科恩-沈（inverse Kohn-Sham）问题旨在寻找能够重现给定电子密度的局域有效势。现有反演表述使用不同语言表达，包括简化变分优化、惩罚正则化、响应迭代和偏微分方程约束优化等，缺乏统一的理论框架。

Method: 通过两个步骤建立统一变分框架：首先，将精确密度泛函理论中嵌入的固定密度非相互作用约束搜索（fixed-density noninteracting constrained search）确定为逆KS反演的自然变分锚点；其次，展示主要反演表述如何实现相同的逆KS结构，并根据KS态方程和密度重现条件被处理为目标、约束、惩罚或可行性关系进行分类。

Result: 在该框架下，Wu-Yang方法表现为简化精确乘子（reduced exact-multiplier）表述，Zhao-Morrison-Parr方法为二次惩罚松弛（quadratic-penalty relaxation），偏微分方程约束方法为显式态约束（explicit state-constraint）表述。该视角还能容纳增广拉格朗日（augmented-Lagrangian）和全一次性残差（all-at-once residual）表述。

Conclusion: 该统一框架阐明了不同反演方法中加法常数模糊性（additive-constant ambiguity）、渐近归一化（asymptotic normalization）、非光滑变分结构（nonsmooth variational structure）和弱间隙不稳定性（weak-gap instability）的作用，为逆KS理论提供了系统化的分类和理解。

Abstract: The inverse Kohn-Sham (KS) problem seeks a local effective potential whose noninteracting ground state reproduces a prescribed electron density. Existing inversion formulations are often expressed in disparate languages, including reduced variational optimization, penalty regularization, response-based iteration, and PDE-constrained optimization. In this work, we develop a unified variational framework for inverse KS theory in two steps. First, we identify the fixed-density noninteracting constrained search embedded in exact density functional theory as the natural variational anchor of inverse KS inversion. In this setting, the KS potential appears as the variational dual object associated with density reproduction. Second, we show how the principal inversion formulations may be understood as realizations of the same inverse-KS structure and how they fit into a broader optimization-theoretic classification according to whether the KS state equations and density-reproduction condition are treated as objectives, constraints, penalties, or feasibility relations. Within this framework, Wu-Yang appears as a reduced exact-multiplier formulation, Zhao-Morrison-Parr as a quadratic-penalty relaxation, and PDE-constrained approaches as explicit state-constraint formulations. The same viewpoint also accommodates augmented-Lagrangian and all-at-once residual formulations, and clarifies the roles of additive-constant ambiguity, asymptotic normalization, nonsmooth variational structure, and weak-gap instability across inversion methods.

</details>

Abstract: Gausslets are one of the few examples of basis sets for electronic structure which allow for two-index/diagonal electron-electron interaction terms. Here we generalize the gausslet construction for the radial coordinate in three dimensions for atomic basis sets. These radial gausslets make a very compact radial basis with a relatively modest number of functions, with diagonal interaction terms. ### [23] [A Conformal Bridge for the Light Transform of QCD Correlation Functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22388)
*Hao Chen,Pier Francesco Monni,Zhaoyan Pang,Gherardo Vita,Hua Xing Zhu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种通过将关联函数（correlation functions）延拓到Wilson-Fisher固定点的方法，作为计算光变换（light transform）的共形桥梁，从而在QCD中建立局域算符关联函数与可测量对撞机关联子（collider correlators）之间的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解局域算符的关联函数（correlation functions）与可测量对撞机关联子（collider correlators）之间的联系为研究对撞机中的规范理论动力学提供了新机遇。然而，QCD的非共形性质使得光变换（light transform）的应用在最低阶微扰之外变得复杂。

Method: 提出将关联函数延拓到Wilson-Fisher固定点的方法，作为计算光变换的共形桥梁。在固定点处，四个局域算符的重整化关联函数（renormalized CF）呈现变量减少，仅依赖于两个共形交叉比（conformal cross ratios），符合真正共形场论（CFT）量的特征。

Result: 该方法首次实现了在更高圈阶进行光变换，并发现四维对撞机关联子可以从该结果中仅使用低圈数据恢复。通过计算QCD中电荷-电荷关联（QQC）在两圈阶的背对背极限，验证了该方法，再现了最近的预测。

Conclusion: 通过将关联函数延拓到Wilson-Fisher固定点，成功建立了QCD中局域算符关联函数与对撞机关联子之间的计算桥梁，克服了非共形性质带来的障碍，使更高阶微扰计算成为可能。

Abstract: Understanding the link between correlation functions (CFs) of local operators and measurable collider correlators has emerged as a new opportunity in the study of gauge theory dynamics at colliders. While in Conformal Field Theories (CFTs) this connection is established by the light transform, the non-conformal nature of QCD complicates its use beyond the lowest perturbative order. We show that a continuation of the CFs to the Wilson-Fisher fixed point can be used as a method to overcome these obstacles, serving as a conformal bridge for the evaluation of the light transform. At the fixed point, the renormalized CF of four local operators features a variable drop and only depends on two conformal cross ratios, in line with a genuine CFT quantity. This allows us to exploit CFT techniques to perform, for the first time, its light transform at higher loop orders. Remarkably, the resulting collider correlator in four dimensions can be recovered from this result simply by using lower-loop data. We demonstrate this method by computing the back-to-back limit of the charge-charge correlation (QQC) at two loops in QCD through the light transform of the CF of four vector currents in the sequential light-cone limit, reproducing a recent prediction.

</details>

Method: 通过施加体无散射条件推导求和规则，筛选出满足交叉对称性（crossing symmetry）的特殊解。在多个理论中进行微扰测试，包括一维长程版本的Ising、O(N)和Lee-Yang模型。首次计算四重扭曲算子（quadruple-twist operators）对长程Ising关联子的主要贡献，并在数值自举（numerical bootstrap）框架中应用这些求和规则。

Conclusion: 研究建立的求和规则有效连接了一维CFT的Regge极限与AdS₂高能散射过程，成功识别出描述长程模型的特殊解。这些规则在微扰理论和数值自举中均得到验证，为理解具有临界边界相互作用的AdS自由场提供了新视角。

Abstract: We study sum rules that control the Regge limit of one-dimensional conformal field theory (CFT) correlators and relate them to dual bulk scattering processes at high energies in $\mathrm{AdS}_2$. By imposing the condition that no scattering takes place in the bulk, these sum rules single out special solutions to crossing symmetry that describe long-range models, which can be understood as free fields in AdS with boundary interactions tuned to criticality. We test these sum rules perturbatively in several distinct theories, namely the 1d long-range versions of the Ising, $O(N)$ and Lee--Yang models, and find that they correctly predict the CFT data characterising these theories. Along the way we compute for the first time the leading contributions of quadruple-twist operators to the long range Ising correlator and analyse their role in the new sum rules. Finally, we explore the consequences of imposing these sum rules in a numerical bootstrap framework and find that they lead to substantial reductions in the allowed parameter space.

Abstract: We derive new integral identities for AdS propagators and further develop the Wilson network expansion for AdS Feynman diagrams. ### [29] [Holography, Brick Wall and a Little Hierarchy Problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23108)
*Vishal Gayari,Chethan Krishnan,Pradipta S. Pathak*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种AdS/CFT中砖墙（brick wall）的启发式定义：边界模式的局域体能量达到（普朗克尺度）紫外截断的位置。这实现了两个目标：(a)将砖墙框架化为体有效场论的失效判据，(b)定义是边界锚定而非视界锚定，与全息原理一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于为AdS/CFT中的砖墙概念提供更自然的定义框架。传统砖墙方法通常是视界锚定的，而本文旨在提出边界锚定的定义，使其更符合全息原理（holography）的基本思想。

Method: 方法包括：提出边界锚定的砖墙启发式定义；对BTZ黑洞直接计算新模式；进行精确数值评估正则模配分函数（normal mode partition function）；分析J方向模的非精确简并性。

Result: 结果显示：新模式在相关谱区与传统't Hooftian砖墙正则模定性不变，成功再现黑洞热力学和外视界光滑相关函数。精确数值计算揭示了砖墙范式中的"小层级"问题：由于J方向模非精确简并，面积定律系数略微次主导，除非砖墙略微超越普朗克尺度。

Conclusion: 结论指出：解决"小层级"问题的可能途径包括增加活跃物种数量，或考虑（拉伸）视界本征自由度。这些观察对黑洞量子混沌和fuzzball计划具有潜在意义，同时保留了J简并玩具模型的成功之处。

Abstract: We propose a heuristic for the brick wall in AdS/CFT: the location where a boundary mode's local bulk energy reaches a (Planckian) UV cut-off. This accomplishes two things: (a) the brick wall is framed as a breakdown criterion for bulk effective field theory, and (b) the definition is boundary-anchored rather than horizon-anchored, aligning it with holography. Near the horizon, spacetime effectively gets cut-off due to blueshift relative to the boundary, and leads to normal modes. By directly computing these new modes for the BTZ black hole, we show that they are qualitatively unchanged from conventional 't Hooftian brick wall normal modes in the relevant part of the spectrum -- successfully reproducing black hole thermodynamics and exterior smooth-horizon correlators, under similar approximations. However, unlike 't Hooft's (and our own previous) calculations, we also do an $exact$ numerical evaluation of the normal mode partition function. This allows us to identify a "little hierarchy" problem in the brick wall paradigm, irrespective of whether it is horizon-anchored or boundary-anchored: because the modes are not exactly degenerate in the $J$-direction, the coefficient of the area law is slightly subleading, unless the brick wall is slightly trans-Planckian. One way to evade the problem is to increase the number of active species. While this is certainly a possibility in string theory, we argue that a natural resolution is to take into account the degrees of freedom intrinsic to the (stretched) horizon, as suggested by the recent results in arXiv:2601.18775. We argue that this will lead to a dominant contribution from a quantum number associated to the radial direction, while retaining the successes of the $J$-degenerate toy model. We discuss the possible significance of these observations for (a) quantum chaos in black holes, and (b) the fuzzball program.

Among these moduli, the axion and dilaton are present as (pseudo-) Goldstone bosons from the spontaneous breaking of an exact (or approximate) global symmetry. These moduli have a different microscopic coupling to matter but appear kinetically coupled in such a way that their interaction can compete with gravity at low energies and have an important effect in strong gravity environments. In this talk, we will discuss some of the astrophysical implications of a stringy-inspired multi-scalar-tensor theory. In particular, we show the numerical solution of the Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkov (TOV) system of equations, necessary to probe the existence of a screening mechanism that reduces the Brans-Dicke dilaton coupling to macroscopic matter sources such as a neutron star.

*Manishankar Ailiga,Gaurav Narain*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过应用Kontsevich-Segal-Witten (KSW)容许性准则，分析了量子宇宙学中的无边界瞬子（no-boundary instanton）和酒杯几何（wine-glass geometry）的容许性。研究发现无边界瞬子是KSW容许的，而酒杯几何是KSW不容许的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在分析量子宇宙学中两种重要几何结构的容许性：作为路径积分主导鞍点的无边界瞬子（no-boundary instanton），以及作为次主导鞍点但被认为具有更长宇宙暴胀阶段的酒杯几何（wine-glass geometry）。研究动机源于KSW容许性准则的要求，该准则基于几何结构上能否定义有意义的量子场论（QFT）来分类几何。

Method: 研究方法采用Kontsevich-Segal-Witten (KSW)容许性准则的较温和版本，对无边界瞬子和酒杯几何进行容许性分析。该方法基于几何结构上定义有意义的量子场论（QFT）的要求来评估几何的容许性。

Result: 分析结果表明，无边界瞬子（no-boundary instanton）是KSW容许的，而酒杯几何（wine-glass geometry）是KSW不容许的。这一结果对于理解量子宇宙学中不同鞍点的物理意义具有重要影响。

Conclusion: 基于KSW容许性准则的分析显示，量子宇宙学中的无边界瞬子满足容许性要求，而酒杯几何则不满足该准则。这一结论对于评估量子宇宙学中不同几何结构的物理相关性提供了重要依据。

Abstract: In this note we consider no-boundary instantons and wine-glass geometries which are of interest in the context of quantum cosmology. While the former appears as a dominant saddle in the path-integral, the later sub-dominant saddle has been argued to have a longer inflationary phase of the Universe. Kontsevich-Segal-Witten (KSW)-allowability criterion which classifies geometries on the basis of the requirement of having a meaningful QFT on it, pushes one to analyse the allowability of the saddles. In this note we do a simple study to seek answer to the allowabilty of no-boundary instantons and wine-glass geometries which are of interest in quantum cosmology. Our simple analysis which make use of a milder version of KSW allowability criterion shows that no-boundary instanton is KSW allowed while wine-glass geometries are KSW disallowed.

</details>

### [33] [Quasinormal Modes and Grey-Body Factors of Scalar, Electromagnetic and Dirac Fields Around Einasto-Supported Regular Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22310)
*S. V. Bolokhov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究分析了被Einasto密度分布物质包围的黑洞中，标量场、电磁场和狄拉克场的准正规模（quasinormal modes）和灰体因子（grey-body factors）。研究发现，对于小Einasto指数（ñ=1/2和ñ=1），基模接近史瓦西黑洞值；而ñ=5时，振荡频率随晕参数增加而增大，阻尼率减小。灰体因子对晕环境不敏感，仅在低频区有轻微抑制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是分析被Einasto密度分布物质包围的黑洞的准正规模和灰体因子特性。Einasto密度分布是描述暗物质晕（dark matter halo）的常用模型，该研究旨在探索这种物质分布如何影响黑洞的扰动动力学和辐射特性。

Method: 研究方法包括：使用高阶WKB方法（high-order WKB method）结合Padé近似（Padé approximants）计算准正规谱；通过时域积分（time-domain integration）进行验证；分析标量场、电磁场和狄拉克测试场（test fields）在Einasto密度分布物质包围的黑洞中的行为。

Result: 研究结果显示：对于小Einasto指数（ñ=1/2和ñ=1），基模（fundamental modes）接近史瓦西黑洞值；对于ñ=5，振荡频率（oscillation frequency）随晕参数（halo parameter）增加而增大，阻尼率（damping rate）减小。灰体因子对晕环境不敏感，仅在低频区因视界附近有效势（effective potential）的适度增加而产生轻微抑制。

Conclusion: 结论表明：Einasto密度分布物质包围的黑洞的准正规模特性对Einasto指数敏感，而灰体因子对晕环境相对不敏感。高频区的透射概率（transmission probabilities）接近史瓦西黑洞情况，主要影响仅限于低频区的轻微抑制。

Abstract: We study quasinormal modes and grey-body factors of scalar, electromagnetic and Dirac test fields for a black hole surrounded by matter distributed according to the Einasto density profile. The quasinormal spectrum is calculated using the high-order WKB method with Padé approximants and checked by the time-domain integration. For small values of the Einasto index $\tilde n=1/2$ and $\tilde n=1$, the fundamental modes remain close to their Schwarzschild values, while for $\tilde n=5$ the oscillation frequency increases and the damping rate decreases as the halo parameter grows. Grey-body factors are much less sensitive to the halo environment: the main effect is a mild suppression at low frequencies caused by a moderate increase of the effective potential near the horizon. At higher frequencies the transmission probabilities remain close to the Schwarzschild case.

</details>


### [34] [Analytical $polyΛ$CDM dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22361)
*Pierros Ntelis,Jackson Levi Said*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种新颖的解析动力学分析方法，用于推导φCDM和polyΛCDM模型的精确能量密度比演化，与标准ΛCDM模型进行比较，并通过数值解验证。该方法为quintessence模型提供亚百分比精度的解析解，且比刚性系统的数值积分更可靠。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于开发精确的解析动力学分析方法，以比较φCDM（quintessence模型）和polyΛCDM（现象学修改引力框架）与标准ΛCDM模型的能量密度比演化。该方法旨在提供比数值积分更可靠的解析解，并深入理解修改引力模型的动力学特性。

Method: 开发了一种新颖的解析动力学分析方法，用于推导φCDM和polyΛCDM模型的能量密度比演化。该方法通过解析解与数值解进行验证，特别针对quintessence模型（φCDM）获得亚百分比精度的解析解。对于polyΛCDM模型，采用动力学分析来区分观测上可行的临界点（critical points）和不同的引力时期。

Result: 解析解显示φCDM模型与ΛCDM模型具有亚百分比（sub percent）的一致性，且比刚性系统的数值积分更可靠。polyΛCDM模型揭示了从暗能量-暗物质交换反射器（dark energy-dark matter exchange reflector）到物质、辐射、曲率和修改引力的鞍点（saddle points），再到SVT修改引力吸引子-鞍点（attractor-saddle），最终在遥远未来达到宇宙常数吸引子（cosmological constant attractor）的全局转变过程。

Conclusion: 所有三种模型（ΛCDM、φCDM、polyΛCDM）都与观测到的宇宙演化一致，但polyΛCDM模型因其更丰富的现象学（richer phenomenology）而提供了对修改引力动力学的更深入见解。该模型整合了多种修改引力模型，为现有研究提供了简化而全面的替代方案。

Abstract: We develop a novel analytical dynamical analysis to derive precise energy density ratio evolutions for the $φ$CDM and $polyΛ$CDM models, comparing them to the standard $Λ$CDM model and validating against numerical solutions. Analytical solutions for the quintessence, i.e. $φ$CDM, show sub percent agreement with $Λ$CDM with greater reliability than numerical integration of stiff systems. The $polyΛ$CDM model, a phenomenological modified gravity framework, captures radiation, matter, dark energy, and exotic epochs, offering a streamlined yet comprehensive alternative to existing studies. Its dynamics reveal a global transition from a dark energy-dark matter exchange reflector, through saddle points of matter, radiation, curvature, and modified gravity, to an SVT modified gravity attractor-saddle, and finally to a cosmological constant attractor in the far future, with saddle transitions between modified gravity components. The $polyΛ$CDM model integrates modified gravity models, using dynamical analysis to distinguish observationally viable critical points and differentiate gravity epochs. All three models align with observed cosmic evolution, but $polyΛ$CDM richer phenomenology provides deeper insights into modified gravity dynamics. Code available at GitHub.

</details>


### [35] [Stable black hole solutions with cosmological hair](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22398)
*Laurens Smulders,Johannes Noller*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了在动态暗能量（dynamical dark energy）理论框架下，黑洞嵌入膨胀宇宙时空时产生的宇宙学毛发（cosmological hair）问题。通过以立方伽利略子（cubic Galileon）为例，作者推导了既满足正则性又保持稳定的黑洞解，这些解能够同时恢复所需的宇宙学长程行为并在黑洞附近产生良好的短程动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动态暗能量理论引入随时间变化的场，导致宇宙在大尺度上的加速膨胀。当将黑洞解嵌入这种宇宙学时空时，时间依赖性自然会产生宇宙学毛发，即局部黑洞物理不再仅由黑洞质量和自旋控制，还受到暗能量场的影响。然而，已知的此类解通常不稳定。

Method: 聚焦于立方伽利略子作为具体且具说明性的例子，详细讨论了物理解的正则性和稳定性所施加的限制。明确推导了既正则又稳定的解，这些解既能恢复所需的宇宙学长程行为，又能在黑洞周围产生良好的短程动力学。

Result: 成功推导出正则且稳定的黑洞解，这些解同时满足宇宙学尺度行为和黑洞附近动力学的要求。研究表明，这些局部黑洞解周围的标量毛发（scalar hair）性质编码了宇宙学信息。

Conclusion: 黑洞周围的标量毛发性质能够编码宇宙学信息，这为通过黑洞观测直接探测宇宙动力学提供了新颖且诱人的前景。该研究为在动态暗能量框架下理解黑洞与宇宙膨胀的相互作用提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Dynamical dark energy theories generically introduce a time-dependent field that causes the accelerated expansion of the Universe on large scales. When embedding black hole solutions in such a cosmological space-time, this time dependence naturally gives rise to cosmological hair, i.e. the local black hole physics is no longer controlled by just the mass and spin of the black hole, but also impacted by the dark energy field. However, known such solutions are unstable. Focusing on the cubic Galileon as a concrete and illustrative example, we discuss the restrictions imposed on physical solutions by their regularity and stability in detail. We explicitly derive regular and stable solutions, that both recover the desired cosmological long-range behaviour and give rise to well-behaved short-range dynamics around black holes. We show how the nature of the scalar hair around these local black hole solutions encodes cosmological information, highlighting novel and tantalising prospects of directly probing cosmological dynamics with black hole observations.

</details>

Main category: gr-qc

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机在于改进等效单体（EOB）形式中的潮汐效应描述，特别是针对后闵可夫斯基（PM）引力散射的最新进展，以提升理论预测与中子星散射数值相对论（numerical-relativity）数据的一致性。

Method: 方法上，研究利用最先进的后闵可夫斯基（PM）引力散射结果，探索了绝热（adiabatic）和后绝热（post-adiabatic）的引力电（gravitoelectric）与引力磁（gravitomagnetic）四极潮汐效应，并构建了拉格朗日-PM-潮汐版本的EOB模型。

Result: 结果显示，与现有EOB模型和PM展开相比，新构建的拉格朗日-PM-潮汐EOB版本与最近的中子星散射数值相对论数据具有更好的吻合度，为发展精确的PM EOB潮汐部分奠定了基础。

Conclusion: 结论指出，这项工作为开发精确的PM EOB模型的潮汐部分奠定了基础，并强调了需要探索改进的PN EOB重求和方案，以处理束缚轨道和圆化轨道问题。

Abstract: Using state-of-the-art scattering results in post-Minkowskian (PM) gravity, we improve the tidal sector of four different flavors of the effective-one-body (EOB) formalism. We notably explore both adiabatic and post-adiabatic gravitoelectric and gravitomagnetic quadrupolar tidal effects at the next-to-next-to-leading PM-order. When comparing the predictions of the so-constructed Lagrange-PM-tidal version of EOB to recent numerical-relativity data on the scattering of neutron stars, we find improved agreement with respect to existing EOB models and PM expansions. Our work lays the foundation for the development of an accurate tidal sector of the PM EOB models, and points out the need to explore improved resummation schemes in PN EOB for bound and circularized orbits.

</details>


### [37] [Choosing the phase for the spin-weighted spheroidal functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22485)
*Gregory B. Cook,Xiyue Wang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文针对自旋权重球体函数（spin-weighted spheroidal functions）的相位模糊性问题，明确界定并深入探讨了两种实用的相位固定方案，建议将球面极限相位固定方案作为默认选择。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自旋权重球体函数作为角向Teukolsky方程的本征函数，在黑洞微扰理论中极为重要。然而，与其他特殊函数类似，它们存在固有的相位模糊性，需要相位固定才能唯一定义。目前，针对这些函数的相位选择方案研究甚少。

Method: 论文明确界定并深入探讨了两种有用的相位固定方案（phase fixing schemes）。作者特别提出将球面极限相位固定方案（spherical-limit phase-fixing scheme）作为自旋权重球体函数的默认相位选择。

Result: 研究系统地分析了两种相位固定方案的特性，并论证了球面极限相位固定方案作为默认选择的合理性。该方案有助于从模式信息中有效提取系统的物理信息。

Conclusion: 论文建议将球面极限相位固定方案采纳为自旋权重球体函数的默认相位固定方案，以解决其相位模糊性问题，确保物理信息的准确提取。

Abstract: The spin-weighted spheroidal functions are the eigenfunctions of the angular Teukolsky equation. They are a generalization of the widely used spin-weighted spherical functions, and are extremely important in the area of black-hole perturbation theory. Like other special functions, they have an inherent phase ambiguity and need to be phase fixed to be uniquely defined. Clearly, such a phase choice does not have a direct physical impact. But, a poorly constructed phase choice could hinder the extraction, from mode information, of physical information about a system. To date, possible phase choices for the spin-weighted spheroidal functions have received little attention. Here, we clearly define and extensively explore two useful phase fixing schemes, and we propose that the spherical-limit phase-fixing scheme be adopted as the default phase-fixing scheme for the spin-weighted spheroidal functions.

</details>


### [38] [Quantum Tunneling of Primordial Black Holes to White Holes: Rates, Constraints, and Implications for Fast Radio Bursts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22516)
*Christopher Ewasiuk,Stefano Profumo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文计算了原初黑洞（PBH）量子隧穿为白洞（white hole）的宇宙学体积率，发现仅在参数空间高度受限的狭窄区域内可能产生快速射电暴（FRB）级别的爆发率，且观测数据不支持白洞作为FRB的主要起源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在研究原初黑洞（primordial black hole, PBH）通过量子隧穿转变为白洞（white hole）的宇宙学爆发率，并评估这一过程作为快速射电暴（fast radio burst, FRB）起源的可能性。研究动机源于探索PBH量子隧穿现象的天体物理可观测性及其与FRB观测特征的潜在关联。

Method: 方法综合考虑了霍金蒸发（Hawking evaporation）与隧穿过程的竞争、宇宙学稀释效应、依赖于质量的现实丰度约束、扩展质量函数，以及替代性的记忆负担（memory-burden）情景。研究在质量-隧穿参数平面上计算爆发率，并评估了来自FRB重复统计、射电频谱特性、伽马射线限制、宿主星系特征和引力波信号等多方面的观测约束。

Result: 结果表明，爆发率在质量-隧穿参数平面上沿一条狭窄的脊线达到最大，该处有效PBH寿命与宇宙年龄相当。在典型的普朗克星（Planck-star）隧穿时间尺度范围内，FRB级别的爆发率仅出现在两个高度受限的区域：蒸发边界附近的低质量窗口，以及蒸发先于隧穿的狭窄序列窗口。扩展PBH质量函数不会定性改变这一结论。

Conclusion: 所有当前观测数据均与白洞对FRB种群存在次要贡献的可能性一致，但强烈反对其作为主要起源。爆发率计算通常不支持FRB级别的事件密度，任何可行的FRB解释都需要参数空间中狭窄、精细调节且强烈依赖于假设的角落。

Abstract: We calculate the present-day and cosmological volumetric rate of primordial black hole (PBH) quantum tunneling events to white holes, incorporating the competition between Hawking evaporation and tunneling, cosmological depletion, realistic mass-dependent abundance constraints, extended mass functions, and the alternative memory-burden scenario. The burst rate is maximized along a narrow ridge in the mass--tunneling-parameter plane where the effective PBH lifetime is comparable to the age of the Universe. Within the canonical Planck-star range of tunneling timescales, FRB-level rates arise only in two highly restricted regions: a low-mass window near the evaporation boundary, and a narrow sequential window where evaporation precedes tunneling; broadening the PBH mass function does not qualitatively alter this conclusion. We further assess observational constraints from FRB repetition statistics, radio spectral properties, prompt and diffuse gamma-ray limits, host-galaxy demographics, and gravitational-wave signatures. All current observations are consistent with a subdominant white-hole contribution to the FRB population but strongly disfavor a dominant origin. The rate calculation does not generically support FRB-level event densities, and any viable FRB interpretation requires narrow, fine-tuned, and strongly assumption-dependent corners of parameter space.

</details>


### [39] [Reconstructed black hole solutions in the scalar-tensor theory with nonminimal coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22517)
*K. K. Ernazarov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究在Jordan框架下探索了具有非最小耦合的标量-张量理论的重构方法，针对静态球对称度规（采用Buchdahl参数化）建立了精确解，并通过Reissner-Nordström-(Anti-)de Sitter和Bocharova-Bronnikov-Melnikov-Bekenstein-(Anti)de-Sitter度规两个示例验证了该形式体系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于发展一种系统性的重构方法，用于在Jordan框架下的标量-张量理论中，针对给定的静态球对称度规构造精确解。该方法旨在建立度规与理论参数（势函数和耦合函数）之间的明确关系。

Method: 采用Buchdahl参数化描述静态球对称度规：$ds^2 = \left(A(u)\right)^{-1}du^2 - A(u)dt^2 + C(u)dΩ^2$。通过求解耦合函数$f(\varphi(u))$的一阶线性微分方程，建立了势函数$U(\varphi(u))$、耦合函数$f(\varphi(u))$和标量场导数$d\varphi/du$之间的关系，从而获得运动方程的精确解。

Result: 研究成功发展了一套重构形式体系，能够从给定的度规函数$A(u)$和$C(u)$出发，推导出标量-张量理论中相应的势函数和耦合函数。该方法的有效性通过两个具体示例得到验证：Reissner-Nordström-(Anti-)de Sitter度规和Bocharova-Bronnikov-Melnikov-Bekenstein-(Anti)de-Sitter度规。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种系统性的重构方法，能够在Jordan框架的标量-张量理论中为给定的静态球对称度规构造精确解。该方法的核心在于求解耦合函数的一阶线性微分方程，并通过具体示例展示了其应用潜力。

Abstract: We consider the scalar-tensor theory witn non-minimal coupling in the Jordan frame. The action of the model contains a potential term $U(\varphi)$, a coupling function $f(\varphi)$. We explore a reconstruction procedure for a generic static spherically symmetric metric written in the Buchdahl parametrization: $ds^2 = \left(A(u)\right)^{-1}du^2 - A(u)dt^2 + C(u)dΩ^2$, with given $A(u) > 0$ and $C(u) > 0$. The procedure gives the relations for $U(\varphi(u))$, $f(\varphi(u))$ and $d\varphi/du$, which lead to exact solutions to equations of motion with a given metric. A key role in this approach is played by the solutions to a first order linear differential equation for the function $f(\varphi(u))$. The formalism is illustrated by two examples when: a) the Reissner-Nordström-(Anti-)de Sitter metric and b) the Bocharova-Bronnikov-Melnikov-Bekenstein-(Anti)de-Sitter metric are chosen as a starting point.

</details>


### [40] [Spontaneous scalarization of neutron stars in teleparallel gravity with derivative torsional coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22522)
*Youcef Kehal,Khireddine Nouicer*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究在包含标量场与物质和挠率耦合的teleparallel引力模型中构建中子星解，发现标量化（scalarization）仅出现在有限中心密度范围内，且在高密度下被抑制，旋转测量可用于检验此类理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索teleparallel引力框架下，标量场与物质和挠率耦合对中子星结构的影响，特别是标量化现象及其对中子星质量-半径关系、旋转特性的可观测效应。

Method: 采用包含标量场与物质和挠率耦合的teleparallel引力模型，在爱因斯坦框架（Einstein frame）中构建静态和缓慢旋转中子星解，重点关注APR和MS1两种状态方程（equations of state）。

Result: 标量化解仅出现在有限中心密度范围内，表现为对广义相对论质量-半径和质量-中心密度关系的局部偏离；标量化的起始和范围取决于状态方程和挠率相互作用的强度，高中心密度下标量化被抑制；无物质耦合时未发现标量化解。

Conclusion: 中子星半径和旋转测量具有检验teleparallel标量化场景的潜力；标量化在中等致密区域出现但在高致密性下被抑制，标量电荷趋势与全局质量关系一致，转动惯量系统地依赖于挠率耦合和状态方程。

Abstract: We study neutron star configurations in a teleparallel gravity model featuring a scalar field coupled to both matter and torsion. In the Einstein frame, the theory includes a derivative coupling between the scalar field and the torsion vector, together with a conformal matter coupling \(A(φ)=\exp(βφ^{2}/2)\). Static and slowly rotating neutron-star solutions are constructed for realistic equations of state, focusing on the APR and MS1 equations of state. Scalarized solutions appear only within a finite range of central densities and correspond to localized deviations from the general-relativistic mass--radius and mass--central-density relations. The onset and extent of scalarization depend on the equation of state and on the strength of the derivative torsional interaction, which can either enhance or suppress scalarization relative to the general-relativistic scalarized branch. At high central densities, scalarization is quenched and the solutions approach the general-relativistic limit, remaining bounded even for strong torsional couplings. No scalarized solutions are found in the absence of matter coupling (\(β=0\)). The normalized scalar charge follows trends consistent with the global mass relations, indicating an intermediate scalarized regime suppressed at high compactness. For slowly rotating stars, the moment of inertia depends systematically on the torsional coupling and the equation of state, with stiffer equations yielding larger values. These results highlight the potential of neutron-star radius and rotational measurements to test teleparallel scalarization scenarios.

Result: 建立了因果结构的数学框架，并研究了因果顶点振幅的渐近行为。重新审视了EPRL和EPRL-KKL自旋泡沫模型半经典分析中出现的两个临界点的物理解释。该因果振幅为解决余弦问题（cosine problem）和不规则光锥结构的存在提供了新的研究视角。

Conclusion: 本文提出的因果振幅为自旋泡沫模型的未来发展提供了新的见解，特别是在处理余弦问题和不规则光锥结构方面。该框架为量子引力的因果结构研究奠定了数学基础。

Abstract: We investigate the role of causality in the generalized EPRL spinfoam model introduced by Kaminski, Kisielowski, and Lewandowski (EPRL-KKL). We first propose a definition of causal structure on an arbitrary 2-complex and analyze how causal orientations can be assigned to its 1-skeleton and 2-skeleton. We identify a criterion that determines when an orientation of the 2-skeleton induces a consistent causal structure on the 1-skeleton. This characterization naturally involves tools from graph theory and linear algebra over the Galois field $\mathbb{F}_2$. Using these results, we introduce a causal vertex amplitude that generalizes previous proposals by Bianchi--Dussaud and Bianchi--Chen--Gamonal. We study its asymptotic behavior and revisit the interpretation of the two critical points appearing in the semiclassical analysis of the EPRL and EPRL-KKL spinfoam models. Finally, we discuss several directions in which the causal amplitude introduced here may provide new insights for future developments, like the cosine problem and the presence of irregular light cone structures.

Abstract: Using matching properties of the gravitational field at timelike and spatial infinity, together with universal formulas for gravitational wave tails, we obtain exact expressions for the peeling-violating components of the Weyl tensor at future and past null infinity. The computation is facilitated by the observation that the tail and peeling-violating coefficients organize into a "celestial diamond" introduced in the context of celestial holography. The analysis suggests a new matching condition at spatial infinity which, together with previously found matching at timelike infinity, capture both tail and peeling-violation formulas. We conclude by pointing out that stronger peeling violations occur in perturbative quantum gravity, in agreement with a recently reported amplitude-based result.

Conclusion: 结论表明，在单模引力中，扩散机制能够驱动大撕裂奇点的产生，同时保持非幻影状态方程和正熵产生。这些结果揭示了一种新型的未来奇点产生机制，在标准广义相对论中没有直接对应物，为理解宇宙演化中的奇点结构提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: This work investigates future cosmological singularities in a flat FLRW universe filled with a single barotropic fluid, ($p = (γ- 1)ρ$), within the framework of unimodular gravity. In this setting, the non-conservation of the energy-momentum tensor is encoded through an energy diffusion function $Q$. While a constant diffusion term leads to an effective cosmological constant and preserves adiabatic evolution, a time-dependent $Q(t)$ induces non-adiabatic dynamics. We consider a power-law Ansatz for $Q$ as a function of the redshift and impose the condition of positive entropy production. This requirement leads to non-trivial constraints on the model parameters, with direct implications for the admissible singularity structure. In particular, within the thermodynamically allowed sector, we show that Big Rip singularities are excluded for non-phantom fluids when the cosmological constant is positive. For phantom fluids, the model reproduces the expected Big Rip behavior, as well as Big Crunch solutions for negative cosmological constant. More importantly, we show that diffusion can induce an effective phantom regime even when the fundamental fluid is non-phantom. In particular, for a negative cosmological constant, we present an explicit realization of a Big Rip singularity in unimodular gravity driven by diffusion, while consistently preserving a non-phantom equation of state and positive entropy production. These results reveal a novel mechanism for the emergence of future singularities, with no direct analogue in standard General Relativity.

The gravastar core is modeled as a Bose--Einstein condensate, while the intermediate shell consists of ultra-dense stiff matter. This highlights the SS braneworld gravastar as a physically viable compact object and a compelling alternative to black holes. A key novelty of our construction is that the stabilizing pressure anisotropy and suppressed effective gravitational mass arise dynamically from higher-dimensional Weyl corrections, rather than being imposed through ad hoc matter sources or thin-shell idealizations. This provides the first fully analytic realization of a finite-thickness, stable gravastar in the Shtanov-Sahni braneworld, highlighting a genuinely geometric mechanism for singularity avoidance in compact objects.

### [48] [Inflation driven by a bare cosmological constant and its graceful exit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23263)

Abstract: Vacuum energy, a prediction of quantum field theory, manifests itself as a cosmological constant in general relativity. In this Letter, we propose a novel inflationary scenario driven by a bare cosmological constant $Λ$, which terminates naturally through a self-tuning mechanism. Within Fab-Four gravity, self-tuning destabilizes the de Sitter state and drives the system toward a stiff-fluid attractor, thereby yielding a graceful exit. We construct two explicit models in which the slow-roll parameter evolves exponentially or as a power law. We show that the latter model, derived from center-manifold dynamics, significantly relaxes the required tuning of initial conditions. Our results establish, for the first time, that bare-vacuum-energy inflation with natural termination constitutes a viable dynamical possibility.

</details>


### [49] [Solutions of the constraints with controlled decay to Kerr, including Schwartz decay](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23484)
*Andrea Nützi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文证明，对于闵可夫斯基时空线性化约束方程的每个小衰减解，可通过添加二次小修正获得完整约束方程的解。修正项在类空间无穷远处由克尔黑洞初始数据给出，且具有优于线性化解的衰减特性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 结果表明，修正项在类空间无穷远处由克尔黑洞初始数据给出，其衰减速度快于线性化解；若线性化解具有施瓦茨衰减，则修正项也具有施瓦茨衰减。利用近期结果，证明具有这些初始数据的爱因斯坦方程解在零无穷远和类时无穷远处允许正则共形紧化。

Conclusion: 该研究成功建立了从线性化约束方程解到完整约束方程解的构造框架，证明了修正项在无穷远处的特定行为，并获得了具有良好紧化性质的解。代数层面的创新在于使用同伦传递定理替代传统几何方法推导约束方程。

Abstract: We show that to every small and decaying solution of the linearized constraint equations about Minkowski spacetime, one can add a quadratically small correction to obtain a solution of the full constraint equations. Near spacelike infinity, the correction is given by Kerr black hole initial data, up to a term that decays faster than the linearized solution, and that has Schwartz decay if the linearized solution has Schwartz decay. Using a recent result, we obtain that the solutions of the Einstein equations with these initial data admit a regular conformal compactification along null and timelike infinity. The construction is based on a right inverse (up to necessary integrability conditions) for the linearized constraint operator about Minkowski initial data obtained previously, that has optimal mapping properties relative to weighted b-Sobolev spaces, where the weights measure decay towards infinity. On an algebraic level, we show that the constraint equations can be derived using the homotopy transfer theorem, rather than using the geometric Gauss and Codazzi equations.

### [50] [How active field theories couple to external potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22424)
*Yariv Kafri,Julien Tailleur*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究通过系统微扰展开方法，确定了活性场论中耦合外部势能所需的最简项，揭示了密度与势能梯度间的非平凡耦合关系，并展示了该方法在粒子相互作用和推进速度空间调制中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在确定活性场论（active field theories）中耦合外部势能（external potentials）所需的最简项，以理解活性粒子在外部势场中的非平衡特性。

Method: 采用活性布朗粒子（active Brownian particles）模型，并在粒子持续时间（particle persistence time）上进行系统微扰展开（systematic perturbative expansion）。

Result: 研究发现了密度与势能梯度间的非平凡耦合（non-trivial coupling），该耦合能够解释活性粒子在外部势场中的非平衡特征，包括边界积累（boundary accumulation）和远场密度调制（far-field density modulation）。

Conclusion: 该方法可扩展应用于通过成对力（pairwise forces）相互作用的粒子体系，以及推进速度（propulsion speed）的空间调制情形，为活性场论与外部势场的耦合提供了系统框架。

Abstract: We study the simplest terms that need to be included in active field theories to couple them to external potentials. To do so, we consider active Brownian particles and implement a systematic perturbative expansion in the particle persistence time. The result is a non-trivial coupling between density and potential gradients, which accounts for the nonequilibrium features of active particles in the presence of an external potential, from boundary accumulation to far-field density modulation. We show how the method can be applied to particles interacting via pairwise forces and to spatial modulations of the propulsion speed.

### [51] [The damage spreading transition: a hierarchy of renormalization group fixed points](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22439)
*Adam Nahum,Sthitadhi Roy*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 确定性经典元胞自动机存在两种相：强不可逆相中不同初始条件的轨迹快速合并，弱不可逆相中轨迹差异可维持指数长时间。损伤传播相变（damage-spreading transition）的理论比定向渗流（directed percolation）更丰富，包含局部可观测量（local observables）的无限层次结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 确定性经典元胞自动机（deterministic classical cellular automata）的动力学规则不可逆性决定其处于两种不同相：强不可逆相中轨迹快速合并，弱不可逆相中轨迹差异可维持指数长时间。损伤传播相变（damage-spreading transition）作为这两种相之间的转变，其完整理论尚未完全建立。

Method: 通过场论表述（field theory formulation）和重整化群（renormalization group）论证分析损伤传播临界点的完整理论。使用1+1维模拟验证理论预测，揭示该相变比定向渗流（directed percolation）更丰富的层次结构。

Result: 损伤传播临界点的完整理论包含局部可观测量（local observables）的无限层次结构，定向渗流仅描述该层次的第一级。高阶可观测量包括多个轨迹的"重叠"（overlaps），可用集合划分（set partitions）标记。该完整层次结构产生反应-扩散型过程（reaction-diffusion-type processes）的非平衡固定点（nonequilibrium fixed points）层次。

Conclusion: 确定性元胞自动机的损伤传播相变理论比定向渗流更丰富，包含无限层次的局部可观测量结构。这些高阶固定点（higher fixed points）包含定向渗流作为子部门，但具有额外的普适临界指数（universal critical exponents），为理解非平衡相变提供了更完整的理论框架。

Abstract: Deterministic classical cellular automata can be in two phases, depending on how irreversible the dynamical rules are. In the strongly irreversible phase, trajectories with different initial conditions coalesce quickly, while in the weakly irreversible phase, trajectories with different initial conditions can remain different for a time exponential in the system volume. The transition between these phases is referred to as the damage-spreading transition (the "damaged" sites are those that differ between the trajectories). We develop a theory for this transition. In the simplest and most generic setting, the transition is known to be related to directed percolation, one of the best-studied nonequilibrium phase transitions. However, we show that full theory of the damage-spreading critical point is richer than directed percolation, and contains an infinite hierarchy of sectors of local observables. Directed percolation describes the first level of the hierarchy. The higher observables include "overlaps" for multiple trajectories, and may be labeled by set partitions. (These higher observables arise naturally if, for example, we consider decay of entropy under the irreversible dynamics.) The full hierarchy yields a hierarchy of nonequilibrium fixed points for reaction-diffusion-type processes, all of which contain directed percolation as a subsector, but which possess additional universal critical exponents. We analyze these higher fixed points using a field theory formulation and renormalization group arguments, and using simulations in 1+1 dimensions.

</details>

*Eric R. Bittner*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典热力学中存在与循环过程相关的几何关系，特别是机械功与$(P,V)$平面上轨迹包围面积的对应关系。研究旨在探索这些几何关系的统一数学基础及其与热力学响应的联系。

Method: 通过引入定义在平衡热力学流形上的单一正则二形式（canonical two-form），将功和可逆热的面积定律统一为该二形式在不同表示（$(P,V)$和$(T,S)$）下的投影，从而提供热力学循环的统一描述。

Result: 研究发现无限小循环产生的功由平衡能量表面的混合曲率$U_{SV}$局部确定，该曲率可用可测量响应函数表达。这确立了热力学功作为状态空间上的局部几何场，而不仅仅是循环过程的全局性质。

Conclusion: 该框架将经典循环几何与随机热力学轨迹联系起来，为非平衡功关系（如Jarzynski等式）提供了几何解释，建立了热力学几何描述的统一基础。

Abstract: Classical thermodynamics contains familiar geometric relations associated with cyclic processes, most notably the identification of mechanical work with the area enclosed by a trajectory in the $(P,V)$ plane. We show that the area laws for work and reversible heat arise as projections of a single canonical two--form defined on the equilibrium thermodynamic manifold, providing a unified description of thermodynamic cycles in both the $(P,V)$ and $(T,S)$ representations. The same structure yields a direct link between cycle geometry and thermodynamic response: the work generated by infinitesimal cycles is set locally by the mixed curvature $U_{SV}$ of the equilibrium energy surface, which can be expressed in terms of measurable susceptibilities. This identifies thermodynamic work as a local geometric field over state space rather than solely a global property of cyclic processes. More broadly, the framework connects classical cycle geometry to stochastic thermodynamic trajectories, providing a geometric interpretation of nonequilibrium work relations such as the Jarzynski equality.

*Matias P. Gonzalez,Micolta-Riascos Bayron*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于将分数阶微积分（fractional calculus）概念引入非广延统计力学（non-extensive statistical mechanics）框架，通过q-Caputo算子对Tsallis熵进行分数阶推广，探索参数空间中的熵行为。

Method: 方法采用q-Caputo微分积分算子（q-Caputo differintegral）作用于生成函数族∑_i p_i^x在x=1处的值，定义分数阶Tsallis熵S_q^α，并利用q-Gamma函数推导出封闭级数表示。

Result: 主要结果包括：1）建立了分数阶Tsallis熵的数学表达式；2）证明了当α→1时收敛到标准Tsallis熵S_q；3）通过数值计算确定了分数参数α和非广延指数q空间中熵的非负性（或负值）区域。

Conclusion: 结论表明，通过q-Caputo算子成功构造了Tsallis熵的分数阶推广，该构造在极限情况下具有良好行为，并通过数值分析揭示了参数空间中熵的正负特性。

Abstract: We introduce a fractional generalization of Tsallis entropy by acting with a $q$-Caputo operator on the generating family $\sum_i p_i^{\,x}$ evaluated at $x=1$. Concretely, we define $S_{q}^α$ through the $q$-Caputo differintegral of order $0<α<1$ and derive a closed series representation in terms of the $q$-Gamma function. The construction is anchored at the evaluation point, which ensures well-behaved limits: as $α\!\to\!1$ we recover the standard Tsallis entropy $S_q$. Finally we perform a numerical calculation to show the regions where the obtained $q$-fractional entropy $S^α_q$ can be non-negative (or negative) through the fractional parameter $α$ and the non extensive index $q$.
