### [54] [Pseudospectral phenomena and the origin of the non-Hermitian skin effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22643)
*J. Sirker*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究重新审视了非厄米趋肤效应（NHSE）与点隙拓扑之间的关联，指出NHSE源于谱不稳定性与非互易性而非拓扑，并证明点隙绕数与边界局域化之间的常见假设关系依赖于平移对称性而非普适性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点常将非厄米趋肤效应（non-Hermitian skin effect, NHSE）归因于布洛赫哈密顿量的非平凡点隙拓扑（point-gap topology）。本研究旨在重新审视这一关联，探讨NHSE的真正物理起源。

Method: 通过分析非正规算子（non-normal operators）的本征谱对边界条件和微扰的敏感性，提出拓扑性质应体现在有限系统的奇异值谱中。以Hatano-Nelson梯子模型为例，独立调节点隙绕数（point-gap winding）与非正规性，验证理论框架。

Result: 研究证明：1）NHSE可以在没有点隙绕数的情况下发生；2）点隙绕数可以在没有NHSE的情况下持续存在；3）本征谱不构成编码拓扑信息的稳定对象，而奇异值谱在有限系统中反映拓扑性质。

Conclusion: 非厄米趋肤效应（NHSE）源于谱不稳定性（spectral instability）和非互易性（non-reciprocity）而非拓扑性质。点隙绕数与边界局域化之间的常见关联依赖于平移对称性（translational invariance），因此不具有普适性。

Abstract: The non-Hermitian skin effect (NHSE), characterized by a macroscopic accumulation of eigenstates at the edge of a system with open boundaries, is often ascribed to a non-trivial point-gap topology of the Bloch Hamiltonian. We revisit this connection and show that the eigenspectrum of non-normal operators is highly sensitive to boundary conditions and generic perturbations, and therefore does not constitute a stable object encoding topological information. Instead, topological properties are reflected in the singular-value spectrum of finite systems and, in the semi-infinite limit, correspond to boundary-localized eigenmodes implied by the index of the corresponding Toeplitz operator. For a Hatano-Nelson ladder, where point-gap winding and non-normality can be varied independently, we demonstrate that the NHSE can occur without point-gap winding and, conversely, that point-gap winding can persist without the NHSE. These results establish that the NHSE originates from spectral instability and non-reciprocity rather than topology, and that the commonly assumed relation between spectral winding and boundary localization relies on translational invariance and is therefore not generic.

</details>


### [55] [Genuine and spurious (non-)ergodicity in single particle tracking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22989)
*Wei Wang,Qing Wei,Igor M. Sokolov,Ralf Metzler,Aleksei Chechkin*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文指出传统基于均方位移（MSD）与时间平均均方位移（TAMSD）比较的遍历性判断标准存在理论缺陷，并提出使用均方增量（MSI）替代MSD进行系综平均与时间平均观测量的比较，以更准确地表征系统的真实（非）遍历性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在单粒子追踪（single-particle tracking, SPT）实验中，理解遍历性（ergodicity）至关重要，因为它确保观测量的时间平均与系综平均相匹配。然而，广泛使用的基于MSD-TAMSD比较的遍历性判断标准缺乏充分的理论论证，且在某些情况下会得出错误的（非）遍历性结果。

Method: 作者提出使用均方增量（mean-squared increment, MSI）而非均方位移（mean-squared displacement, MSD）来比较系综平均与时间平均观测量。通过分析多个已知随机模型（stochastic models），验证MSI-TAMSD准则的有效性。

Result: MSI-TAMSD准则不仅能有效揭示弱遍历性破缺（weak ergodicity breaking），与MSD-TAMSD方法等效，而且能更准确地表征MSD-TAMSD方法失效系统的真实（非）遍历性。对于展现"超弱"遍历性破缺（"ultraweak" ergodicity breaking）的系统，MSI还能揭示过程增量的渐近平稳性和遍历性本质。

Conclusion: 该研究强调了MSI观测量在SPT实验和反常扩散（anomalous diffusion）研究中的重要作用，为遍历性判断提供了更可靠的理论框架，纠正了传统MSD-TAMSD方法可能导致的虚假结果。

Abstract: In single-particle tracking experiments measuring anomalous diffusion dynamics, understanding ergodicity is crucial, as it ensures that the time average of an observable matches the ensemble average, and can thus be fitted with known ensemble-averaged observables. A commonly used criterion for assessing the ergodicity of a stochastic process is based on the comparison of the mean-squared displacement (MSD) with the time-averaged MSD (TAMSD). This approach has been widely applied and proves effective in cases of weak ergodicity breaking across various systems in both theoretical and experimental studies. However, there is relatively little discussion regarding the theoretical justification and limitations of this definition. Here, we demonstrate that this widely accepted criterion to some extent contradicts the classical definition of ergodicity as well as physical intuition, leading to spurious (non-)ergodicity results when applied to several well-known stochastic models. To address this limitation, we propose using the mean-squared increment (MSI) instead of the MSD for comparison of ensemble- and time-averaged observables. Several well-established examples demonstrate that our MSI-TAMSD criterion not only effectively reveals weak ergodicity breaking, equivalent to the MSD-TAMSD approach, but also provides a more accurate characterization of the genuine (non-)ergodicity of systems where the MSD-TAMSD method fails. Additionally, for systems exhibiting "ultraweak" ergodicity breaking, the MSI can reveal the asymptotic stationarity and ergodic nature of the process' increments. Our findings emphasize the important role of the MSI observable for SPT experiments and anomalous diffusion studies.

</details>

Method: 利用福克-普朗克方程与薛定谔方程的经典联系，采用精确对角化方法分析全谱特性，并将该方法扩展到非互易相互作用情形，此时问题转化为类似于开放量子力学的非厄米薛定谔问题。

Abstract: There has been recent interest in the relaxational modes of small-scale fully connected systems of aligning self-propelled particles (Spera et al., Phys. Rev. Lett. {\bf 132}: 078301 (2024)). We revisit the classical connection between Fokker-Planck and Schrödinger equations to address this by means of exact diagonalization, allowing for rigorous analytical insight into the full spectrum. This allows us to extract exact results which we compare to the existing result from linearized statistical field theory. We derive asymptotically correct analytical results that improve upon the prior approximations. We show that this methodology can fruitfully be extended to the case of non-reciprocal interactions which gives rise to a non-Hermitian Schrödinger problem akin to those in open quantum mechanics. While the non-reciprocity can be chosen such as not to alter the stationary distribution, it fundamentally changes the nature of the steady state which we quantify via the entropy production. We discuss the case of low particle numbers as well as the emergence of mean-field dynamics at large numbers.

### [57] [Basis dependence of eigenstate thermalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23058)
*Lennart Dabelow,Christian Eidecker-Dunkel,Peter Reimann*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本研究表明，在具有简并性的多体系统中，本征态热化（eigenstate thermalization）的表现会因本征基的选择而异：在某些基中满足弱本征态热化假设，而在其他基中则违反该假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本征态热化假设认为，多体系统的能量本征态在局部可观测量期望值方面与相同能量的热平衡系综无法区分。然而，在存在简并性的系统中，能量本征基的选择不唯一，不同基中表现出本征态热化的态比例可能不同。

Method: 研究提供了一个简单示例，展示在热力学极限下，一个基选择中表现出本征态热化的态比例消失，而在另一个基选择中该比例保持非零。同时证明了当系统同时具有空间平移和反射对称性时，简并性必然大量存在。

Result: 研究发现，弱本征态热化假设（weak eigenstate thermalization hypothesis）在第一个基选择中得到满足，但在第二个基选择中被违反。研究还推导了本征态热化对基选择依赖程度的一般界限。

Conclusion: 本征态热化对能量本征基的选择具有依赖性，这种依赖性受到一般界限的约束。研究揭示了这种依赖性对系统时间弛豫特性的有趣影响，特别是在同时具有空间平移和反射对称性的系统中，简并性必然普遍存在。

Abstract: Eigenstate thermalization refers to the property that an energy eigenstate of a many-body system is indistinguishable from a thermal equilibrium ensemble at the same energy as far as expectation values of local observables are concerned. In systems with degeneracies, the choice of an energy eigenbasis is not unique and the fraction of basis states exhibiting eigenstate thermalization can vary. We present a simple example where this fraction vanishes in the thermodynamic limit for one basis choice, but remains nonzero for another choice. In other words, the weak eigenstate thermalization hypothesis is satisfied in the first, but violated in the second basis. We furthermore prove that degeneracies must abound whenever a system is simultaneously symmetric under spatial translations and reflection. Finally, we derive general bounds on how strongly eigenstate thermalization may depend on the choice of the basis, and we reveal some interesting implications regarding the temporal relaxation properties of such systems.

</details>


### [58] [Amplification based on the noise-induced negative differential resistance in a Zener diode](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23169)

TL;DR: 该论文展示了通过噪声反馈（noise feedback）在12V齐纳二极管（Zener diode）的反向偏置区诱导出负微分电阻（negative differential resistance），并利用此特性构建音频频率范围的电压放大器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统电压偏置的齐纳二极管始终呈现正微分电阻（positive differential resistance），无法作为信号放大元件使用。研究旨在探索在齐纳二极管中实现放大功能的新方法。

Method: 采用噪声反馈技术，在12V齐纳二极管的反向偏置区诱导负微分电阻现象。基于此构建音频频率范围的电压放大器，并进行系统表征。

Result: 成功在齐纳二极管中实现了负微分电阻，构建了音频放大器。提供了带宽、增益、功耗、增益压缩和输出噪声谱密度等关键性能参数。

Conclusion: 通过噪声反馈可在齐纳二极管中诱导负微分电阻，使其具备信号放大能力，为传统二极管器件提供了新的应用可能性。

Abstract: A voltage biased Zener diode always exhibit positive differential resistance, thus cannot be used as an element to provide amplification of a signal. We show how to induce negative differential resistance in the reverse bias regime of a 12V Zener diode by noise feedback. We use this to build a voltage amplifier in the audio frequency range, which we characterize by providing bandwidth, gain, power consumption, gain compression and output noise spectral density.

### [59] [Dynamics of O(2) excitations in a non-reciprocal medium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23225)
*Ylann Rouzaire,Daniel JG Pearce,Ignacio Pagonabarraga,Demian Levis*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了$\mathcal{O}(2)$模型中非互易性（non-reciprocity）引发的涌现动力学，建立了非互易性与活性（activity）的类比，并推导了描述一维激发的广义Burgers方程，为控制非互易介质中的激发轨迹提供了基本原理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索$\mathcal{O}(2)$模型中由非互易性产生的涌现动力学现象。非互易性源于类似视锥（vision cone）的耦合机制，这种非平衡特性与活性系统具有相似性，值得深入探究其动力学行为。

Method: 采用晶格XY模型（lattice XY model）作为研究框架，其中非互易性通过视锥状耦合实现。通过连续介质描述（continuum description），将非互易性转化为依赖于取向场旋度（rotational of the orientation field）的新项。从连续模型推导出描述一维激发的广义Burgers方程（generalized Burgers equation），并将结果扩展到二维扰动。

Result: 研究发现非互易性类似于活性（activity），其水动力学方程与恒定密度Toner-Tu框架（constant density Toner-Tu framework）存在联系。活性力（active force）能够平流和重塑模式，这是许多非互易系统的普遍特征。研究阐明了如何通过调节非互易程度和背景介质取向来控制激发的时间演化，并展示了不同初始激发导致截然不同的动力学行为。非互易性还影响具有非零绕数（winding numbers）的无缺陷激发的稳定性，使系统在超过特定阈值后能够弛豫到基态（ground state）。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了非互易$\mathcal{O}(2)$介质中激发轨迹控制的基本原理（first principles of excitation trajectory control）。通过分析非互易程度和背景介质取向对激发演化的影响，揭示了非互易系统独特的动力学特性，为非平衡统计物理和活性物质研究提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: We investigate emergent dynamics due to non-reciprocity in the $\mathcal{O}(2)$ model. The lattice XY model, where non-reciprocity stems from vision cone like couplings, can be described by a continuum description in which non-reciprocity translates into a new term depending on the rotational of the orientation field. We argue that non-reciprocity is akin to activity and we highlight the connection between our hydrodynamic equation and the constant density Toner-Tu framework. The active force advects and reshapes patterns, a generic feature found in many non-reciprocal systems. We show how $1d$ excitations in the non-reciprocal $\mathcal{O}(2)$ model can be described by a generalized Burgers equation, derived from our continuum model. We then extend the results to $2d$ perturbations. As such, we establish the first principles of excitation trajectory control in a non-reciprocal $\mathcal{O}(2)$ medium. Concretely, we explain how tuning the degree of non-reciprocity and the orientation of the background medium impacts the time evolution of excitations. We also showcase how initially different excitations lead to very different dynamical behavior. Non-reciprocity also affects the stability of defect-free excitations with non-zero winding numbers and, unlike in its equilibrium $O(2)$ counterpart, enables the system, above a certain threshold, to relax to its ground state.

</details>


### [60] [Internal stress drives ferromagnetic-like ordering in networks of proliferating bacteria](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23320)
*Nicola Pellicciotta,Luca Angelani,Roberto Di Leonardo*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究以大肠杆菌在单文件微通道网络中生长为模型，发现增殖系统在非平衡条件下会自发产生相干生长模式，这些模式可通过有效平衡统计力学描述，揭示了增殖活性物质与平衡统计力学之间的对应关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 增殖是生命的基本特征，但现有活性物质物理研究主要关注自推进剂，对增殖系统的定量框架仍在发展中。本研究旨在探索结构化环境中增殖系统的集体现象，以填补这一研究空白。

Method: 研究使用大肠杆菌在单文件微通道网络中生长作为结构化环境的最小模型。通过模拟生长弹性细胞，分析网络节点处因动力学约束积累的内部应力。

Result: 自由体积竞争驱动了跨代持续的相干生长模式自发出现，但当通道连接超过典型细胞出生大小时模式消失。尽管动力学具有强非平衡特征，观察到的现象可通过有效平衡描述定量捕捉，其中每个节点的流动状态由具有铁磁相互作用的自旋变量表示。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了增殖活性物质与平衡统计力学之间的惊人对应关系，突出了开放的基本问题，并为描述真实世界复杂环境中的生长现象提供了第一步。

Abstract: Proliferation is a defining feature of life. Through growth, division, and death, living systems consume energy and inject mass, breaking conservation laws and driving collective phenomena from biofilm formation to embryonic development. Yet, while active matter physics has advanced our understanding of self-propelled agents, quantitative frameworks for proliferating systems are still emerging, and most work focuses on simplified settings. Here, we study \textit{E.coli} bacteria growing inside a network of single-file microchannels as a minimal model of structured environments. Competition for free volume drives the spontaneous emergence of coherent growth patterns that persist across generations but vanish when the channel links exceed the typical cell size at birth. Despite the strongly out-of-equilibrium character of the dynamics, the observed phenomenology can be quantitatively captured by an effective equilibrium description in which the flow state at each node is represented by a spin variable with ferromagnetic interactions. Simulations of growing elastic cells show that this coupling arises from internal stress accumulated at network nodes due to dynamical constraints. Our results reveal a surprising correspondence between proliferating active matter and equilibrium statistical mechanics, highlighting open fundamental questions and offering a first step toward describing growth phenomena in real-world complex environments.

### [61] [The Fermi-Pasta-Ulam-Tsingou problem after 70 years: Universal laws of thermalization in lattice systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23347)
*Weicheng Fu,Zhen Wang,Wei Lin,Dahai He,Jiao Wang,Yong Zhang,Hong Zhao*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文总结了费米-帕斯塔-乌拉姆-曾九（Fermi-Pasta-Ulam-Tsingou）问题中弱非线性晶格系统热化（thermalization）机制的研究进展，提出了两类普适性晶格系统的热化行为及其判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在澄清费米-帕斯塔-乌拉姆-曾九（Fermi-Pasta-Ulam-Tsingou）问题的核心疑问：弱非线性晶格系统是否会发生热化（thermalization），以及通过何种机制实现热化。过去十年在这一领域取得了实质性进展。

Method: 研究基于微扰理论框架（perturbative framework），特别强调基于共振网络连通性（resonance-network connectivity）的热化判据，这一方法根植于弱波湍流理论（weak wave turbulence theory）。

Result: 研究发现经典晶格系统分为两个普适性类别：第一类系统具有扩展的正规模（extended normal modes），其热化时间标度（thermalization time scale）为$T_{\rm eq}\sim g^{-γ}$（$γ=2$），在热力学极限下必然热化；第二类系统的所有正规模都局域化（localized），其弛豫时间与系统尺寸无关，且指数$γ$在$g\to0$时发散，表明任意弱的非线性扰动都无法诱导热化。

Conclusion: 在第一类系统中，无序（disorder）不会阻碍热化，反而通过破坏平移对称性和放松波矢共振约束来增加准共振过程（quasi-resonant processes）的数量，从而加速热化；在第二类系统中，当同时存在在位势（on-site potentials）和无序时，所有正规模在足够大的系统中都会局域化，从而抑制热化。

Abstract: Over the past decade, substantial progress has been made in clarifying a central question of the Fermi-Pasta-Ulam-Tsingou problem: whether weakly nonlinear lattice systems thermalize and, if so, through what mechanisms. The current understanding is as follows. (a) Classical lattice systems fall into two universal classes. In the first, the Hamiltonian has extended normal modes. For sufficiently large systems, the thermalization time scales as $T_{\rm eq}\sim g^{-γ}$ with $γ=2$, where $g$ denotes the effective nonlinear strength, i.e., the perturbation strength or degree of non-integrability. Thus, in the thermodynamic limit, these systems inevitably thermalize. Typical examples include common one-, two-, and three-dimensional lattice models. In the second class, all normal modes are localized. Here the relaxation time is essentially independent of system size. Although one may still formally write $T_{\rm eq}\sim g^{-γ}$, the exponent $γ$ diverges as $g\to0$, implying that arbitrarily weak nonlinear perturbations cannot induce thermalization. For sufficiently small $g$, such systems may therefore be viewed, in a theoretical sense, as thermal insulators. (b) In systems of the first class, disorder does not obstruct thermalization. Rather, by breaking translational symmetry and relaxing wave-vector resonance constraints, it increases the number of quasi-resonant processes and can therefore accelerate thermalization. (c) In systems of the second class, when both on-site potentials and disorder are present, all normal modes become localized in sufficiently large systems, suppressing thermalization. The perturbative framework underlying these conclusions will also be presented systematically, with particular emphasis on the thermalization criterion based on resonance-network connectivity, an approach rooted in weak wave turbulence theory.

</details>

### [62] [Non-Hermitian Mosaic Maryland model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22682)
*Zhenning Wang,Ni Lu,Dan Liu,Xiaosen Yang,Xianqi Tong*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文引入非厄米马赛克马里兰模型，通过离散调制周期和非厄米相位的引入，使原本可积系统变得不可积，为研究结构调制如何控制复杂准周期势中的局域化提供了独特平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究结构调制如何控制复杂准周期势中的局域化，探索非厄米系统中波传输工程的新自由度，并增强扩展态的鲁棒性。

Method: 采用Avila全局理论，解析推导精确的李雅普诺夫指数，并获得复迁移率边的显式公式；通过谱缠绕数表征相位的拓扑性质；数值计算逆参与率和分形维数验证解析预测。

Result: 对于调制周期κ≥2，系统本征地拥有κ-1个鲁棒扩展带，这些扩展带独立于势强度和非厄米性而持续存在；马赛克调制诱导了迁移率边，相变是连续的，反映了系统的不可积性质。

Conclusion: 这项工作确立了结构设计作为工程化波传输的强大自由度，能够增强非厄米系统中扩展态的鲁棒性，为调控复杂准周期系统中的局域化提供了新途径。

Abstract: We introduce the non-Hermitian mosaic Maryland model, where a discrete modulation period and a non-Hermitian phase are incorporated into the potential, rendering the originally exactly solvable system generally non-integrable. This model provides a unique platform to investigate how structural modulation governs localization in complex quasiperiodic potentials. Using Avila's global theory, we analytically derive the exact Lyapunov exponent and obtain explicit formulas for the complex mobility edges. Remarkably, for modulation periods kappa >= 2, the system intrinsically hosts kappa-1 robust extended bands that persist independently of the potential strength and non-Hermiticity. We further characterize the topological nature of these phases via the spectral winding number. Unlike the standard Maryland model, the mosaic modulation induces mobility edges, and the resulting phase transitions are continuous, reflecting the non-integrable nature of the system. Numerical calculations of the inverse participation ratio and fractal dimension confirm the analytical predictions for the asymptotic form of the mobility edges in the large non-Hermiticity limit. This work establishes structural design as a powerful degree of freedom for engineering wave transport and enhancing the robustness of extended states in non-Hermitian systems.

### [63] [Generative Inversion of Spectroscopic Data for Amorphous Structure Elucidation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23210)
*Jiawei Guo,Daniel Schwalbe-Koda*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: GLASS是一个生成式框架，能够将多模态光谱测量数据反演为真实的原子结构，无需了解势能面信息。该框架通过基于分数的模型从低保真数据中学习结构先验，并生成符合可微分光谱目标的分布外结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从表征数据确定原子结构是材料科学中最常见但复杂的问题之一。特别是在非晶材料中，提出既真实又与实验一致的结构需要专家指导、良好的原子间势能或两者兼备。

Method: GLASS采用基于分数的模型（score-based model）从低保真数据中学习结构先验，并采样生成符合可微分光谱目标（differentiable spectral targets）的分布外结构。该方法无需了解势能面（potential energy surface）信息。

Result: 使用对分布函数（pair distribution functions, PDFs）、X射线吸收光谱和衍射测量的重建量化了光谱模态之间的互补性，并证明PDFs是该框架最具信息量的探针。GLASS成功应用于三个有争议的实验问题：非晶硅的准晶性、硫的液-液相变以及球磨非晶冰。

Conclusion: GLASS生成的原子结构能够重现实验测量结果，并揭示仅靠衍射分析无法获得的机制。该框架为从多模态光谱数据反演真实原子结构提供了一种无需势能面知识的有效方法。

Abstract: Determining atomistic structures from characterization data is one of the most common yet intricate problems in materials science. Particularly in amorphous materials, proposing structures that balance realism and agreement with experiments requires expert guidance, good interatomic potentials, or both. Here, we introduce GLASS, a generative framework that inverts multi-modal spectroscopic measurements into realistic atomistic structures without knowledge of the potential energy surface. A score-based model learns a structural prior from low-fidelity data and samples out-of-distribution structures conditioned on differentiable spectral targets. Reconstructions using pair distribution functions (PDFs), X-ray absorption spectroscopy, and diffraction measurements quantify the complementarity between spectral modalities and demonstrate that PDFs is the most informative probe for our framework. We use GLASS to rationalize three contested experimental problems: paracrystallinity in amorphous silicon, a liquid-liquid phase transition in sulfur, and ball-milled amorphous ice. In each case, generated structures reproduce experimental measurements and reveal mechanisms inaccessible to diffraction analysis alone.

### [65] [Cartier integration of infinitesimal 2-braidings via 2-holonomy of the CMKZ 2-connection, II: The pentagonator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22694)
*Cameron Kemp*

Main category: math.QA

TL;DR: 本文延续先前研究，提出Drinfeld-Kohno (Lie) 2-代数的上同调平凡猜想，并证明该猜想可简化辫子幺半2-范畴的构造：给定相干全对称无穷小2-辫子t，由四项关系子和t的whiskering构成的零变换上的修改自动消失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在重新阐释Cirio和Martins的工作，以提出Drinfeld-Kohno (Lie) 2-代数上同调平凡的基本猜想。该研究是系列论文的延续，关注辫子幺半2-范畴（braided monoidal 2-category）构造的简化问题。

Method: 通过重新语境化Cirio和Martins的研究来论证基本猜想，并证明该猜想的技术含义。最终利用Cirio和Martins在复直线上4个可区分粒子构型空间Y_4上的Knizhnik-Zamolodchikov 2-连接构造五角形算子（pentagonator），特别采用了Bordemann、Rivezzi和Weigel在Y_4中的五角形结构。

Result: 证明了Drinfeld-Kohno (Lie) 2-代数上同调平凡猜想蕴含重要推论：给定相干全对称无穷小2-辫子t，由四项关系子（four-term relationators）和t的whiskering构成的零变换上的修改自动消失。这一结果使得在相关上下文中只需构造辫子幺半2-范畴的数据即可自动满足公理。

Conclusion: 通过利用Cirio和Martins的Knizhnik-Zamolodchikov 2-连接和Bordemann等人的五角形结构，成功构造了五角形算子。研究展示了Drinfeld-Kohno (Lie) 2-代数上同调平凡猜想在简化高阶范畴构造中的实际应用价值。

Abstract: This is a continuation of the previous paper (arXiv:2508.01944) in this series. We recontextualise Cirio and Martins' work to motivate our fundamental conjecture that the Drinfeld-Kohno (Lie) 2-algebra has trivial cohomology. It is then shown that this conjecture implies the following: given a coherent totally symmetric infinitesimal 2-braiding $t$, every modification endomorphic on the zero transformation vanishes if it is made up of the four-term relationators and whiskerings by $t$. The power of such an implication is that, in our context, one need only construct the data of a braided monoidal 2-category and it will automatically satisfy the axioms. We thus conclude by constructing the pentagonator via Cirio and Martins' Knizhnik-Zamolodchikov 2-connection over the configuration space of 4 distinguishable particles on the complex line, $Y_4$. In particular, we make use of Bordemann, Rivezzi and Weigel's pentagon in $Y_4$.

</details>

### [66] [Primordial Non-Gaussianity and the Field-Level Cramer-Rao Bound](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22415)
*Eugene Chen,Daniel Green,Vincent S. H. Lee*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了如何从星系巡天图中最优提取原初非高斯性（primordial non-Gaussianity）信息，通过场级克拉美-罗界（field-level Cramer-Rao bound）分析发现，对于局域型非高斯性，多示踪尺度依赖偏置（multi-tracer scale-dependent bias）方法可超越传统高阶统计分析的灵敏度，但未能达到包含所有暗物质晕尺度模式时的最优约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原初非高斯性（primordial non-Gaussianity）是探测暴胀时期物理的有力探针，暴胀相关的粒子谱（包括质量和自旋）编码在绝热模的统计关联中。然而，在非线性结构形成背景下，测量这些信号的最优方法仍不明确，因为晚期非高斯性可能与原初物理产生简并，且尺度依赖偏置（scale-dependent bias）表明信息可从非高斯初始条件转移到高斯涨落的振幅中。

Method: 研究采用场级克拉美-罗界（field-level Cramer-Rao bound）来探究从现实宇宙巡天图中可提取信息的理论极限。该方法用于评估不同分析策略的最终约束能力，特别比较了多示踪尺度依赖偏置分析与包含所有暗物质晕（dark matter halos）尺度模式的最优约束。

Result: 对于局域型非高斯性（local non-Gaussianity），多示踪尺度依赖偏置分析可超越保守的高阶点（higher-point）统计分析的灵敏度。但正如预期，当包含暗物质晕尺度的所有模式时，多示踪分析未能达到最优约束。研究还对未来巡天在等边型（equilateral）和局域型非高斯性方面的探测潜力进行了预测。

Conclusion: 等边型非高斯性对先验和建模假设高度敏感，可从理论输入（如偏置（bias）的红移演化）中显著受益。研究阐明了原初信息在星系巡天图中的编码方式，并为未来观测提供了理论指导。

Abstract: Primordial non-Gaussianity is one of the most powerful probes of the inflationary epoch. The particle spectrum relevant to inflation, including masses and spins, is encoded in the precise form of statistical correlations of the adiabatic modes. Yet, in the presence of nonlinear structure formation, the optimal approach to measuring these signals remains unclear. Accurate modeling becomes crucial as late-time non-Gaussianty can become degenerate with primordial physics. Moreover, scale-dependent bias shows that information can move from non-Gaussian initial conditions to the amplitude of the Gaussian fluctuations. In this paper, we aim to clarify how primordial information is encoded in maps of galaxies. We use the field-level Cramer-Rao bound to investigate the ultimate limit of what can be extracted from realistic maps of the Universe. For local non-Gaussianity, we show that multi-tracer scale-dependent bias can exceed the sensitivity of conservative higher-point analyses. However, as expected, the multi-tracer analysis falls short of the optimal constraint when all the modes at the scale of the dark matter halos are included. We then forecast the potential reach of future surveys for equilateral and local non-Gaussianity. Equilateral in particular is highly sensitive to priors and modeling assumptions and can benefit dramatically from theoretical input such as the redshift evolution of the bias.

</details>


### [67] [Phantom-Crossing Dark Energy and the $Ω_m$ Tug-of-War](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22406)
*David Shlivko,Vivian Poulin*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 联合宇宙微波背景（CMB）、重子声学振荡（BAO）和Ia型超新星（SN）数据的分析显示，暗能量状态方程$w$存在穿越幻影（phantom crossing）的观测倾向。这种倾向源于各数据集单独拟合ΛCDM模型时出现的Ω_m张力，特别是由于Ω_m^BAO < Ω_m^CMB < Ω_m^SN的排序关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期结合宇宙微波背景（cosmic microwave background, CMB）、重子声学振荡（baryon acoustic oscillations, BAO）和Ia型超新星（Type Ia supernovae, SN）数据的分析显示，暗能量状态方程$w$存在穿越幻影（phantom crossing）的观测倾向。本研究旨在探讨这种倾向的物理根源，特别是其与各数据集在ΛCDM框架下Ω_m参数张力之间的关系。

Method: 通过理论分析和经验验证相结合的方法，研究穿越幻影模型如何调整各数据集的Ω_m推断值以实现相互对齐。同时对比分析限制在$w \geq -1$的quintessence理论在处理不同数据集张力时的表现差异。

Result: 穿越幻影模型能够将所有数据集的Ω_m推断值向相互对齐的方向调整，而quintessence理论虽然能缓解与SN数据的张力，却会加剧BAO-CMB之间的差异。在联合分析中，BAO和CMB测量（而非SN数据）驱动了对穿越幻影模型的偏好。此外，SN数据在穿越幻影模型下与其他数据集表现出更大的张力，导致CMB+BAO+SN联合分析中对穿越幻影的偏好弱于单独的CMB+BAO分析。

Conclusion: 观测数据对穿越幻影的偏好是Ω_m张力的自然结果，特别是由于Ω_m^BAO < Ω_m^CMB < Ω_m^SN的排序关系。BAO和CMB测量是驱动穿越幻影偏好的主要因素，而非SN数据。在完整数据集分析中，SN数据与穿越幻影模型的较大张力削弱了这种偏好强度。

Abstract: Recent analyses combining data from the cosmic microwave background (CMB), baryon acoustic oscillations (BAO), and Type Ia supernovae (SN) have revealed a tentative observational preference for phantom crossing in the dark energy equation of state $w$. We argue that this preference is a natural consequence of the $Ω_m$ tensions that arise when these datasets are individually fit to $Λ$CDM, specifically because of the ordering $Ω_m^\mathrm{BAO} < Ω_m^\mathrm{CMB} < Ω_m^\mathrm{SN}$. We show both theoretically and empirically that models with phantom crossing can shift all of these inferred $Ω_m$ values toward mutual alignment. In contrast, quintessence theories restricted to $w \geq -1$ can alleviate the tensions with SN data but only at the cost of exacerbating the BAO-CMB discrepancy. We therefore conclude that it is the BAO and CMB measurements - not the SN data - that drive the preference for phantom crossing over quintessence in joint analyses. Moreover, we point out that SN data exhibit greater tensions with the other datasets when fit to phantom-crossing models than when fit to quintessence, causing the preference for phantom crossing to be weaker in joint CMB+BAO+SN analyses than in analyses of CMB+BAO data alone.

</details>


### [68] [Revisiting Constraints on Primordial Curvature Power Spectrum from PBH Abundances](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23025)
*Ashu Kushwaha,Teruaki Suyama*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究利用最新原初黑洞（PBH）丰度约束推导了原初曲率功率谱振幅的上限，系统比较了Press-Schechter（PS）形式与峰值理论，并量化了球对称与非球对称塌缩标准的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原初黑洞（PBH）形成机制在原初曲率扰动峰值尺度与PBH质量间建立了近似一一对应关系，使得PBH丰度约束可转化为原初曲率功率谱振幅的上限，从而间接探测与这些较小尺度对应的暴胀最后e-fold阶段。

Method: 采用最新PBH丰度约束推导窄峰和宽峰原初曲率功率谱的振幅限制，系统比较Press-Schechter（PS）形式与峰值理论，并考虑曲率扰动与密度对比间的非线性关系，量化球对称与非球对称塌缩标准的影响。

Result: 包含非球对称性显著增加了推断的原初功率谱振幅，反映了PBH形成所需的更大阈值密度对比；对于单色情况，PS形式与峰值理论约束基本相似，但在宽原初功率谱情况下向较小尺度显著偏离，突显当前约束对统计形式选择的敏感性。

Conclusion: 对单色和扩展质量函数的一致处理提供了基于现有方法的系统映射，同时强调减少这些理论不确定性是通过PBH探测早期宇宙的关键步骤，当前约束仍对统计形式选择敏感。

Abstract: Primordial black holes (PBHs) can form in the early Universe, for instance during radiation domination, from the collapse of large-amplitude density perturbations shortly after horizon re-entry. This mechanism establishes an approximate one-to-one correspondence between the PBH mass and the scale of the peak in the primordial curvature perturbations. Consequently, the constraints on PBH abundances can be translated into upper limits on the amplitude of the primordial curvature power spectrum, thereby providing an indirect probe of the last e-folds of inflation corresponding to these smaller scales. We derive constraints on the amplitude of primordial curvature power spectra with both narrow and broad peaks using the most up-to-date bounds on PBH abundances. Given the theoretical uncertainties in PBH formation, we systematically compare the constraints obtained using the Press-Schechter (PS) formalism and peak theory, accounting for the nonlinear relation between curvature perturbations and density contrast. We quantify the impact of spherical versus non-spherical collapse criteria and show that including non-sphericity significantly increases the inferred amplitude of the primordial power spectrum, reflecting the larger threshold density contrast required for PBH formation. We also find that whereas the constraints obtained using the PS formalism and peak theory remain largely similar for the monochromatic case, they differ significantly toward smaller scales in the case of a broad primordial power spectrum. This discrepancy underscores that current constraints remain sensitive to the choice of statistical formalism. Our consistent treatment of monochromatic and extended mass functions provides a systematic mapping based on existing methodologies, while highlighting that reducing these theoretical uncertainties is a crucial step toward probing the early Universe through PBHs.

</details>


### [69] [Low-Frequency Stochastic Gravitational-Wave Background in Gaia DR3 catalogue](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23028)
*V. Akhmetov,L. Filipello,M. Crosta,M. G. Lattanzi,B. Bucciarelli,U. Abbas,F. Santucci*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究探讨利用Gaia任务观测的类星体自行运动探测低频引力波（gravitational waves）的潜力，通过模拟分析比较了两种数据分析方法：矢量球谐函数（Vector Spherical Harmonics）和角相关函数（Hellings-Downs curves），并评估了Gaia DR3数据对随机引力波背景（stochastic GW background）的探测极限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索利用Gaia任务观测的遥远类星体自行运动来探测低频引力波的可能性。该方法基于引力波对类星体自行运动的影响，为引力波天文学提供了新的观测窗口。

Method: 研究方法包括使用Gaia DR3的天体测量数据，模拟引力波对类星体自行运动的影响，并采用两种数据分析技术：矢量球谐函数（VSH）和角相关函数（Hellings-Downs curves, HDC）。研究还评估了不同数据限制和加权方案对引力波应变估计的影响。

Result: 研究结果显示，对于Gaia DR3的自行运动误差，可探测的引力波应变下限为10^{-11}，下一代Gaia数据释放（DR4）可能改进至约3×10^{-12}。VSH方法在统计上更稳健，计算成本更低（与N成比例），而HDC方法对引力波探测更敏感但计算复杂度更高（与N^2成比例）。

Conclusion: 研究表明利用Gaia观测的类星体自行运动探测低频引力波具有可行性。VSH方法在统计稳健性和计算效率方面优于HDC方法，而探测极限受观测时间跨度、天体测量精度和类星体天空分布等因素约束，为未来引力波探测提供了重要参考。

Abstract: We investigate the potential to detect low-frequency gravitational waves (GWs) through their imprints on the proper motions of distant quasars observed by the Gaia mission. Using astrometric data from Gaia DR3, we simulate the effect of GWs on the proper motions of quasars, incorporating their actual sky positions and measurement uncertainties.
  We investigate two data analysis techniques for the extraction and characterization of GW signals from quasar proper motions: Vector Spherical Harmonics (VSH) and angular correlation functions, commonly referred to as Hellings-Downs curves (HDC). Using realistic simulated data, we forecast their sensitivity and accuracy to GWs, and evaluate the impact of systematic errors. From these simulations, we derive an upper limit on the amplitude of a stochastic GW background, constrained by the observational timespan, astrometric precision, and the sky distribution of quasars.
  Compared to HDC, VSH appears more statistically robust, less prone to selection effects, and with a significantly smaller computational cost, scaling as N. The HDC method is more sensitive for detecting gravitational waves, but its complexity scales as N^2.
  We find that, with Gaia DR3 proper motion errors, the lower limit for a detectable GW strain is of 10^{-11}, with possible improvements to about 3 x 10^{-12} for the next Gaia Data Release 4 (for the same number of quasars). This limit holds for a stochastic GW spectrum integrated over all frequencies less than half the inverse of the 34-month observational timespan of Gaia DR3, corresponding to approximately 5.6 nHz. We also investigate how different data-restriction and weighting schemes influence the final estimate of the gravitational wave strain.

</details>


### [70] [Solving the Cosmic Coincidence Problem: The Locally Pumped Dark Energy Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23473)
*Carlo R. Contaldi,Mauro Pieroni*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出局域泵浦暗能量（LPDE）机制，认为宇宙加速膨胀由暗物质非线性结构的形成触发。通过有效场论描述，暗物质晕形成过程中短波长模式的增长会诱导重标量场χ的局域平衡点偏移，产生真空能量贡献，其全局效应由晕的体积填充因子控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在建立宇宙加速膨胀与结构形成之间的物理联系。传统ΛCDM模型将暗能量视为宇宙学常数，缺乏与宇宙结构演化的直接关联，而LPDE机制试图从暗物质晕形成的物理过程中自然推导出暗能量行为。

Method: 采用有效场论（effective-field-theory）描述，通过对密度对比剖面进行粗粒化（coarse-graining），分析暗物质晕形成过程中短波长模式的增长如何诱导重标量场χ的局域平衡点偏移。利用基准ΛCDM宇宙学的晕质量函数（halo mass function）进行计算，并通过体积平均（volume-averaging）处理晕种群的贡献。

Result: 研究表明真空能量主导通常在红移z∼O(1)时出现，自然地将宇宙加速膨胀与结构形成关联起来。该机制的具体实现显示，由于自然地具有瞬态加速时期，能与包括暗能量光谱仪（DESI）在内的最新宇宙学数据保持极好的一致性。

Conclusion: LPDE机制为宇宙加速膨胀提供了与结构形成直接相关的物理解释，避免了宇宙学常数问题。该机制通过暗物质晕形成过程中诱导的局域真空能量贡献，自然地产生瞬态加速时期，与观测数据相符。

Abstract: We propose the Locally Pumped Dark Energy (LPDE) mechanism in which cosmic acceleration is triggered by the emergence of non-linear dark matter structure. In an effective-field-theory description, coarse-graining over the density contrast profile, whose short-wavelength modes grow during halo formation, induces a shift in the local equilibrium point of a second, sufficiently heavy scalar field $χ$. At early times, the pump mechanism is negligible and $χ$ remains fixed at the origin, contributing no DE. As structures form, the equilibrium value of $χ$ is locally displaced within halos, generating a vacuum energy whose global contribution, in a mean-field picture, is controlled by the halo volume filling factor. If the $χ$ field is sufficiently heavy, with a Compton wavelength limited by halo scales, its response is localised, and spatial gradients are exponentially suppressed on large scales. After volume-averaging over the halo population, the resulting contribution on large scales behaves as a homogeneous DE component. Using the halo mass function of a fiducial $Λ$CDM cosmology, we show that vacuum-energy domination generically emerges at $z\sim\mathcal{O}(1)$, naturally correlating cosmic acceleration with structure formation. For reference, we present an explicit realisation of such a mechanism and show that, by naturally featuring a transient acceleration epoch, it can be in excellent agreement with the most recent cosmological data, including the Dark Energy Spectroscopic Instrument (DESI).

</details>

Using flow techniques, we prove that a neighbourhood of a stable MOTS in a null cone may be foliated by hypersurfaces of constant spacetime mean curvature. We also provide methods to construct prescribed spacetime mean curvature surfaces within null cones.

### [72] [Energy-Morawetz estimates for Teukolsky equations in perturbations of Kerr](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23437)
*Siyuan Ma,J'er'emie Szeftel*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文证明了在完全亚极端（full subextremal）范围内，对Kerr度规扰动时空中的Teukolsky方程解的能量估计和Morawetz估计，这是解决Kerr稳定性猜想的关键步骤。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在将当前仅适用于慢旋转情况的Kerr稳定性证明（见参考文献GCM1、GCM2等）扩展到完全解决Kerr稳定性猜想，即证明Kerr时空族对所有亚极端角动量都是非线性稳定的。

Method: 采用基于非可积形式（non-integrable formalism）的张量形式Teukolsky方程，遵循Teukolsky波/输运系统（Teukolsky wave/transport system）方法。通过扩展标量波问题的思想，使用r-叶化适应微局部分析乘子（r-foliation-adapted microlocal multipliers）控制波部分，并结合技术控制线性耦合项。引入合适的正则标量化程序（regular scalarization procedure）以适应张量波。

Result: 证明了在完全亚极端范围内，对Kerr度规扰动时空中的Teukolsky方程解的能量估计和Morawetz估计。这些估计与标量波问题的结果共同构成了扩展Kerr稳定性证明的关键步骤。

Conclusion: 本文结果为解决完整的Kerr稳定性猜想提供了重要进展，将当前仅适用于慢旋转情况的稳定性证明扩展到所有亚极端角动量范围，是证明Kerr时空族非线性稳定性的关键组成部分。

Abstract: In this paper, we prove energy and Morawetz estimates for solutions to Teukolsky equations in spacetimes with metrics that are perturbations, compatible with nonlinear applications, of Kerr metrics in the full subextremal range. The Teukolsky equations are written in tensorial form using the non-integrable formalism in \cite{GKS22}, and we follow the approach in \cite{Ma} of relying on a Teukolsky wave/transport system. The estimates are proved by extending the ideas from our earlier result \cite{MaSz24} on the corresponding problem for the scalar wave, notably the use of $r$-foliation-adapted microlocal multipliers for the wave part, and by incorporating techniques from \cite{Ma} to control the linear coupling terms between the components of the Teukolsky wave/transport system. Additionally, in order to adapt the methodology of \cite{MaSz24} to tensorial waves, we introduce a well-suited regular scalarization procedure which is of independent interest. This result, alongside our companion paper \cite{MaSz24}, is an essential step towards extending the current proof of Kerr stability in \cite{GCM1} \cite{GCM2} \cite{KS:Kerr} \cite{GKS22} \cite{Shen}, valid in the slowly rotating case, to a complete resolution of the Kerr stability conjecture, i.e., the statement that the Kerr family of spacetimes is nonlinearly stable for all subextremal angular momenta.

</details>

### [73] [The Crimson Kiss of Two Giants: Helium Detonation and High-Energy Neutrino Production](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22419)
*Cecilia Romero Rodríguez,Pau Amaro Seoane*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该研究提出红巨星碰撞过程中氦核并合（erythrohenosis）产生高能中微子的新机制，能够解释IceCube观测到的弥散中微子通量，并为致密恒星系统中的多信使观测提供独特信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索红巨星碰撞中简并氦核并合过程（erythrohenosis）作为高能中微子新型天体物理源的潜力，特别是解释IceCube观测到的弥散中微子通量。

Method: 采用MESA生成的恒星模型和SPH（smoothed particle hydrodynamics）模拟最终螺旋阶段，建立半解析模型估算氢混合量、能量释放（约4.28×10^49 erg）、最终温度（T_f≈5.3×10^8 K）、磁场放大（B≈1.77×10^10 G）及中微子通量。

Result: 预测的TeV-PeV中微子信号可解释IceCube观测的弥散中微子通量；单个并合事件在约2 Mpc内可被探测；磁化氦闪概率及氢混合激活CNO循环（carbon-nitrogen-oxygen cycle）被评估；¹⁸F衰变中微子为爆轰提供直接观测检验。

Conclusion: 红巨星核碰撞同时产生高能强子中微子、引力波和可能的电磁信号，构成独特的多信使特征，将erythrohenosis事件定位为致密恒星系统中奇特但潜在可观测的现象。

Abstract: The coalescence of degenerate helium cores during red giant collisions - a process we term erythrohenosis - introduces a novel class of transient astrophysical sources of high-energy neutrinos. Using stellar models generated with MESA and SPH simulations of the final inspiral phase, we develop a semi-analytical model to estimate the amount of hydrogen mixed into the cores, the energy release ($\approx 4.28 \times 10^{49}$ erg) that heats the remnant to $T_f \approx 5.3 \times 10^8$ K, the magnetic field amplification ($B \approx 1.77 \times 10^{10}$ G), and the resulting neutrino flux. We find that the predicted TeV--PeV neutrino signal can account for the diffuse neutrino flux observed by IceCube and demonstrate that a single merger event within $\sim 2$ Mpc would be detectable in this energy regime. Furthermore, we discuss the probability of a magnetized helium flash and assess the subsequent activation of the CNO cycle in the remnant core due to hydrogen mixing. In particular, neutrinos from the decay of $^{18}$F offer a direct observational test of the detonation. The simultaneous emission of high-energy hadronic neutrinos, gravitational waves, and -- if the optical depth permits -- an electromagnetic signal would constitute a unique multimessenger signature of red giant core collisions, positioning erythrohenosis events as exotic yet potentially observable phenomena in dense stellar systems.

</details>


### [74] [Impact of eccentricity on the population properties of neutron star - black hole mergers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22461)
*Gonzalo Morras,Geraint Pratten,Patricia Schmidt*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该研究利用GWTC-4中的低质量致密双星并合事件，重新分析中子星-黑洞（NSBH）并合系统的群体性质。通过使用能同时捕捉轨道偏心率和自旋进动的pyEFPE波形模型，发现GW200105是唯一在20Hz处显示显著残余偏心率的NSBH系统，支持其动态形成机制，而其他NSBH事件则与孤立恒星演化形成的低自旋双星一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在重新审视中子星-黑洞（NSBH）并合系统的群体性质，特别是通过分析轨道偏心率和自旋进动来区分不同的形成通道（formation channels）。随着NSBH探测数量的增加，对这些系统质量、自旋和轨道偏心率的联合约束将能够更精确地检验动态形成与孤立演化机制。

Method: 采用pyEFPE波形模型重新分析GWTC-4中所有双中子星（BNS）和NSBH事件，该模型仅包含旋近阶段（inspiral-only）但能同时捕捉轨道偏心率和自旋诱导的进动（spin-induced precession）。使用分层贝叶斯推断（hierarchical Bayesian inference）获得NSBH双星质量、自旋和偏心率的首次联合分布约束。

Result: 双中子星系统GW170817和GW190425完全符合准圆形旋近（quasi-circular inspirals），而NSBH系统中只有GW200105在20Hz处显示出显著的残余偏心率，支持其动态形成路径（dynamically driven formation pathways）。其余NSBH事件未显示可测量的偏心率，与孤立恒星演化形成的低自旋双星基本一致。研究首次获得了NSBH双星质量、自旋和偏心率的联合分布约束，并首次同时约束了NSBH并合中的自旋进动和轨道偏心率。

Conclusion: 偏心率的测量已成为区分不同形成通道的关键判别因子。将所有NSBH系统视为单一群体时，结果与分层三重系统（hierarchical triples）形成机制兼容，而准圆形群体则与孤立演化基本一致。随着NSBH探测数量的增加，对质量、自旋和轨道偏心率的联合约束将能够更精确地检验动态形成与孤立演化机制，确立NSBH系统作为致密天体天体物理学的有力探针。

Abstract: We revisit the population properties of neutron star-black hole (NSBH) mergers using low-mass compact binary coalescences reported through GWTC-4. Employing pyEFPE, an inspiral-only waveform model that captures both orbital eccentricity and spin-induced precession, we reanalyse all binary neutron star (BNS) and NSBH events observed via gravitational waves. The BNS systems GW170817 and GW190425 are fully consistent with quasi-circular inspirals, while GW200105 stands out among the NSBH binaries as the only system exhibiting significant residual eccentricity at 20 Hz, strengthening evidence for dynamically driven formation pathways. The remaining NSBH events show no measurable eccentricity and appear broadly compatible with low-spin binaries formed through isolated stellar evolution. Using hierarchical Bayesian inference, we obtain the first joint constraints on the mass, spin, and eccentricity distributions of NSBH binaries. Our results also yield the first simultaneous constraints on spin precession and orbital eccentricity in NSBH mergers, while the inferred merger rates remain fully consistent with previous LVK measurements. Treating all NSBH systems as a single population yields results compatible with formation in hierarchical triples, whereas the quasi-circular population remains broadly consistent with isolated evolution. Our results highlight the emerging role of eccentricity as a key discriminator between formation channels. As the number of NSBH detections grows, joint constraints on masses, spins, and orbital eccentricity will enable increasingly sharp tests of dynamical versus isolated binary evolution, establishing NSBH systems as powerful probes of compact-object astrophysics.

</details>

### [75] [Probing Electromigration of Oxygen Vacancies in YBa$_2$Cu$_3$O$_{7-δ}$ Devices by Multimodal X-ray Techniques](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22635)
*Caio C. Quaglio-Gomes,Stefan Marinković,Elijah A. Abbey,Davi A. D. Chaves,Anna Palau,Alejandro V. Silhanek,Pedro Schio,Maycon Motta*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过多技术表征揭示了脉冲电迁移（pulsed electromigration）在YBCO微桥中诱导的氧空位重排过程，发现晶格c轴膨胀与光学对比度变化具有空间一致性，表明不同表征技术捕获了相同的氧重排机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电流控制YBa₂Cu₃O₇-δ（YBCO）等复杂氧化物中氧空位的方法因其实现相对简单且在基础研究和超导器件性能调控方面具有潜力而备受关注。然而，基于电流技术的结构演化和深度依赖效应，特别是光学特征与氧空位空间分布之间的联系，仍未被充分探索。

Method: 研究结合纳米探针X射线衍射（NanoXRD）、Cu K边X射线吸收近边结构（XANES）、X射线光电子能谱（XPS）、电输运测量和光学测量等多种技术，系统表征了脉冲电迁移在YBCO微桥中诱导的改性效应。

Result: 观察到c轴膨胀与Cu-O链中氧耗尽的光谱特征相关，并确认氧重排、晶体结构变化和铜配位在不同技术中表现一致。特别地，晶胞膨胀的空间分布与电迁移后观察到的光学对比度变化紧密对应，表明不同特征捕获了相同的底层氧重排过程。研究还发现光学显微镜无法可靠捕获涉及强电阻变化的两极电迁移过程，因为表面脱氧过程在很大程度上不可逆。

Conclusion: 这些发现为微观理解YBCO中电流辅助的氧迁移提供了重要进展，并为有效利用高温超导器件中的空位控制建立了框架。

Abstract: Control of oxygen vacancies by electrical currents in complex oxides such as YBa$_2$Cu$_3$O$_{7-δ}$ (YBCO) has attracted considerable interest due to the relative simplicity of its implementation and its potential for both fundamental studies and the tuning of superconducting device properties. However, the structural evolution and depth-dependent effects associated with current-based techniques remain largely unexplored, particularly with respect to the connection between optical signatures and the spatial distribution of oxygen vacancies. Here, we combine nanoprobe X-ray Diffraction (NanoXRD), Cu K-edge X-ray Absorption Near-Edge Structure (XANES), X-ray Photoelectron Spectroscopy (XPS), electrical transport, and optical measurements to reveal modifications induced in YBCO microbridges by pulsed electromigration. We observe a c-axis expansion correlated with spectroscopic features of oxygen depletion in the Cu-O chains, and we confirm that oxygen redistribution, crystallographic changes, and copper coordination evolve consistently across techniques. Notably, the spatial profile of unit-cell expansion closely follows the optical contrast observed after electromigration, demonstrating that the different signatures capture the same underlying oxygen reordering. We further show that optical microscopy cannot reliably capture bipolar electromigration involving strong resistance modifications, as surface deoxygenation appears largely irreversible. Taken together, our findings provide a significant step toward a microscopic understanding of current-assisted oxygen migration in YBCO and establish a framework for effectively exploiting vacancy control in high-temperature superconducting devices.

*Chethan Sanjeevappa,Anirudh Chandrasekaran,Joseph J. Betouras*

TL;DR: 该研究分析了具有X$_9$型高阶范霍夫奇点（Van Hove singularity）的四重对称量子材料，探讨了其在哈伯德排斥相互作用（Hubbard repulsive interactions）下形成三重态超导（triplet state superconductivity）的可能性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于分析具有四重对称色散关系（four-fold symmetric dispersion relation）的量子材料，该材料在费米能（Fermi energy）处表现出单个X$_9$型高阶范霍夫奇点，并探讨其在排斥相互作用下形成超导态的可能性。

Method: 首先详细分析了色散关系在标准形式下的结构、类型和态密度（density of states）；随后考虑哈伯德排斥相互作用，通过求解能隙方程（gap equation）研究超导态的形成条件。

Result: 当布里渊区（Brillouin zone）存在单个奇点时，可以形成临界温度T$_c$与相互作用强度呈幂律依赖关系的三重态超导。研究还讨论了涨落效应，并为钌酸盐Sr$_3$Ru$_2$O$_7$提供了可能的超导临界温度上限。

Conclusion: 研究表明，具有X$_9$型高阶范霍夫奇点的量子材料在排斥相互作用下能够支持三重态超导，这为理解钌酸盐Sr$_3$Ru$_2$O$_7$等材料的超导性质提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We study a four-fold symmetric dispersion relation of a quantum material, which exhibits a single high-order Van Hove singularity of X$_9$ type at the Fermi energy. First, we analyze in detail its form, type and density of states when the energy dispersion is in its canonical form. Subsequently, we study the possibility of a superconducting state when Hubbard repulsive interactions are taken into account. By solving the gap equation, it is shown that triplet state superconductivity with power-law dependence of the critical temperature T$_c$ on the interaction strength can be formed when a single singularity is present in the Brillouin zone. We discuss the effects of fluctuations and provide an upper bound of a possible superconducting critical temperature for the ruthenate Sr$_3$Ru$_2$O$_7$ which has been shown to exhibit this type of singularity.

### [77] [A mechanism for nonmonotonic $T_{c,max}(n)$ in multilayer cuprates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22662)
*Pavel Kornilovitch*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究基于预配对机制（preformed pair mechanism）解释了层状铜氧化物超导体中最大临界温度$T_{c,max}$与导电层数$n$的依赖关系，揭示了铜氧平面通过调控晶格各向异性来平衡载流子空穴的吸引能与动能，从而优化超导性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在解释层状铜氧化物超导体中观察到的最大临界温度$T_{c,max}$与导电层数$n$之间的依赖关系，特别是$T_{c,max}$在$n=1$到$n=3$之间增加，而在$n>3$时下降的实验现象。

Method: 采用预配对机制（preformed pair mechanism）框架，分析铜氧平面（copper-oxygen planes）如何精细调控晶格各向异性（lattice anisotropy），并调节载流子空穴（carrier holes）的吸引能与动能之间的平衡。

Result: 研究发现$T_{c,max}$在$n=1$到$n=3$之间增加是因为配对变得"更轻"（lighter），而$n>3$时动能上升削弱了配对，导致配对体积膨胀和$T_{c,max}$降低；通过调节模型参数，$T_{c,max}(n)$的峰值可出现在$n=2$、$n=3$或$n>3$处。

Conclusion: 该研究为理解层状铜氧化物超导体的$T_{c,max}$与层数关系提供了理论解释，并讨论了利用这一知识将$T_{c,max}$提升超过当前138 K记录的策略，为设计更高临界温度的超导材料提供了理论指导。

Abstract: We propose an explanation of the observed dependence of the maximal critical temperature $T_{c,max}$ on the number of conducting layers $n$ in layered copper-oxide superconductors within the preformed pair mechanism. Copper-oxygen planes fine-tune the lattice anisotropy and regulate the balance between the attractive and kinetic energies of carrier holes. To maximize the Bose-Einstein condensation temperature, real-space pairs must be compact and light at the same time. Generally, $T_{c,max}$ increases between $n = 1$ and $n = 3$ because pairs become lighter. For $n > 3$, the rising kinetic energy weakens the pairs, leading to inflated pair volumes and reduced $T_{c,max}$. By varying model parameters, the peak of $T_{c,max}(n)$ can be tuned to $n = 2$, $n = 3$, or $n > 3$. We also discuss strategies for using this knowledge to boost $T_{c,max}$ beyond the current record of 138 K.

</details>

*Angelo Valli,Laura Fanfarillo*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文研究了多轨道向列金属中Hund关联如何重塑玻色子介导的超导性，发现超越准粒子描述的动力学关联效应对于理解Hund区域超导鲁棒性至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导性和向列性（nematicity）在许多关联系统中共存，包括铁基超导体。研究旨在探索Hund驱动的关联如何重塑多轨道向列金属中的玻色子介导超导性。

Method: 采用超越准粒子描述的动力学关联效应方法，对多轨道向列金属中的Hund关联进行控制截断分析，研究不同频率窗口对配对的贡献。

Result: Hund关联同时增强了超导能隙的轨道分化，并抑制了极端向列驱动的轨道极化和相干性崩溃。控制截断分析揭示了能隙的非平凡、轨道依赖的积累过程。

Abstract: Superconductivity and nematicity coexist in the phase diagram of many correlated systems, including iron-based superconductors. We investigate how Hund-driven correlations reshape boson-mediated superconductivity in a multiorbital nematic metal. We find that dynamical correlation effects beyond a quasiparticle-only description are essential to capture the robustness of superconductivity in the Hund regime. In the nematic phase, Hund correlations simultaneously enhance the orbital differentiation of the superconducting gaps and inhibit the most extreme nematic-driven orbital polarization and coherence collapse that would otherwise suppress pairing at strong coupling. A controlled cutoff analysis reveals a nontrivial, orbital-dependent buildup of the gaps, indicating that different frequency windows of the correlated spectrum contribute unevenly to pairing in the nematic Hund regime. This implies that pairing mechanisms with different characteristic boson energies can lead to distinct gap structures and trends.

### [79] [Glassy magnetic freezing of interacting clusters in LK-99-family materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23377)
*Serafim Teknowijoyo,Domenico Napoletani,Vahan Nikoghosyan,Armen Gulian*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在澄清LK-99家族材料中观察到的磁化异常现象的本质，这些异常先前可能被误解为超导特征。需要确定这些可重复出现的低温磁化异常的物理起源。

Method: 采用水热合成法制备铜掺杂磷灰石材料，通过直流磁化、交流磁化率、磁场依赖性和磁记忆效应等多重磁学测量进行详细分析。同时进行成分和结构分析以识别材料中的相组成。

Result: 磁化异常在可比条件下制备的样品中一致出现，Mydosh参数虽处于超导体涡旋玻璃行为范围内，但综合分析表明现象与超导无关。数据与相互作用团簇的玻璃态磁冻结行为一致，成分分析确认covellite（CuS）相是观测行为的主要来源。

Conclusion: 研究明确了LK-99相关异常的磁性起源，并强调了相复杂性在解释该材料家族中表观超导特征时的重要性。观测到的现象源于材料中普遍存在的covellite（CuS）次生相引起的玻璃态磁冻结。

Abstract: We report reproducible magnetization anomalies appearing below room temperature in copper-doped apatite materials belonging to the LK-99 family synthesized via hydrothermal methods. These anomalies are observed consistently across samples prepared under comparable conditions. Although the extracted Mydosh parameter lies within the range often associated with vortex-glass behavior in superconductors, a detailed analysis of DC magnetization, AC susceptibility, field dependence, and magnetic memory effects demonstrates that the observed phenomena are not related to superconductivity. Instead, the data are consistent with glassy magnetic freezing of interacting clusters. Compositional and structural analysis identifies covellite (CuS), an ubiquitous secondary phase in these intrinsically multiphase materials, as the primary origin of the observed behavior. Our results clarify the magnetic origin of LK-99-related anomalies and highlight the importance of phase complexity in interpreting apparent superconducting signatures in this materials family.

</details>


### [80] [A Zero-Bias Superconducting Voltage Amplifier Based on the Bipolar Thermoelectric Effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23400)
*Giacomo Trupiano,Giorgio De Simoni,Francesco Giazotto*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文介绍了一种零偏置超导电压放大器，该器件利用非对称隧道结中的负微分电阻（NDR），从热梯度中获取能量实现电压放大。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在开发一种无需外部电偏置的超导电压放大器，仅利用电极间的温差实现信号放大，为超导电路应用提供新的解决方案。

Method: 器件基于非对称超导体-绝缘体-超导体（SIS）结，其能隙比为Δ₁/Δ₂ = 0.5，与负载电阻串联。利用超导双极热电效应，在结的电流-电压特性中产生负微分电阻区域。

Result: 数值模拟预测电压增益达20 dB，1 dB压缩点输入幅度为2 μV，总谐波失真低于-50 dB。输入参考噪声约1 nV/√Hz，热负载为纳瓦量级，频率响应从近直流到约180 MHz。

Conclusion: 热电超导结能够实现从近直流到约200 MHz的无偏置电压放大，适用于跃迁边缘传感器读出、量子电路仪器化和低频低温信号处理等应用。

Abstract: We introduce a zero-bias superconducting voltage amplifier that harvests energy from a thermal gradient by exploiting negative differential resistance (NDR) in an asymmetric tunnel junction. The device is based on an asymmetric superconductor-insulator-superconductor (SIS) junction with an energy-gap ratio of $Δ_1/Δ_2 = 0.5$, connected in series with a load resistor. Owing to the superconducting bipolar thermoelectric effect, the current-voltage characteristic of the junction exhibits a region of NDR, in which the net current flows opposite to the applied voltage. This mechanism enables voltage amplification in the absence of any external electrical bias, relying solely on the temperature difference between the electrodes ($T_H \simeq 1$ K, $T_B \simeq 20$ mK). Numerical simulations predict a voltage gain of 20 dB, a 1 dB compression point at an input amplitude of 2 $μ$V, and a total harmonic distortion below $-50$ dB. The input-referred noise is approximately 1 nV/$\sqrt{Hz}$, with an associated thermal load on the order of nanowatts. The frequency response is broadband from near DC, with a $-3$ dB cutoff around 180 MHz, set by the RC time constant of the junction. Using Al-, Al-Cu-, and AlO$_x$-based technologies, the amplifier is compatible with conventional superconducting circuit fabrication processes. These findings demonstrate that thermoelectric superconducting junctions can deliver bias-free voltage amplification from near DC up to about 200 MHz, making them promising candidates for transition-edge sensor readout, quantum circuit instrumentation, and low-frequency cryogenic signal processing.

</details>


### [81] [Magnetic flux distribution, quasiparticle spectroscopy, and quality factors in Nb films for superconducting qubits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23402)
*Amlan Datta,Bicky S. Moirangthem,Kamal R. Joshi,Anthony P. Mcfadden,Florent Lecocq,Raymond W. Simmonds,Makariy A. Tanatar,Matthew J. Kramer,Ruslan Prozorov*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究比较了不同沉积温度下生长的铌（Nb）超导薄膜，通过磁光成像和伦敦穿透深度测量，建立了材料内部品质因子与磁通分布、准粒子光谱特性的关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铌（Niobium）是超导微波电路的实际材料平台，但器件性能受薄膜生长和处理条件影响显著。研究旨在理解不同沉积温度如何影响薄膜的超导特性，特别是内部品质因子（internal quality factor, Q_i）的变化机制。

Method: 研究比较了在c面蓝宝石（c-plane sapphire）衬底上生长的三种外延铌薄膜，沉积条件除温度外均相同。采用磁光成像（magneto-optical imaging）分析磁通分布，结合通过伦敦穿透深度（London penetration depth, λ(T)）测量进行的准粒子光谱（quasiparticle spectroscopy）分析。

Result: 低Q_i薄膜表现出较弱的磁场屏蔽能力和不规则的λ(T)温度变化，表明存在局域带隙内态（localized in-gap states）。高Q_i薄膜则呈现相反趋势，具有更好的磁场屏蔽和更规则的λ(T)行为。

Conclusion: 该测量方法为表征和优化用于量子信息学（quantum informatics）应用的超导薄膜提供了有效手段，能够将材料特性与器件性能直接关联。

Abstract: Niobium is a practical material platform for superconducting microwave circuits; however, device-level performance can vary significantly depending on film growth and processing conditions. We compare three epitaxial Nb films grown on $c-$plane sapphire substrates under nominally identical conditions, except for the deposition temperature. To correlate internal quality factors, $Q_{\mathrm {i}}$, with material properties, we combine magneto-optical imaging of magnetic flux distribution with quasiparticle spectroscopy via measurements of the London penetration depth, $λ(T)$. In the low-$Q_{\mathrm i}$ film, there is a lesser ability to screen the magnetic field and an irregular temperature variation of $λ(T)$, implying the existence of localized in-gap states. High $Q_{\mathrm i}$ films show the opposite trend. We conclude that our measurements provide an efficient method for characterizing and optimizing superconducting films for quantum informatics applications.

</details>

### [82] [Unified Algebraic Absorption of Finite-Blocklength Penalties via Generalized Logarithmic Mapping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22358)
*Hiroki Suyari*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于q-代数框架的有限码长信息论新方法，通过动态缩放参数吸收高阶矩修正，避免了传统高斯近似和Edgeworth展开中的外部误差项。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统有限码长信息论中评估信道编码基本极限通常依赖正态近似和Edgeworth展开，这些方法通过添加多项式修正来处理偏度和高阶矩。本文旨在提供一种替代方法，避免向高斯基线添加外部误差项。

Method: 提出基于广义q-代数框架的方法，引入动态缩放律 $1-q_n = αn^{-1}$ 作为调谐参数。通过设置缩放常数 $α= T/(3V^2)$（其中V是变熵，T是第三中心矩），该框架能够恢复三阶编码极限。

Result: 证明q-广义信息密度对应宏观高阶涨落，能够吸收O(1)非高斯惩罚而无需依赖Hermite多项式。同时展示代数展开的k次项匹配(k+1)阶矩Edgeworth修正的O(n^{1-k/2})渐近阶。

Conclusion: 该方法在单一代数结构内统一了经典概率近似，建立了有限码长分析与广义对数映射之间的数学联系，为信道编码极限评估提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: In finite-blocklength information theory, evaluating the fundamental limits of channel coding typically relies on normal approximations and Edgeworth expansions, which introduce additive polynomial corrections for skewness and higher-order moments. This paper proposes an alternative approach: rather than appending external error terms to a Gaussian baseline, we absorb these finite-length penalties using a generalized $q$-algebraic framework. By introducing a dynamic scaling law $1-q_n = αn^{-1}$ for the tuning parameter, we prove that the $q$-generalized information density corresponds to macroscopic higher-order fluctuations. Specifically, by setting this scaling constant to $α= T/(3V^2)$ (where $V$ is the varentropy and $T$ is the third central moment), our framework recovers the third-order coding limit, absorbing the $O(1)$ non-Gaussian penalty without relying on Hermite polynomials. Furthermore, we demonstrate that the $k$-th degree term of our algebraic expansion matches the $O(n^{1-k/2})$ asymptotic order of the $(k+1)$-th moment Edgeworth correction. This approach unifies classical probabilistic approximations within a single algebraic structure, establishing a mathematical connection between finite-blocklength analysis and generalized logarithmic mappings.

</details>

Result: 50升原型机LIME已成功在LNGS地下实验室运行，展示了在三维事件重建、详细能量沉积映射以及有效拓扑和头尾辨别方面的进展。下一步将部署0.4立方米的演示器CYGNO-04，计划于2026年完成。

Conclusion: CYGNO-04演示器将验证该技术的可扩展性并确认其优势，推动暗物质探测项目的发展。近期LIME的结果显示了在三维追踪和粒子识别方面的显著进展。

Abstract: The CYGNO collaboration is developing a novel strategy for directional Dark Matter searches based on a gaseous Time Projection Chamber (TPC). The detector is optimized for the exploration of light (0.5-50 GeV) WIMPs-like particles and employs a He/CF4 gas mixture at atmospheric pressure, sensitive to both spin-dependent and spin-independent interactions. A key feature of the project is its optical readout, which relies on photon detection rather than charge collection. In CYGNO detectors, electrons released by ionizing tracks drift toward an amplification stage of three Gas Electron Multipliers (GEMs). The electron avalanches generate scintillation light that is captured by scientific CMOS (sCMOS) cameras for high-resolution two-dimensional imaging and by Photomultiplier Tubes (PMTs) that provide a precise time profile along the drift direction. This allows a 3D event reconstruction, detailed energy deposition mapping, and effective topology and head-to-tail discrimination. Building on the achievements of the 50 L prototype (LIME), which successfully operated underground at LNGS, the next step is the deployment of a 0.4 m3 demonstrator, CYGNO-04, to be completed in 2026. The demonstrator will validate scalability and confirm the advantages of the proposed technique. Recent results from LIME highlight strong progress in 3D tracking and particle identification. The current status of CYGNO-04 and its role in advancing the program will be presented as well.

### [84] [Cotunneling theory and multiplet excitations: emergence of asymmetric line shape in inelastic scanning tunneling spectroscopy of correlated molecules on surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22505)
*Marco Lozano,Manish Kumar,Pavel Jelinek,Diego Soler-Polo*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扫描隧道谱（STS）实验中经常观察到费米能级附近的不对称峰谷特征，而传统共隧穿理论和有效模型哈密顿量（如Hubbard模型和自旋模型）主要解释对称的阶跃状特征。需要扩展理论框架来解释这些不对称线形。

Method: 将共隧穿形式体系（cotunneling formalism）扩展至一般的多参考态系统（multireference systems），考虑轨道依赖性和强烈不对称的针尖/基底耦合。

Result: 研究表明，多参考态特性结合轨道依赖性和强烈不对称的耦合，能够在非弹性扫描隧道谱（inelastic STS）中产生显著的不对称线形。这为实验中观察到的费米能级附近不对称峰谷提供了替代的微观机制。

Conclusion: 该工作扩展了共隧穿理论框架，揭示了多参考态系统和不对称耦合在扫描隧道谱线形形成中的关键作用，为表面分子磁激发谱的解释提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: Recent advances in on-surface chemistry, combined with scanning probe microscopy, have enabled the synthesis of correlated molecules on surfaces and the characterization of their chemical and electronic properties with unprecedented spatial resolution. Low-energy magnetic excitations of individual molecules are frequently investigated by scanning tunneling spectroscopy (STS) and often appear as symmetric step-like features in the differential conductance as a function of bias voltage. The interpretation of such steps is well established within cotunneling theory and effective model Hamiltonians (e.g., Hubbard- and spin-based models). Here, we extend the cotunneling formalism to general multireference systems. We show that multireference character, together with orbital-dependent and strongly asymmetric tip/substrate couplings, can produce pronounced asymmetric line shapes in inelastic STS. These results provide an alternative microscopic mechanism for the asymmetric peaks and dips near the Fermi level frequently observed in STS experiments.

### [85] [Exploring Spectral Singularities in Dirac Semimetals: The Role of Non-Hermitian Physics and Dichroism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23001)
*Mustafa Sarisaman,Murat Taş,Enes Talha Kırca*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究基于非厄米物理（non-Hermitian physics）进展，通过散射技术利用谱奇点（spectral singularities）探索狄拉克半金属（Dirac semimetals）新特性，首次发现二向色性狄拉克半金属可产生12种独特拓扑激光类型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于非厄米物理领域的最新进展，旨在通过散射技术和谱奇点探索狄拉克半金属的新特性，揭示其额外独特性质。特别关注轴子纹理（axion texture）如何影响拓扑性质及其与电磁波的相互作用。

Method: 采用散射技术分析谱奇点，研究狄拉克半金属中轴子纹理对拓扑性质的影响。重点考察横向电模式（transverse electric mode）配置，其中磁电效应（magneto-electric effect）诱导材料的二向色性（dichroic property）。

Result: 首次报道二向色性狄拉克半金属可产生12种独特的拓扑激光类型。发现狄拉克半金属板表面由拓扑项产生表面电流，并揭示θ项（θ term）在拓扑性质中的独特作用比以往更清晰。确认单狄拉克锥狄拉克半金属的拓扑性质在外部影响下保持稳定。

Conclusion: 研究证实具有单狄拉克锥的狄拉克半金属拓扑性质在外部影响下保持稳定，据此可开发拓扑鲁棒的狄拉克半金属激光器。轴子相关的θ项在拓扑性质中发挥独特作用，为拓扑材料研究提供新见解。

Abstract: In this study, motivated by recent advancements in non-Hermitian physics, we explore new characteristics of Dirac semimetals (DSMs) using the spectral singularities by means of scattering techniques, with the goal of uncovering additional unique properties. To achieve this, we investigate how the axion texture of a DSM affects its topological properties by analyzing its interaction with electromagnetic waves. We examine the transverse electric (TE) mode configuration, where the magneto-electric effect induces a dichroic property in these materials. This behavior is particularly interesting and commonly seen in potential DSM candidates. Consequently, we report for the first time that a dichroic DSM generates 12 unique topological laser types. We discover that surface currents are generated by topological terms on the surface of the DSM slab. Furthermore, we examine how the θ term associated with axions in topological materials contributes to these topological properties. Our study reveals distinct topological role of the θ term more clearly than ever before. Our results confirm that the topological properties of DSMs with a single Dirac cone remain stable under external influences and that a topologically robust DSM laser can be developed accordingly

### [86] [Magnetic Weyl semimetals: Interplay of band topology and magnetism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22568)
*Akihiro Ozawa,Yasufumi Araki,Koji Kobayashi,Kentaro Nomura*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在系统回顾磁性外尔半金属领域的最新进展，重点关注其电子能带拓扑与磁性之间的相互作用。这种拓扑性质不仅对基础物理研究具有重要意义，也为开发低耗散电子学和自旋电子学器件提供了潜在应用前景。

Method: 本文采用综述性研究方法，首先介绍外尔半金属中电子的基本拓扑性质，然后系统梳理磁性外尔半金属的各种现象。方法包括理论分析、材料分类、机制探讨以及介观尺度计算研究。

Result: 综述涵盖了磁性外尔半金属的多种现象：包括异常霍尔效应（anomalous Hall effect）、手征磁效应（chiral magnetic effect）、非均匀磁织构与磁化动力学导致的拓扑相互作用（表现为自旋动力力和自旋力矩），以及磁输运现象如畴壁磁阻（domain wall magnetoresistance）。

Conclusion: 外尔电子的拓扑性质在磁性外尔半金属中展现出丰富的物理现象，这些现象不仅对基础物理研究至关重要，也为开发低耗散电子学和自旋电子学器件提供了重要的理论基础和应用潜力。

Abstract: We review recent theoretical and experimental developments in magnetic Weyl semimetals, focusing on the electromagnetic responses emerging from the interplay of their electronic band topology and magnetism. We begin by introducing the fundamental topological properties of the electrons in Weyl semimetals, and provide an overview of the characteristic phenomena arising from their band topology, such as the anomalous Hall effect and chiral magnetic effect. The materials exhibiting the magnetic Weyl semimetal state, with ferromagnetic ordering, antiferromagnetic ordering, etc., are listed. The possible mechanisms for their magnetism are discussed in connection with the Weyl electrons. Non-uniform magnetic textures and magnetization dynamics are expected to exhibit a topological interplay with the Weyl electrons, manifesting as spinmotive force and spin torques. We also review the magnetotransport phenomena such as domain wall magnetoresistance, studied by mesoscopic scale calculations. Finally, we mention the spin transport properties studied in magnetic Weyl semimetals. The topological nature of Weyl electrons reviewed here is important not only for fundamental physics, but also for the potential application to low-dissipative electronics and spintronics devices.

</details>


### [87] [Two-dimensional bound excitons in the real space and Landau quantization space: a comparative study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22715)
*Kunxiang Li,Yi-Xiang Wang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 朗道量子化空间基于电子和空穴在磁场中的相对运动，为理解实验中观测到的束缚激子行为提供了新途径。本研究旨在通过该空间分析单层WSe₂的二维激子特性。

Method: 在实空间和朗道量子化空间同时研究单层WSe₂的二维激子性质，聚焦于零质心动量激子，计算其能谱。通过对比两种空间的结果，获得抗磁系数和均方根半径等参数。

Result: 两种空间计算的能谱结果吻合良好，抗磁系数和均方根半径与实验观测的s态结果一致。研究发现激子态nl中主导电子-空穴对成分受磁场和库仑相互作用调控：磁场驱动主导成分向自由电子-空穴对{n_e=n+l-1, n_h=n-1}转变，而库仑相互作用则驱动其向低指数对转变。

Conclusion: 朗道量子化空间为理解二维激子行为提供了有效框架，磁场和库仑相互作用对激子内部电子-空穴对成分的竞争调控机制得以揭示，这有助于解释实验观测到的激子行为。

Abstract: The Landau quantization space is based on the respective motion of the electron and hole in a magnetic field and can provide a new route to understand the bound exciton behaviors observed in the experiments. In this paper, we study the two-dimensional exciton properties of monolayer WSe$_2$ in both the real space and Landau quantization space. Focusing on the excitons of zero center-of-mass momentum, we calculate its energy spectrum in both spaces, with the results agreeing well with each other. We then obtain the diamagnetic coefficients and root-mean-square radius, which are consistent with the $s$ state results from the experiments. More importantly, in the exciton state $nl$, we find that the dominant electron-hole pair component may shift with the magnetic field and the Coulomb interactions, and reveal that the magnetic field will drive the dominant component to be the free electron-hole pair $\{n_e=n+l-1,n_h=n-1\}$, whereas the Coulomb interactions drives it to be the pair of the lower index.

### [88] [Electron scattering by a magnetic monopole in solid-state experiments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22865)
*P. S. Sidorov,N. A. Vlasov,I. S. Terekhov,A. I. Milstein*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用eikonal近似（eikonal approximation）方法计算微分散射截面（differential scattering cross section），并分析在类似霍尔实验（Hall experiment）的实验装置中的电子行为。

Conclusion: 该研究证实了在二维电子气中磁单极场会导致电子散射产生自旋极化现象，为实验观测这一效应提供了理论框架和方案设计。

Abstract: The scheme of experiment for studying electron scattering in the field of a magnetic monopole in two dimensional electron gas is proposed. For unpolarized initial electron, the differential cross section coincides with that in the field of an infinitely long solenoid, up to redefinition of a magnetic flux. It is shown that the scattered electron becomes polarized even for unpolarized initial electron. Besides, in an experimental setup similar to the Hall experiment, the spin polarization arises in the direction perpendicular to the electron current.

### [89] [Solitary waves in a phononic integrated circuit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22898)
*Timothy M. F. Hirsch,Xiaoya Jin,Nicolas P. Mauranyapin,Nishta Arora,Erick Romero,Matthew Reeves,Glen I. Harris,Warwick P. Bowen,Christopher G. Baker*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过集成声子波导产生声学孤子，实现了对暗孤子（dark solitons）动力学的精确观测，包括数百次孤子碰撞、孤子裂变和孤子维格纳晶体熔化等强非线性现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 孤子（solitons）作为普遍存在的非线性激发，在光学、水波和量子气体等多个领域均有出现。然而，在强非线性且频繁相互作用的体系中，现有简化模型的适用性及其动力学行为仍缺乏实验验证，主要受限于难以同时精确调控色散和非线性，以及获得足够时空分辨率的观测能力。

Method: 研究采用集成声子波导（integrated phononic waveguides）产生声学孤子。该方法利用波导色散（waveguide dispersion）与机械克尔非线性（mechanical Kerr nonlinearity）之间的相互作用，生成了能够在米级传播距离上稳定存在的暗孤子。

Result: 实验成功观测到数百次暗孤子碰撞（数量级比以往研究高出两个数量级）、孤子裂变（soliton fission）以及孤子维格纳晶体（soliton Wigner crystal）的熔化过程。前所未有的动力学分辨率证实了暗孤子行为的两个长期预测：碰撞相移（collisional phase shift）的存在，以及两种依赖于孤子深度的碰撞机制。

Conclusion: 该研究不仅揭示了非线性能量传输的基本过程，还为开发基于声学孤子的技术（如频率梳和锁模激光器的声学版本）指明了方向。

Abstract: Solitons are universal nonlinear excitations that appear in settings as varied as optics, water waves, and quantum gases [1-5]. While reduced models of soliton dynamics are well established, their validity and dynamical behaviour in strongly nonlinear regimes with frequent interactions remain largely unexplored experimentally. Progress has been constrained by the difficulty of simultaneously achieving precise control of dispersion and nonlinearity, together with the temporal and spatial resolution required for dynamical observations. Here we overcome these difficulties by producing acoustic solitons in integrated phononic waveguides. We exploit the interplay between waveguide dispersion and mechanical Kerr nonlinearity to generate 'dark' solitons that persist over metre-scale propagation distances. The slow phonon velocity allows direct imaging of hundreds of dark soliton collisions -- two orders of magnitude more than have previously been accessible [6, 7] -- as well as soliton fission and the melting of a soliton Wigner crystal. Furthermore, the unprecedented dynamical resolution allows us to verify two long-predicted aspects of dark soliton behaviour: the existence of a collisional phase shift and two depth-dependent collision regimes [8, 9]. These results not only illuminate fundamental nonlinear energy transport processes, but also show a path towards acoustic versions of soliton-enabled technologies such as frequency combs and mode-locked lasers [1, 2, 10].

</details>

Method: 采用严格的自洽数值方法，迭代求解耦合的薛定谔-泊松方程（Schrödinger-Poisson equations），获得不同外部偏压下的精确波函数、能级和势能分布。使用非对称厄朗分布（asymmetric Erlang distribution）来表征界面效应，并全面建模电荷密度和静电势分布。

Abstract: In this study, we investigate the electronic structure, charge transport dynamics, and optical properties of a quantum dot light-emitting diode (QD-LED) featuring a double nanorod (NR) emission layer composed of CdSe-ZnS core-shell structures. Utilizing a rigorous self-consistent numerical approach, we solve the coupled Schrodinger-Poisson equations iteratively to obtain accurate wave functions, energy levels, and potential profiles under varying external bias voltages. Detailed analyses reveal voltage-dependent electron localization dynamics, demonstrating a systematic transition of electrons between distinct NR regions via quantum tunneling. Charge density and electrostatic potential distributions are modeled comprehensively, employing the asymmetric Erlang distribution to characterize interface effects. By calculating current-voltage (I-V) characteristics and photoluminescence spectra, we demonstrate that external voltage serves as a robust tuning parameter for modulating emission energies and intensities, underscoring the potential of these NR-LED systems for tunable optoelectronic and photonic applications.

### [91] [Quantum correlations and dissipative blockade of polaritons in a tunable fiber cavity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23002)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索腔激子极化激元（cavity exciton-polaritons）的量子关联特性，特别是极化激元相互作用如何受腔-激子失谐（cavity-exciton detuning）影响，这对于实现强极化激元阻塞（polariton blockade）机制至关重要。

Method: 采用连续波共振激光激发下的光子关联测量（photon correlation measurements），通过调节激光频率跨越极化激元共振，并分析不同腔-激子失谐条件下的关联特性。

Result: 实验发现极化激元相互作用对腔-激子失谐具有强烈依赖性：在激子主导区域，观察到从光子反聚束（photon antibunching）到聚束（bunching）的转变；在双激子模式（biexciton mode）诱导的双极化激元费什巴赫共振（two-polariton Feshbach resonance）条件下，反聚束程度与激光失谐无关，这归因于大双激子展宽引起的耗散阻塞机制（dissipative blockade mechanism）。

Conclusion: 研究表明，通过将极化激元衰减率降低10倍，可以实现强极化激元阻塞（strong polariton blockade）机制，这为量子信息处理中的极化激元应用提供了重要指导。

Abstract: Cavity exciton--polaritons are quasiparticles that form when quantum well excitons hybridize with a cavity mode. Here, we carry out photon correlation measurements under continuous wave resonant laser excitation to demonstrate quantum correlations between cavity--polaritons. Our experiments reveal an unexpectedly strong dependence of polariton interactions on cavity--exciton detuning. When the polaritons are predominantly exciton-like, we observe a transition from photon antibunching to bunching as the laser is tuned across the polariton resonance, in agreement with a simple Kerr-nonlinearity model. When the lower-branch polariton energy is tuned to induce a two-polariton Feshbach resonance with the biexciton mode, the degree of polariton antibunching becomes independent of the laser detuning: we explain our finding by invoking a dissipative blockade mechanism arising from large biexciton broadening. Our experiments demonstrate that the strong polariton blockade regime would be achieved by reducing the polariton decay rate by a factor of 10.

In WTe2- and Bi1.5Sb0.5Te1.7Se1.3-based Josephson junctions, this architecture yields systematically larger I_c R_N and longer-ranged coupling than conventional top contacts. Abstract: Moiré superlattices have emerged as a premier platform for simulating the Hubbard model, yet achieving high tunability in square-lattice systems remains a key challenge. We demonstrate that $Γ$-valley twisted square homobilayers provide a faithful and highly tunable realization of $t-t'-U$ Hubbard model, extending the recent proposal in M-valley systems. We show that at small twist angles, an emergent layer-exchange symmetry decouples electronic states into flat bands residing on two nested square sublattices. An interlayer displacement field breaks this symmetry to induce controllable inter-sublattice hybridization, enabling wide-range experimental tuning of the effective hopping ratio $t'/t$. By establishing a direct correspondence between $Γ$- and M-valley systems, we provide a unified framework for understanding displacement-field tunability in square moiré physics. These findings establish $Γ$-valley twisted bilayers as a versatile platform for simulating the square-lattice Hubbard model and exploring its rich landscape of correlated phenomena.

### [94] [Enhanced spin-current generation in Dirac altermagnets through Klein tunneling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23235)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用低能狄拉克模型（low-energy Dirac model）结合散射理论（scattering theory），分析克莱因隧穿在交变磁体中的自旋依赖性。通过调整势垒高度、宽度和方向等参数，研究对电子自旋电流极化的控制机制。

Result: 交变磁体中的克莱因隧穿具有强自旋依赖性，可通过势垒参数有效控制自旋电流极化。特别地，g波狄拉克交变磁体在势垒存在时能显著提升自旋电流极化，即使本征极化极小。通过静电门控（electrostatic gating）实现势垒，可通过栅极电压开关自旋电流极化。

Conclusion: 克莱因隧穿是增强狄拉克交变磁体自旋输运的有效机制，其自旋依赖性为自旋电流极化控制提供了新途径。g波对称性狄拉克交变磁体结合势垒调控，为实现栅压可调的自旋电流开关提供了有前景的方案。

Abstract: Altermagnets have recently emerged as a new platform for spintronics applications, offering spin-split electronic bands despite vanishing net magnetization. Here, we investigate spin-current generation in Dirac altermagnets and identify Klein tunneling as an efficient mechanism for enhancing spin transport. Using a low-energy Dirac model combined with scattering theory, we demonstrate that Klein tunneling in altermagnets is strongly spin-dependent and can be used to effectively control the electronic spin-current polarization by, for instance, adjusting the height, width and orientation of the potential barrier. Finally, we explore how the l-wave symmetry of the Dirac altermagnet shapes the spin-current polarization and transmission, focusing especially on the d- and g-wave cases. Particularly promising results are obtained for the g-wave Dirac altermagnet, as it is found that the presence of a potential barrier can significantly boost the spin-current polarization, even when the intrinsic polarization due to the spin-split band structure is vanishingly small. For a barrier implemented via electrostatic gating, such a mechanism would in turn allow the spin-current polarization to be switched on and off via a gate voltage.

Abstract: We investigate the Goos--Hänchen (GH) shifts and group delay time of Dirac fermions traversing a rectangular electrostatic potential barrier in silicene. By analyzing their dependence on the incident angle, barrier height, barrier width, and incident energy, we demonstrate that the GH shifts exhibit pronounced oscillations arising from quantum interference within the barrier region. The amplitude and number of oscillation peaks increase with increasing energy, barrier width, and incidence angle, resulting in enhanced lateral beam displacement. Meanwhile, the group delay time exhibits resonant features associated with the formation of quasi-bound states, increasing with barrier width, energy, and incidence angle, while decreasing with increasing barrier height. These results clarify how barrier-induced quantum interference controls both the lateral and temporal dynamics of Dirac fermions in silicene, highlighting the potential role of electrostatic barriers in enabling tunable transport in two-dimensional Dirac materials.
