Conclusion: 埋入式应力层概念为高度相干、位置可控的O波段量子发射器提供了一条可扩展路径，兼容工业光子集成。理论支持的多应力层策略可进一步将发射红移至O波段中心及更远波长。

Abstract: The deterministic realization of quantum light sources operating at telecom wavelengths is essential for long-distance fiber-based quantum communication and distributed quantum computing. In this work, we demonstrate that telecom O-band emission can be achieved from site-controlled InGaAs/GaAs quantum dots (QDs). Our concept utilizes a buried AlAs/Al$_2$O$_3$ stressor layer with the unique feature that induces a well-defined and controllable tensile strain field at the growth surface, enabling both a redshift of QD emission to the $\sim$1.3~μm range and site-selective nucleation at the mesa centers. This concept eliminates not only the need for strain-reducing layers (SRLs), which are known to degrade optical coherence, but also provides spatial control and spectral tunability. The grown telecom QDs show pure single-photon emission with $g^{(2)}(τ) = (5.0 \pm 1.0) \times 10^{-2}$ at 4 K and $(2.8 \pm 0.3) \times 10^{-1}$ at 77~K, demonstrating the quantum nature and thermal stability of the emitters. The emission characteristics of complex excitonic states are analyzed using 8-band $k \cdot p$ and configuration-interaction modeling, which quantitatively reproduces the experimental observations. Finally, we present a theory-supported strategy to further redshift the emission toward the center of the O-band and beyond by employing a multi-buried-stressor approach. This combined framework of experiment and theory establishes the buried stressor concept as a scalable route toward highly coherent, position-controlled O-band quantum emitters compatible with industrial photonic integration.

</details>

### [98] [Geometric Quantum Mechanics in a Symplectic Framework: Metric-Affine Extensions and Deformed Quantum Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22354)
*Hoshang Heydari*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于射影希尔伯特空间的辛结构，提出了量子力学的几何表述扩展，通过引入与度量-仿射背景几何耦合的辛结构，实现了量子态空间上哈密顿流的形变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在扩展标准Kähler框架，探索量子力学在度量-仿射背景几何下的几何表述，研究背景曲率和仿射结构如何诱导量子演化的几何修正。

Method: 基于射影希尔伯特空间（projective Hilbert space）的辛结构，引入与度量-仿射背景几何（metric-affine background geometry）耦合的扩展框架，导致态空间上哈密顿流的形变（deformation）。

Result: 在适当条件下，形变后的结构保持辛特性并定义良定的哈密顿系统；曲率依赖的形变导致哈密顿流重新标度，而挠率诱导的贡献产生方向依赖的修正；几何相位获得由形变辛结构决定的修正。

Conclusion: 该框架为探索由背景曲率和仿射结构诱导的量子演化几何修正提供了数学一致的基础，当几何形变消失时，该表述约化为标准薛定谔动力学。

Abstract: We present a geometric formulation of quantum mechanics based on the symplectic structure of the projective Hilbert space. Building upon the standard Kähler framework, we introduce an extension in which the symplectic structure is allowed to couple to a metric-affine background geometry, leading to a deformation of the Hamiltonian flow on the state space.
  We show that, under suitable conditions, the deformed structure remains symplectic and defines a well-posed Hamiltonian system. The formulation reduces to standard Schrödinger dynamics in the limit where the geometric deformation vanishes.
  Explicit analytical examples are constructed to illustrate the effect of the deformation. In particular, curvature-dependent deformations lead to a rescaling of Hamiltonian flows, while torsion-induced contributions produce direction-dependent corrections. In addition, geometric phases acquire corrections determined by the deformed symplectic structure.
  These results provide a mathematically consistent framework for exploring geometric modifications of quantum evolution induced by background curvature and affine structure.

</details>


### [99] [Single-letter one-way distillable entanglement for non-degradable states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23417)
*Rabsan Galib Ahmed,Graeme Smith,Peixue Wu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对单向量子纠缠蒸馏（one-way distillable entanglement）的计算难题，识别了三类非退化（non-degradable）且非PPT（non-PPT）的量子态，其单向量子纠缠蒸馏仍具有单字母公式（single-letter formula）。通过引入弱化的退化型条件、正交标记混合的稳定性结果以及广义自旋对齐原理，解决了在退化性和PPT条件之外的可加性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单向量子纠缠蒸馏（one-way distillable entanglement）是量子纠缠的核心操作度量，但因其定义涉及多副本正则化优化和自适应单向量子协议（adaptive one-way protocols），计算极为困难。目前仅对（共轭）退化态（degradable states）和PPT态有单字母公式，而在退化性和PPT条件之外的可加性问题仍不明确。

Method: 首先引入两种弱化的退化型条件：正则化更少噪声（regularized less-noisy）和信息可退化（informationally degradable），证明它们保证可加性。其次展示正交标记混合（orthogonally flagged mixtures）的稳定性结果：当某分量在Alice系统上具有正交支撑且零单向量子纠缠蒸馏时，混合态仍保持单字母公式。最后提出张量积设置中熵最小化的广义自旋对齐原理（generalized spin-alignment principle）。

Result: 识别了三类非退化且非PPT量子态，其单向量子纠缠蒸馏仍具有单字母公式。建立了广义自旋对齐原理在多个关键情况下的有效性，包括完整的Rényi-2结果。作为应用，获得了广义直和信道（generalized direct-sum channels）及其对应Choi态的可加性结果。

Conclusion: 本文填补了单向量子纠缠蒸馏可加性研究的空白，超越了传统的退化性和PPT条件限制。通过引入新的结构条件和原理，为更广泛量子态的单字母公式计算提供了理论框架，并建立了与量子信道容量可加性问题的联系。

Abstract: The one-way distillable entanglement is a central operational measure of bipartite entanglement, quantifying the optimal rate at which maximally entangled pairs can be extracted by one-way LOCC. Despite its importance, it is notoriously hard to compute, since it is defined by a regularized optimization over many copies and adaptive one-way protocols. At present, single-letter formulas are only known for (conjugate) degradable and PPT states. More generally, it has remained unclear when one-way distillable entanglement can still be additive beyond degradability and PPT settings, and how such additivity relates to additivity questions of quantum capacity of channels.
  In this paper, we address this gap by identifying three explicit families of non-degradable and non-PPT states whose one-way distillable entanglement is nevertheless single-letter. First, we introduce two weakened degradability-type conditions--regularized less-noisy and informationally degradable--and prove that each guarantees additivity and hence a single-letter formula. Second, we show a stability result for orthogonally flagged mixtures: when one component has orthogonal support on Alice's system and zero one-way distillable entanglement, the mixture remains single-letter, even though degradability is typically lost under such mixing. Finally, we propose a generalized spin-alignment principle for entropy minimization in tensor-product settings, which we establish in several key cases, including a complete Rényi-2 result. As an application, we obtain additivity results for generalized direct-sum channels and their corresponding Choi states.

</details>


### [100] [Initial State Memory in Finite Random Brickwork Circuits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23469)
*Jakob Bannister,Katja Klobas,Colin Rylands,Bruno Bertini*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨有限砖墙结构随机门电路在何种条件下能保留初始状态的局部信息，发现信息保留与否取决于被追踪子系统（环境）的大小是否小于系统的一半，并观察到在引入边界耗散时存在记忆保持相和信息完全丢失相之间的相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是探究有限砖墙结构（brickwork）随机门电路在何种条件下能够保留关于初始状态的局部信息，这对于理解量子信息在随机电路中的动力学行为具有重要意义。

Method: 通过测量两个任意初始状态演化后经部分系统追踪得到的约化态之间的平均弗罗贝尼乌斯距离（averaged Frobenius distance），并在所有时间点上精确表征这一距离。

Result: 研究发现信息保留与否取决于环境（被追踪子系统）的大小：当环境小于系统一半时信息得以保留，否则信息被完全洗去。弗罗贝尼乌斯距离的动力学依赖于具体初始状态，但该依赖性在大尺度下逐渐减弱，最终距离随时间呈现普适形式。

Conclusion: 通过引入足够弱的边界耗散（boundary dissipation），可以观察到记忆保持相（memory preserving phase）和信息完全丢失相之间的相变（phase transition），揭示了随机电路中信息保留的临界行为。

Abstract: We ask under what conditions a finite brickwork circuit of random gates retains local information about the initial state. To answer this question we measure the averaged Frobenius distance between the reduced states obtained by evolving two arbitrary initial states and tracing out a portion of the system. By characterising this distance exactly at all times we find that the information is retained if the environment -- the subsystem traced out -- is smaller than half of the system and washed away otherwise. We also find that, while the dynamics of the Frobenius distance depends on the specific initial states chosen, this dependence becomes increasingly weak for large scales and eventually the Frobenius distance attains a universal form as a function of time. Finally, we show that by introducing weak enough boundary dissipation, one can observe a phase transition between a memory preserving phase and one where the information is completely lost.

</details>


### [101] [Boundary Floquet Control of Bulk non-Hermitian Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22396)
*Yu-Min Hu,Yu-Bo Shi,Linhu Li,Gianluca Teza,Ching Hua Lee,Roderich Moessner,Shu Zhang,Sen Mu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文发展了一个关于边界驱动非厄米系统的一般理论，将非布洛赫能带理论扩展到时间周期系统，揭示了边界驱动频率对体谱和动力学的控制作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非厄米系统（non-Hermitian systems）为超越厄米框架的非平衡现象工程提供了强大平台，非厄米趋肤效应（non-Hermitian skin effect）进一步扩展了动力学控制的范围。然而，边界驱动对非厄米系统体性质的影响尚缺乏统一理论描述。

Method: 论文发展了一个关于边界驱动非厄米系统的一般理论，将非布洛赫能带理论（non-Bloch band theory）扩展到时间周期系统。该框架在热力学极限下提供了边界驱动频率依赖的体谱和动力学的统一描述。

Result: 在代表性模型中，研究展示了边界驱动诱导的宇称-时间对称性破缺（parity-time symmetry breaking）。驱动频率作为控制旋钮，而在有限尺寸系统中，驱动幅度提供了额外的调控手段。

Conclusion: 边界弗洛凯驱动（boundary Floquet driving）被确立为控制非厄米系统体性质的多功能机制，为驱动开放系统中的动力学工程开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Non-Hermitian systems provide a powerful platform for engineering and controlling nonequilibrium phenomena beyond Hermitian settings, with the presence of non-Hermitian skin effect broadening the scope of dynamical control. Here, we develop a general theory of non-Hermitian systems driven exclusively at their boundaries, providing a unified description of the driving-frequency dependence of bulk spectra and dynamics in the thermodynamic limit. Our framework extends non-Bloch band theory to time-periodic systems at arbitrary boundary driving frequencies. Applying it to representative models, we demonstrate boundary-driving-induced parity-time symmetry breaking, with the driving frequency serving as a control knob and the driving amplitude providing an additional handle in finite-size systems. These results establish boundary Floquet driving as a versatile mechanism for controlling bulk properties of non-Hermitian systems and open new routes for dynamical engineering in driven open systems.

</details>


### [102] [Dicke materials as a resource for quantum squeezing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22416)
*Vaibhav Sharma,Shung-An Koh,Jonathan Stepp,Dasom Kim,Takumu Obata,Yuki Saito,Motoaki Bamba,Han Pu,Hanyu Zhu,Junichiro Kono,Kaden R. A. Hazzard*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究提出"狄克材料（Dicke materials）"概念，探讨了这类材料中基态压缩（ground state squeezing）对常见缺陷（如有限温度、无序和局域相互作用）的鲁棒性，为固态系统中的量子计量学和纠缠见证提供了理论支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于在狄克材料中观测压缩（squeezing）的前景，这种压缩可作为固态系统中量子计量学和纠缠见证的资源。然而，作为纠缠度量，压缩对通常与相关函数和序参数无关的扰动可能很敏感。

Method: 采用解析和数值技术，研究基态压缩在普遍存在的缺陷（如有限温度、无序和局域相互作用）下的鲁棒性。通过分析狄克模型在这些材料中的涌现机制，探讨了快色散和慢色散自旋强耦合共存的特征。

Result: 研究表明，获得的压缩对这些缺陷具有微扰稳定性（perturbatively stable），并定量评估了有希望进行实验观测的体系。狄克材料在超辐射相变（superradiant phase transition）附近预期表现出压缩基态。

Conclusion: 狄克材料中的基态压缩对常见缺陷具有鲁棒性，为实验观测提供了可行性。这类材料可作为固态系统中量子计量学和纠缠见证的资源，其压缩特性在超辐射相变附近尤为显著。

Abstract: We study magnetic materials whose low energy physics can be effectively described by a Dicke model, which we term Dicke materials. We show how a Dicke model emerges in such materials due to a coexistence of fast-dispersing and slow-dispersing spins, which are strongly coupled. Analogous to the paradigmatic Dicke model describing light-matter interactions, these materials also exhibit signatures of a superradiant phase transition. The ground state near the superradiant phase transition is expected to be squeezed, making Dicke materials a resource for quantum metrology and witnessing entanglement in solid-state systems. However, as an entanglement measure, squeezing can be sensitive to perturbations that are otherwise irrelevant for usual correlation functions and order parameters. Motivated by the prospect of observing squeezing in such Dicke materials, we study the robustness of ground state squeezing under ubiquitous imperfections such as finite temperature, disorder, and local interactions. Using analytical and numerical techniques, we show that the squeezing obtained is perturbatively stable against these imperfections and quantitatively evaluate regimes promising for experimental observation.

</details>


### [103] [Geometric Thermodynamics in Open Quantum Systems: Coherence, Curvature, and Work](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22452)
*Eric R. Bittner*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文建立了一个开放量子系统准静态热力学的几何框架，将功表达为曲率二形式的通量，并揭示了量子相干性如何重塑曲率结构，导致功的几何抵消甚至反转。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在为开放量子系统的准静态热力学建立几何框架，探索量子相干性如何影响热力学功的产生和分布，超越经典热力学面积定律的局限。

Method: 通过参数化控制流形上的动力学，在准静态极限下系统遵循稳态流形；使用固定基Lindblad模型分析非平衡稳态中的相干性效应，将功表达为曲率二形式Ω的通量。

Result: 对于热稳态，曲率是各向同性的且仅依赖于瞬时能量尺度；对于含相干的非平衡稳态，相干性使曲率变为各向异性和符号可变的，将控制流形划分为正负曲率区域，导致功的几何抵消甚至反转。

Conclusion: 热力学功作为曲率通量出现，其结构在经典系统中由热力学响应决定，在开放量子系统中则由哈密顿量本征基与环境选择的指针基之间的不对齐决定，量子相干性能够显著改变功的分布和符号。

Abstract: We formulate a geometric framework for quasistatic thermodynamics in open quantum systems by parameterizing the dynamics on a control manifold. In the quasistatic limit, the system follows a manifold of stationary states, and the work performed over a cycle is given by the flux of a curvature two-form, $W \sim \int Ω$, defined by the parametric response of the stationary state, establishing an open-system analog of classical thermodynamic area laws. For thermal stationary states, the curvature is isotropic and depends only on the instantaneous energy scale, yielding a population-driven geometry in which environmental parameters reshape how work is distributed across the control manifold. Beyond this limit, nonequilibrium stationary states can retain coherence in the energy representation; using a fixed-basis Lindblad model, we show that this coherence reshapes the curvature, making it anisotropic and sign-changing, so that work depends sensitively on the placement and orientation of the cycle. Quantum coherence therefore partitions the control manifold into regions of opposite curvature, producing geometric cancellation of work and allowing the net work over a cycle to be reduced or reversed despite dissipative dynamics. Thermodynamic work thus emerges as a curvature flux whose structure is set by thermodynamic response in classical systems and by basis misalignment between the Hamiltonian eigenbasis and the environment-selected pointer basis in open quantum systems.

</details>


### [104] [Development of Biphoton Entangled Light Spectroscopy (BELS) using Bell pairs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22547)
*V. V. Desai,N. P. Armitage*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文介绍了双光子纠缠光光谱学（BELS）——一种利用偏振纠缠贝尔对和双光子干涉探测材料特性的量子光谱技术，通过映射琼斯矩阵操作与贝尔态流形变换的关系，实现了对线性双折射和法拉第旋转的区分测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统光谱技术主要基于单光子强度测量，而BELS旨在开发一种利用量子纠缠特性的新型光谱学框架，通过探测双光子贝尔对的联合偏振和路径相关性变化来表征材料性质，为量子材料、纳米光子器件和光-物质相互作用研究提供更强大的量子增强方法。

Method: BELS采用偏振纠缠贝尔对作为探针，通过测量样品透射或散射后双光子贝尔对的联合偏振和路径相关性变化，利用跨通道符合计数进行分析。该方法的核心是建立琼斯矩阵操作与贝尔态流形变换之间的显式映射关系，使经典偏振光学中等效的光学元件在纠缠光子探测下产生不同的符合计数特征。

Result: 实验证明线性双折射和法拉第旋转产生正交的贝尔态混合，在单次测量中产生实验可区分的符合计数通道。研究成功测量了各向异性介质中的双折射现象和Tb₃Ga₅O₁₂中的法拉第旋转效应，验证了BELS技术区分不同光学效应的能力。

Conclusion: BELS通过映射光子纠缠态的变化，为未来的纠缠增强光谱学建立了新框架。该技术有望成为表征量子材料、纳米光子器件和光-物质相互作用的强大工具，最终可能在基础量子层面实现更深入的研究。

Abstract: We introduce Biphoton Entanglement Light Spectroscopy (BELS), a quantum spectroscopic technique that employs polarization entangled Bell pairs and two photon interference to probe material properties. In BELS, the measured signal arises not from single photon intensities but from changes in the joint polarization and path correlations of biphoton Bell pairs transmitted through or scattered by a sample and analyzed via cross channel coincidences. A key concept of BELS is the explicit mapping between Jones matrix operations and transformations within the Bell state manifold. Optical elements that are equivalent under classical polarization optics can produce qualitatively distinct signatures in the coincidence landscape when interrogated with entangled photons. We demonstrate that linear birefringence and Faraday rotation generate orthogonal admixtures of Bell states, yielding experimentally distinguishable coincidence channels within a single measurement. We measure birefringence in an anisotropic dielectric and Faraday rotation in $\text{Tb}_3\text{Ga}_5\text{O}_{12}$. By mapping the changes to the photonic entanglement, BELS establishes a new framework for future entanglement enhanced spectroscopy, a potentially powerful approach in characterizing quantum materials, nanophotonic devices, and light matter interactions perhaps eventually at a fundamentally quantum level.

</details>


### [105] [Boundary-sensitive non-Hermiticity of Floquet Hamiltonian: spectral transition and scale-free localization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22746)
*Bo Li,He-Ran Wang,Fei Song*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文报道了一维Floquet系统中边界敏感的PT对称性破缺新机制。通过设计时间周期驱动协议，实现了在周期边界条件下为厄米（Hermitian）但在开放边界条件下获得非厄米（non-Hermitian）边界项的Floquet哈密顿量，并建立了PT对称性破缺的相变条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在探索Floquet系统中由边界条件诱导的PT对称性破缺新机制。传统静态非厄米系统的PT对称性破缺通常需要能带接触（band touching），而本文研究Floquet系统中由边界条件差异引发的独特相变行为。

Method: 通过设计时间周期驱动协议（time-periodic driving protocol），构造了在周期边界条件下为厄米但在开放边界条件下获得非厄米边界项的Floquet哈密顿量。建立了PT对称性破缺的相变条件，并提供了构建多能带模型（multi-band models）的一般框架。

Result: 研究发现当准能（quasienergy）带宽扩展到覆盖整个频率布里渊区（frequency Brillouin zone）时，系统发生PT对称性破缺相变。在PT破缺相中，本征态表现出尺度无关的局域化（scale-free localization），这一现象源于非厄米项的系统尺寸特定标度行为。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了一维Floquet系统中边界敏感的PT对称性破缺新机制，该机制与静态非厄米系统的传统相变条件存在本质差异。研究结果为构建具有边界诱导相变的多能带模型提供了通用框架，深化了对Floquet系统中非厄米物理的理解。

Abstract: We report a novel mechanism of boundary-sensitive PT symmetry breaking in one-dimensional Floquet systems. By designing a time-periodic driving protocol, we realize a Floquet Hamiltonian that is Hermitian under periodic boundary conditions yet acquires non-Hermitian boundary terms under open boundary conditions due to the non-commutativity of driving Hamiltonians. We establish that a PT symmetry breaking transition occurs when the quasienergy bandwidth expands to cover the entire frequency Brillouin zone. This condition highlights a crucial difference from static non-Hermitian systems, where such transitions typically require band touching. Furthermore, we demonstrate that in the PT-broken phase, the eigenstates exhibit scale-free localization, a phenomenon arising from the specific system-size scaling of non-Hermitian terms. Finally, we provide a general framework for constructing multi-band models that exhibit this boundary-induced phase transition.

</details>


### [106] [A PAC-Bayesian approach to generalization for quantum models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22964)
*Pablo Rodriguez-Grasa,Matthias C. Caro,Jens Eisert,Elies Gil-Fuster,Franz J. Schreiber,Carlos Bravo-Prieto*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文针对量子机器学习中泛化能力分析的局限性，首次为广泛类别的量子模型推导了PAC-Bayesian泛化边界，通过通道扰动分析建立了依赖于学习参数矩阵范数的非均匀边界，并扩展至对称约束的等变量子模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子模型的泛化能力分析主要依赖于基于模型整体容量的均匀边界，这些边界通常过于宽松且完全无法反映实际训练过程。先前理论保证未能提供反映学习解特定性质而非整个假设类最坏行为的非均匀、数据依赖边界。

Method: 通过分析由一般量子通道（包括中间电路测量和前馈等耗散操作）组成的分层电路，推导了广泛类别量子模型的PAC-Bayesian泛化边界。采用通道扰动分析建立依赖于学习参数矩阵范数的非均匀边界，并将结果扩展至对称约束的等变量子模型。

Result: 建立了首个针对广泛量子模型的PAC-Bayesian泛化边界，这些边界依赖于学习参数矩阵的范数而非模型整体容量。通过数值实验验证了理论框架，为量子机器学习提供了更细致的泛化理解工具。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了可操作的模型设计见解，并为更细致理解量子机器学习中的泛化能力建立了基础工具，解决了现有容量基均匀边界过于宽松且不敏感于实际训练过程的问题。

Abstract: Generalization is a central concept in machine learning theory, yet for quantum models, it is predominantly analyzed through uniform bounds that depend on a model's overall capacity rather than the specific function learned. These capacity-based uniform bounds are often too loose and entirely insensitive to the actual training and learning process. Previous theoretical guarantees have failed to provide non-uniform, data-dependent bounds that reflect the specific properties of the learned solution rather than the worst-case behavior of the entire hypothesis class. To address this limitation, we derive the first PAC-Bayesian generalization bounds for a broad class of quantum models by analyzing layered circuits composed of general quantum channels, which include dissipative operations such as mid-circuit measurements and feedforward. Through a channel perturbation analysis, we establish non-uniform bounds that depend on the norms of learned parameter matrices; we extend these results to symmetry-constrained equivariant quantum models; and we validate our theoretical framework with numerical experiments. This work provides actionable model design insights and establishes a foundational tool for a more nuanced understanding of generalization in quantum machine learning.

</details>

Abstract: We analyze the metastability of Bose-Hubbard condensates for finite-size one-dimensional ring lattices and open chains, using a semiclassical tomographic perspective that emphasizes the relation of the many-body spectrum to the underlying classical phase-space structures. This constitutes an arena for inspection of quantum ergodicity and localization, in far-from-equilibrium scenarios of experimental interest. ### [108] [Two-parameter Family-Vicsek scaling in a dissipative XXZ spin chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23388)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典系统中的Family-Vicsek标度律描述了涨落的增长和有限尺寸饱和行为，但该标度律在量子系统特别是耗散量子系统中的扩展尚未充分研究。本研究旨在将FV粗糙度概念推广至耗散量子淬火动力学。

Method: 在非相互作用极限下，推导了耗散存在时粗糙度的闭式表达式；对于相互作用链，采用张量网络模拟方法研究Lindblad演化动力学，分析耗散弛豫时间对系统行为的影响。

Result: 非相互作用情况下，粗糙度显示双参数Family-Vicsek标度，能够平滑地插值于干净弹道行为和耗散主导标度之间。相互作用链中，有限磁化下的非耗散弹道增长具有鲁棒性，而完整Lindblad演化通常由耗散弛豫时间控制并呈现耗散主导的坍缩。

Conclusion: 该研究成功将Family-Vicsek标度律扩展至耗散量子系统，揭示了耗散在量子淬火动力学中的关键作用，为理解非平衡量子系统中的标度行为提供了新视角。

Abstract: Family-Vicsek (FV) scaling provides an understanding for the growth and finite-size saturation of fluctuations in classical systems. Here, we extend the FV roughness to transferred segment magnetization after quantum quenches in a dissipative XXZ spin chain with homogeneous gain and loss, starting from a nonequilibrium steady state with finite magnetization. In the non-interacting limit, we derive a closed-form expression for the roughness in the presence of dissipation. It displays two-parameter FV scaling and smoothly interpolates between the clean ballistic behavior and the dissipation dominated scalings. For interacting chains, tensor-network simulations show that the non-dissipative ballistic growth at finite magnetization is robust, whereas the full Lindblad evolution is generically controlled by the dissipative relaxation time and exhibits a dissipation-dominated collapse.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Motzkin自旋链是连接对称保护拓扑相（symmetry-protected topological phases）和AdS/CFT对偶（AdS/CFT correspondence）的重要数学模型，其高度纠缠的基态违反面积律且难以用传统数值方法模拟。大系统尺寸下由于高维自旋结构使得模拟更加困难，这使其成为超冷系统量子模拟的理想测试平台。

Method: 作者提出了一种基于里德堡原子的量子模拟方案，使用实验可访问的参数集有效实现Motzkin自旋。该方案能够产生有效的Motzkin基态。

Result: 研究结果表明，所得的有效Motzkin基态再现了理想Motzkin态的特征纠缠标度（entanglement scaling）和约化密度矩阵（reduced density matrix）的块结构特性。

Conclusion: 该工作为超越纯数学构造的Motzkin自旋的具体实验实现建立了途径，为在可编程里德堡模拟器中探索其他类似奇异的非面积律纠缠相（non-area-law entangled phases）开辟了道路。

Abstract: Motzkin spin chain is a well-known mathematical model with connections to symmetry-protected topological phases, such as the Haldane phase, as well as to concepts in the AdS/CFT correspondence. They exhibit highly entangled ground states that violate the area law and are exceptionally difficult to simulate with conventional numerical methods. Numerical simulations of the Motzkin ground state become further challenging at large system sizes due to their high-dimensional spin structure, rendering it a natural test bed for quantum simulation with ultra-cold systems. Here, we propose a Rydberg-atom based quantum simulation scheme that effectively realizes Motzkin spins using an experimentally accessible set of parameters. We show that the resulting effective Motzkin ground state reproduces the characteristic entanglement scaling and the block-structure properties of the reduced density matrix associated with the ideal Motzkin state. Our results establish a pathway toward a concrete experimental realization of Motzkin spins beyond purely mathematical constructions, opening avenues for exploring other similar exotic non-area-law entangled phases in programmable Rydberg simulators.

### [110] [Exact analytical PGSE signal for diffusion confined to a cylindrical surface using a spectral Laplacian formalism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23421)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有圆柱表面受限扩散的MRI信号模型通常依赖于窄脉冲极限、有限梯度持续时间的近似处理或高斯相位近似，这些方法在高扩散权重下准确性显著下降，需要更精确的解析解决方案。

Method: 基于限制几何特征基中的拉普拉斯算子谱矩阵形式，推导了有限PGSE梯度下圆柱表面扩散的Bloch-Torrey方程精确解析解。利用圆柱表面对称性引入简化实谱基，并开发了包括Strang分裂近似和高斯-勒让德积分的高效数值策略。

Result: 获得了适用于任意梯度持续时间和间隔的扩散MRI信号精确表达式，验证了该解析信号在广泛圆柱半径和实验参数范围内与蒙特卡洛模拟的一致性，并量化了加速实现与精确公式之间的精度-运行时间权衡。

Abstract: Pulsed-gradient spin-echo (PGSE) MRI experiments probe molecular self-diffusion through spin phase accumulation under time-dependent magnetic field gradients. For diffusion confined to cylindrical surfaces, existing analytical signal models typically rely on the narrow-pulse limit, approximate treatments of finite gradient durations, or the Gaussian phase approximation, which become increasingly inaccurate at high diffusion weightings. Here, we derive an exact analytical solution of the Bloch-Torrey equation for diffusion confined to a cylindrical surface under finite PGSE gradients and obtain the corresponding diffusion MRI signal expression valid for arbitrary gradient durations and separations. The derivation is based on a spectral matrix formalism of the Laplace operator in the eigenbasis of the confining geometry. The signal is expressed as a product of non-commuting matrix exponentials, without approximations to the diffusion propagator or the spin phase distribution. We further introduce a reduced real spectral basis exploiting the symmetry of the cylindrical surface, substantially improving computational efficiency. Building on this exact formulation, we develop efficient numerical strategies for repeated signal evaluations, including a Strang splitting approximation of the matrix exponentials and an efficient computation of the spherical mean signal using Gauss-Legendre quadrature. The analytical signal is validated against Monte Carlo simulations over a wide range of cylinder radii and experimental parameters. The accelerated implementations are benchmarked against the exact formulation to quantify accuracy-runtime trade-offs. These results establish a computationally efficient framework for evaluating directional and orientationally averaged diffusion MRI signals in applications requiring large numbers of model evaluations.

### [111] [Tunable Floquet selection rules in a driven Ising chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23493)
*Rishi Paresh Joshi,Sanchayan Banerjee,Sneha Narasimha Moorthy,Tapan Mishra*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 该研究通过Floquet微扰理论分析周期性驱动的Ising链，揭示了由单一Floquet选择规则导致的Hilbert空间碎片化、Floquet冻结现象以及预热边缘记忆等奇异预热动力学行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索周期性驱动自旋-1/2 Ising链中的奇异预热现象，特别是通过Floquet微扰理论揭示由单一选择规则支配的动力学行为，包括Hilbert空间碎片化和非传统形式的动力学局域化。

Method: 采用Floquet微扰理论分析周期性驱动的自旋-1/2 Ising链，该链包含最近邻耦合、纵向场以及诱导单自旋翻转的弱横向场。通过推导Floquet选择规则来研究不同参数区域下的预热动力学。

Result: 发现单一Floquet选择规则支配预热动力学，导致Hilbert空间碎片化。在特定场-相互作用强度比和可公度驱动周期下，该规则仅允许受限的自旋翻转子集，产生预热Hilbert空间碎片化。开放边界条件下产生长寿命预热边缘记忆，周期性边界条件下最大存活碎片精确对应PXP扇区并展现Floquet继承的疤痕现象学。更高可公度比下所有一阶单自旋翻转通道被抑制，系统进入Floquet冻结区域。

Conclusion: 研究通过Floquet微扰理论获得的选择规则，在不同参数区域实现了奇异的预热现象，包括Hilbert空间碎片化、Floquet冻结和预热边缘记忆，这些现象均由单一Floquet选择规则支配。

Abstract: We study a periodically driven spin-$1/2$ Ising chain with a nearest-neighbour coupling and longitudinal field while a weak transverse field induces single-spin flips. Through Floquet perturbation theory (FPT), we obtain signatures of Hilbert space fragmentation (HSF) and an unconventional form of dynamical localisation which we call the Floquet freezing. Our analysis suggests that these observations emerge due to a single Floquet selection rule that dictates the prethermal dynamics. For a special value of the field-to-interaction strength ratio together with commensurate drive periods, this rule permits only a constrained subset of bulk spin flips, leading to prethermal HSF in the full spin-$1/2$ Hilbert space. Under open boundary conditions, the same rule suppresses boundary spin flips up to higher order in perturbation and produces long-lived prethermal edge memory, which is neither topological in origin nor is a strong zero mode. Furthermore, under periodic boundary conditions, the largest surviving fragment is exactly the PXP sector at leading order and therefore exhibits Floquet-inherited scar phenomenology in the prethermal window. At higher commensurate ratios of field strength to interaction strength, all first-order single-spin-flip channels are suppressed and the system enters a regime of Floquet freezing. Hence, our study leverages the selection rules obtained through Floquet perturbation theory to obtain exotic prethermal phenomena at different parameter regimes.

Conclusion: 压力可作为建立氧化铪多晶型物理家族关系的有效判据，解决了现有研究中缺乏连接母相和子相的物理理论基础的问题，并为理解该材料的相变和铁电性提供了新视角。

Abstract: Several candidate reference phases have been proposed to discuss phase transitions and ferroelectricity in hafnia in recent years. Although these proposals comply with crystallographic requirements, a physically compelling rationale connecting parent and daughter phases is often lacking. This problem is aggravated by the absence of clearly dominant polarization switching pathways, making it difficult to formulate a robust physical criterion for identifying the relevant high-symmetry states. Here we use first-principles calculations to show that pressure provides a simple and robust criterion for establishing physically meaningful family relationships among many hafnia polymorphs, including the monoclinic ground state and the technologically relevant ferroelectric phase, and their respective parent structures. Our simulations also reveal several previously unreported phases, including higher-energy structures that act as common ancestors of the widely discussed cubic and orthorhombic reference phases.

### [113] [Electrochemical and thermal control of continuous phase transitions in P2-NaxNi1/3Mn2/3O2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22487)
*Dylan A. Edelman,John Cattermull,Jue Liu,Zhelong Jiang,Hari Ramachandran,Edward Mu,Cheng Li,Anton Van der Ven,Katherine J. Harmon,William C. Chueh*

Method: 采用中子衍射和中子衍射（neutron diffraction）与X射线衍射（X-ray diffraction）相结合的方法，分析P2-NaxNi1/3Mn2/3O2（NNM）的低对称性正交晶胞。通过变温同步辐射X射线衍射进一步阐明钠空位无序化与正交-六方相变之间的耦合关系。

Abstract: Sodium layered oxides often undergo phase transformations involving ordering or disordering of Na+ upon desodiation, i.e., when cycled as a battery electrode. Accurately characterizing these phases is crucial for understanding functional properties, such as chemical diffusivity. In this work, we reveal that Na+-vacancy (dis)ordering in a layered oxide is intrinsically coupled to continuous symmetry-changing transformations of the host structure. We examine the low-symmetry orthorhombic unit cell of P2-NaxNi1/3Mn2/3O2 (NNM) using both neutron and X-ray diffraction. Specifically, special sodium stoichiometries (x = 2/3 and 1/2) exhibit concomitant Na+-vacancy ordering and an orthorhombic distortion from the parent hexagonal unit cell. We then demonstrate that electrochemical desodiation drives symmetry-changing transformations in NNM that are linked to Na+-vacancy (dis)ordering, with evidence of second-order behavior observed near x = 2/3. Variable-temperature synchrotron X-ray diffraction further clarifies the coupling between Na+-vacancy disordering and orthorhombic-to-hexagonal phase transitions in NNM. The temperature-driven phase transitions at both x = 2/3 and 1/2 are also consistent with a second-order mechanism. Our analysis of the phase transitions in NNM has fundamental consequences for sodium chemical diffusivity in the vicinity of the ordered phases. The insights from this work are directly applicable to other layered oxides that exhibit alkali-metal-vacancy ordering.

### [114] [Chirality Cannot Be Ferroic in Enantiomorphic Space-Groups](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22501)
*F. Gómez-Ortiz,S. Mamoudou Taganga,E. E. McCabe,A. H. Romero,E. Bousquet*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该论文通过群论证明和系统分析，论证了从非手性母相到手性相变不能由布里渊区中心（Γ点）不稳定性驱动，因此手性不能作为初级铁性序参量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着对周期性固体中结构手性（structural chirality）兴趣的增长，有观点认为手性可能构成新的铁性序参量（ferroic order parameter）。本研究旨在从群论角度检验这一可能性。

Method: 采用形式化的群论证明和系统的群-子群分析，并明确展示了所有允许对称手性声子本征矢的非手性母相空间群在区中心均不存在此类本征矢。

Result: 证明了从共同非手性母相产生对映体对（enantiomorphic pair）任一成员的非手性到手性相变，不能由布里渊区中心（Γ-point）不稳定性驱动。初级铁性序参量必须满足在区中心不可约表示下变换的要求，而手性相变不满足此条件。

Conclusion: 导致对映体空间群（enantiomorphic space groups）的相变不能归类为初级铁性相变。这预示着任何临界涨落增强必须发生在有限波矢（finite-q）处，而非作为均匀宏观磁化率的发散。

Abstract: With growing interest in structural chirality in periodic solids, it has been suggested that chirality might constitute a new ferroic order parameter. In this work, we demonstrate, by means of a formal group-theoretical proof and a systematic group-subgroup analysis, that achiral-to-chiral transitions that produce either member of an enantiomorphic pair cannot be driven by a Brillouin-zone-center ($Γ$-point) instability from a common achiral parent. We further substantiate this result by explicitly showing that none of the achiral parent space groups that admit symmetry-chiral phonon eigenvectors host them at the zone center. Given that a primary ferroic order parameter must, among other requirements, transform according to a zone-center irreducible representation, we conclude that phase transitions leading to enantiomorphic space groups cannot be classified as primary ferroic transitions. This predicts that any critical enhancement of fluctuations must occur at finite-$q$ rather than as a divergence of a uniform macroscopic susceptibility.

</details>

Conclusion: 机器学习方法为钙钛矿太阳能电池的稳定性监测提供了新途径，通过数字孪生模型可以深入讨论测量结果与器件实际物理状态之间的差异及其物理意义。

These results are compared to what can be classically interpreted by analysing changes in J-V curves, and the evolution of the predicted parameters is studied. The predictions are then used to simulate a digital twin of the measured devices, and their physical implications and the differences between measurements and devices are discussed.

However, their computational cost limits the size of the systems studied to a few nanometers and a few pores while experimental materials are highly heterogeneous with a distribution of particle and pore sizes. The code calculates quantities of adsorbed ions, diffusion coefficients and NMR spectra of ions / molecules adsorbed in porous carbon matrices. In this work, we report on a new implementation of LPC3D, written in Python using the PyStencils module which can generate optimized C++ and CUDA code. This implementation is parallel, can be run on CPU and GPU, and allows one to simulate systems going from a single carbon particle to a supercapacitor with hundreds of micrometers in length. ### [117] [Origin of the tetragonal-to-hexagonal phase transitions in Fe-doped BaTiO$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22571)
*Zhiyuan Li,Ruiwen Xie,Hongbin Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究Fe掺杂BaTiO₃中四方相到六方相相变的机制，通过第一性原理计算验证实验观察到的相变行为，并比较不同钛酸盐（CaTiO₃和SrTiO₃）在相同掺杂条件下的差异。

Method: 采用详细的第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations），包括总能计算和电子结构分析，量化三种可能机制：氧空位（oxygen vacancies）、Jahn-Teller畸变（Jahn-Teller distortions）和容忍因子（tolerance factor）变化的影响。

Result: 总能计算证实Fe掺杂约4%时发生四方相到六方相的交叉转变，与实验观察一致；氧空位通过电荷补偿将相变浓度从~4%降至~2%；Jahn-Teller畸变施加较大弹性惩罚促进相变；容忍因子减小则抑制六方相形成。

Conclusion: Fe掺杂BaTiO₃的四方相到六方相相变受多种机制共同影响：氧空位和Jahn-Teller畸变促进相变，而容忍因子减小抑制六方相形成；电子结构分析显示氧空位引起的电荷重新分布具有强烈的轨道依赖性。

Abstract: Based on detailed first-principles calculations, we investigate the tetragonal-to-hexagonal phase transition in Fe-doped BaTiO$_3$. Total energy calculations confirm a crossover from the tetragonal to hexagonal phases around 4\% Fe, in agreement with experimental observations, where comparative calculations show that neither CaTiO$_3$ nor SrTiO$_3$ exhibits similar behavior under equivalent substitution. Furthermore, three possible mechanisms are quantified: oxygen vacancies shift the crossover concentration from $\sim$4\% to $\sim$2\% through charge compensation, Jahn-Teller distortions impose a larger elastic penalty, both favoring tetragonal-to-hexagonal phase transitions; whereas the tolerance factor is reduced in comparison with that of pristine BaTiO$_3$ for reasonable Fe valence states, disfavoring the occurrence of the hexagonal phases. Detailed analysis on the electronic structure reveals that the charge redistribution induced by oxygen vacancy is strongly orbital dependent due to the local crystal structure distortions.

### [118] [Influence Functional Approach to Non-Perturbative Exciton Binding Renormalization from Phonons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22575)
*Rohit Rana,Eric R. Heller,Antonios M. Alvertis,Jeffrey B. Neaton,David T. Limmer*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究构建了一个多体模型哈密顿量（many-body model Hamiltonian）来捕捉声子（phonons）如何随温度重整化激子（exciton）结合能，通过第一性原理参数化并结合路径积分蒙特卡洛（path integral Monte Carlo）方法进行非微扰计算，发现激子结合能主要受光学声子耦合影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解声子如何随温度重整化激子结合能，特别是需要构建一个能够从第一性原理完全参数化的多体模型哈密顿量来定量描述这一物理过程。

Method: 研究方法包括：1）使用GW近似（GW approximation）和密度泛函微扰理论（density functional perturbation theory）从第一性原理完全参数化多体模型哈密顿量；2）采用基于影响泛函（influence functional）的路径积分蒙特卡洛方法在虚时间（imaginary time）中演化哈密顿量，以非微扰方式捕获静态准粒子性质。

Result: 研究结果包括：1）对于Wannier-Mott型激子（Wannier-Mott type excitons），计算得到的结合能与实验定量吻合；2）除了纵向光学模式（longitudinal optical modes）的长程偶极相互作用外，声学模式（acoustic modes）和横向光学模式（transverse optical modes）的短程形变势（deformation potentials）在高温下能显著重整化电子和空穴极化子（polaron）结合能；3）激子结合能主要受光学声子耦合重整化。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，激子结合能主要受光学声子耦合重整化，而声学模式和横向光学模式的短程形变势虽能显著影响电子和空穴极化子结合能，但对激子结合能的重整化作用有限。

Abstract: We construct a many-body model Hamiltonian to capture how phonons renormalize exciton binding as a function of temperature. By using the GW approximation and density functional perturbation theory, we are able to parameterize this Hamiltonian completely from first principles. To capture static quasiparticle properties non-perturbatively, we evolve this Hamiltonian in imaginary time with path integral Monte Carlo using an influence functional based approach. For a class of Wannier-Mott type excitons, our binding energies are in quantitative agreement with experiment. We find that in addition to long-range dipolar interactions from longitudinal optical modes, short-ranged deformation potentials from acoustic modes and transverse optical modes can significantly renormalize electron and hole polaron binding energies at elevated temperature. However, exciton binding energies are only appreciably renormalized by coupling to optical phonons.

Analysis that accounts for additional diffraction features such as diffraction spots and excess-deficiency effects should provide more robust and accurate indexing, if they can be incorporated in pattern indexing or simulation routines. A more accurate understanding of their physics of formation and geometry is required to enable this change. In this work, we demonstrate geometric and full contrast dynamical simulation of on-axis transmission Kikuchi patterns, based on experimental patterns captured using a modular, direct electron detector-based set-up in the scanning electron microscope. First, a diffraction geometry calibration routine is proposed based on the electron channeling pattern of the direct electron detector. This allows us to accurately account for the position of diffraction spots in both geometric and dynamical simulations with good agreement with experimental patterns. Abstract: Driven-dissipative dynamics underlie a wide range of nonequilibrium phenomena in quantum materials, yet reduced descriptions beyond the quasi-equilibrium picture remain difficult to establish. Combined with experimentally constrained Lindblad dynamics, we show that this delay reflects the finite-time spreading of excitations across many phonon levels. Method: 采用方波脉冲源热反射技术（square-pulsed source thermoreflectance），结合时间分辨检测与宽带调制，探测铝-水和铝-辛烷界面。同时使用铝-二氧化硅界面作为对照实验，以区分液体特异性效应。

Result: 实验观察到铝-水和铝-辛烷界面的表观界面热导随调制频率增加而可重复性增大。铝-二氧化硅界面未显示可测量的频率依赖性，表明该效应是液体特有的而非所有非晶材料的共性。数据可用双通道液体模型解释，其中扩散模式和类声子模式在有限非平衡长度上弱交换能量。

Conclusion: 根据热渗透深度与非平衡长度的相对大小，研究识别出三种输运机制。这些发现挑战了液体模式完全平衡的常见假设，并为模拟液体界面动态能量交换提供了实验约束。

Abstract: Understanding heat transfer across solid-liquid interfaces is central to thermal management and energy technologies, yet whether the interfacial thermal conductance (ITC) depends on the timescale of heating remains unclear. Here we use square-pulsed source thermoreflectance, which combines time-resolved detection with broadband modulation, to probe Al-water and Al-octane interfaces. We observe a reproducible increase of the apparent ITC with modulation frequency. A control Al-silica interface shows no measurable frequency dependence, indicating that the effect is specific to liquids rather than a generic feature shared by all amorphous materials. We explain the data with a two-channel liquid picture in which diffusional and phonon-like modes exchange energy weakly over a finite nonequilibrium length. From the relative magnitude of the thermal penetration depth and the nonequilibrium length, we identify three transport regimes. These findings challenge the common assumption of fully equilibrated liquid modes and provide experimental constraints for modeling dynamic energy exchange at liquid interfaces.

</details>


### [123] [First-Principles Theory of Chirality-Induced Spin Selectivity at Molecule-Metal Interfaces in Photoemission](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22725)
*Amos Afugu,Gyanu P. Kafle,Zhen-Fei Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过第一性原理计算发现，手性分子-金属界面的光电子能谱自旋极化主要反映杂化界面的电子结构，而非分子手性本身。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自旋分辨光电子能谱（spin-resolved photoelectron spectroscopy）是手性诱导自旋选择性（chirality-induced spin selectivity）的主要实验探针，但尚不清楚测量的自旋极化反映的是分子手性本身还是杂化界面的更广泛电子结构。

Method: 采用第一性原理理论，在三步光发射框架内使用密度泛函理论（density functional theory），将界面作为整体而非金属基底加独立分子自旋过滤器来处理。计算了(M)-和(P)-七螺烯吸附在Au(111)和Cu(111)上以及非手性对照物晕苯/Au(111)的光激发步骤产生的自旋极化。

Result: 吸附显著改变了相对于清洁金属表面的光电子能谱自旋极化，但对映异构体产生对称相关的、定性相似的响应，且与非手性晕苯的响应相当。这表明自旋极化变化更自然地归因于杂化界面的电子结构而非单独的分子手性。

Conclusion: 光电子能谱自旋极化主要反映手性分子-金属界面的整体电子结构特性，而非分子手性本身的直接效应，这对理解手性诱导自旋选择性现象的实验测量具有重要意义。

Abstract: Spin-resolved photoelectron spectroscopy (PES) is a major experimental probe of chirality-induced spin selectivity (CISS), yet it remains unclear whether the measured spin polarization reflects molecular chirality itself or the broader electronic structure of the hybrid interface. We present a first-principles theory of PES spin polarization at chiral molecule-metal interfaces, treating the interface holistically rather than as a metal substrate plus a separate molecular spin filter/polarizer. Using density functional theory within a three-step photoemission framework, we compute the spin polarization generated in the optical-excitation step for ($M$)- and ($P$)-heptahelicene adsorbed on Au(111) and Cu(111), and for coronene/Au(111) as a non-chiral control. We find that adsorption strongly reshapes the PES spin polarization relative to the clean metal surface, but opposite enantiomers yield symmetry-related, qualitatively similar responses that are also comparable to that of the non-chiral coronene. These results indicate that changes in the PES spin polarization are more naturally attributed to the electronic structure of the hybrid interface than to molecular chirality alone.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了层间相互作用对交替磁体电子结构和输运性质的关键调控机制，特别是栅压调控的不对称性源于电极几何结构诱导的面外对称性破缺。这些发现为多层交替磁体自旋电子学器件的设计和优化提供了重要指导。

Abstract: Two-dimensional altermagnets exhibit exceptional potential for low-power spintronics via nonrelativistic spin splitting and zero net magnetization. Here, we systematically investigate the influence of interlayer interactions on the electronic, magnetic and quantum transport properties of bilayer vanadium oxysulfide (V2S2O), a prototypical layered altermagnet, using DFT and NEGF calculations. Our results reveal that interlayer interactions predominantly modulate the p-orbital derived top valence bands, inducing a profound competitive valence band maximum position between Gamma-point pz and X/Y-point pxy orbitals, with an energy difference as small as 9 meV. Furthermore, interlayer interactions suppress the piezomagnetic effect and impose additional requirements on the type of strain for the bilayer system, compared to its monolayer counterpart. Out-of-plane external electric fields effectively weaken interlayer coupling by enlarging the energy difference of Gamma/X-Y top valence bands to 170 meV. Quantum transport simulations on a bilayer Au/V2S2O/Au two-probe device demonstrate the presence of pronounced spin current. Interlayer interactions reduce the transmission spin polarization from nearly 100% (monolayer) to 60% (bilayer) for energies above the Fermi level. Notably, gate-voltage modulation exhibits significant asymmetry in controlling charge-to-spin current conversion efficiency, originating from the out-of-plane symmetry breaking induced by the electrode geometry. Specifically, a positive gate voltage markedly enhances the contribution of the bottom layer to the overall spin polarization, while a negative gate voltage induces a marginal reduction of transmission spin polarization, attributed to the inherently weak polarization contribution of the bottom layer. These findings provide essential insights for the design and optimization of multilayer altermagnetic spintronics.

### [127] [Ultrafast electrically controlled magnetism in charge-order-induced ferroelectric altermagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22848)
*Yuhao Gu,Yu-Hui Song,Yihao Wang,Ze-Feng Gao,Huan-Cheng Yang,Peng-Jie Guo,Zhong-Yi Lu*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于对称性分析（symmetry analysis）和第一性原理电子结构计算（first-principles electronic structure calculations），预测LiV₂F₆同时具有交变磁性和电荷序诱导铁电性。通过时间依赖密度泛函理论（time-dependent density functional theory）计算电极化翻转动力学。

Result: 计算表明LiV₂F₆同时具有交变磁性和铁电性，且两者均源于电荷序（charge order），因此表现出强磁电耦合（magnetoelectric coupling）。电极化翻转可在15飞秒（femtoseconds）内完成，并能诱导能带自旋极化切换。

Abstract: The altermagnetism with antiparallel spin alignment exhibits anisotropic spin splitting and may possess an insulating state with a high Neel temperature, while the charge-order-induced ferroelectricity has ultrafast electric polarization switching. Considering that altermagnetism requires breaking space inversion,, the physical foundation for exploring ultrafast electrically controlled magnetism in altermagnetic ferroelectric materials is thus established. In this Letter, based on symmetry analysis and first-principles electronic structure calculations, we predict that LiV$_2$F$_6$ is a material that simultaneously hosts altermagnetism and charge-order-induced ferroelectricity. Since both the altermagnetism and ferroelectricity originate from charge order, LiV$_2$F$_6$ should exhibit strong magnetoelectric coupling. Our calculations indeed demonstrate that electric polarization reversal can induce band spin-polarization switching in LiV$_2$F$_6$. Moreover, time-dependent density functional theory calculations show that the electric polarization reversal in LiV$_2$F$_6$ occurs in 15 femtoseconds. Consequently, ultrafast electrically controlled magnetism can be realized in LiV$_2$F$_6$. Given that LiV$_2$F$_6$ has already been experimentally synthesized, our work provides a promising material platform for achieving ultrafast electrically controlled magnetism, which might have significant implications for the design of future electronic devices.

### [128] [Mechanical Origin of High-Temperature Thermal Stability in Platinum Oxides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22849)
*Fangyuan Ma,Mengzhao Sun,Xuejian Gong,Jun Cai,Zhujun Wang,Di Zhou*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究通过分析原子尺度弹性网络的机械特性来探究热稳定性增强的根源。重点考察结构转变前后晶格约束状态的变化，以及氧化物与铂衬底之间莫尔图案（Moiré pattern）的匹配关系。

Result: 结构转变前，过度约束的晶格通过与铂衬底的不匹配莫尔图案产生局部自应力状态，降低热耐久性。转变后，氧化物转变为机械柔性结构，形成等静压网络（isostatic network），与衬底构成匹配的莫尔超晶格，释放弹性能量并增强稳定性。

Conclusion: 网络连通性在调控热稳定性中起根本作用，这为极端环境下的催化剂设计提供了原理指导。机械鲁棒性转变是热稳定性提升的关键机制。

Abstract: Platinum oxides are vital catalysts, but their limited thermal stability hinders applications. Recent studies have uncovered a structural transition in two-dimensional platinum oxides that significantly enhances their thermal resilience by several hundred Kelvin. Herein, we demonstrate that this enhanced stability stems from the mechanical robustness of the elastic network at the atomic scale. Prior to the transition, an over-constrained lattice generates localized states of self-stress through an incommensurate Moiré pattern with the platinum substrate, reducing thermal endurance. After the transition, the oxide shifts to a mechanically flexible structure with balanced degrees of freedom and constraints. The isostatic network, together with the platinum substrate, forms a commensurate Moiré superlattice that relaxes elastic energy and enhances stability. These findings highlight the fundamental role of network connectivity in governing thermal stability, and provide a design principle for catalysts in extreme environments.

We find that all universal MLIPs employed in this work yield unsatisfactory mixing energies without fine-tuning. Applied to the experimentally synthesized (Mo,Ta,Nb,W,V)S$_2$ system, fine-tuned models based on enumerated structures can achieve near-DFT accuracy in predicting mixing energies while enabling Monte-Carlo simulations and random structure sampling at scales inaccessible to DFT.

*Inês Freitas,Ana Sofia Sousa,Duarte Magalhães Esteves,Mamour Sall,Ângelo Rafael Granadeiro da Costa,Joana Madureira,Sandra Cabo Verde,Katharina Lorenz,Marco Peres*

Method: 采用射频溅射（RF sputtering）在蓝宝石衬底上沉积Ga₂O₃薄膜，然后以150 keV能量和5×10¹⁶ ions/cm²名义注量进行Ag或Au离子注入，随后在200-700°C温度范围内进行热退火处理。使用卢瑟福背散射谱（RBS）和透射电子显微镜（TEM）进行表征。

Result: RBS测量显示注入过程中的饱和效应导致实际掺入注量较低，且退火后出现外扩散现象。TEM证实了金属纳米颗粒的形成，其分布与RBS测量的金属分布一致。光学吸收测量显示Ag注入薄膜中观察到明显的局域表面等离子体共振（LSPR）带，而Au注入薄膜仅在≥500°C退火后才出现明显的LSPR峰。

Conclusion: 退火引起的LSPR位移主要归因于Ga₂O₃基质的变化而非纳米颗粒尺寸的改变。研究结果确立了离子注入作为将等离子体纳米结构集成到Ga₂O₃中的可行方法。

Abstract: Gallium oxide (Ga$_2$O$_3$) is a wide-bandgap semiconductor with exceptional electrical and optical properties, making it a promising material for optoelectronic and sensing applications. In this work, we demonstrate for the first time the formation of plasmonic silver (Ag) and gold (Au) nanoparticles embedded in Ga$_2$O$_3$ thin films via ion implantation. Ga$_2$O$_3$ films deposited by RF sputtering on sapphire substrates were implanted with Ag or Au ions at 150 keV and a nominal fluence of 5 $\times$ 10$^{16}$ ions/cm$^2$, followed by thermal annealing between 200 and 700 °C. Rutherford backscattering spectrometry (RBS) measurements revealed saturation effects during implantation, resulting in lower incorporated fluences, as well as out-diffusion with post-implantation annealing. Transmission electron microscopy confirmed the formation of metallic nanoparticles with a distribution consistent with the metal profiles measured by RBS. Optical absorption measurements showed a pronounced localized surface plasmon resonance (LSPR) band in the Ag-implanted films, visible even in the as-implanted state and red-shifting with increasing annealing temperature, while Au-implanted films exhibited a distinct LSPR peak only after annealing at $\geq$500 °C. The observed LSPR shifts with annealing are attributed primarily to changes in the Ga$_2$O$_3$ matrix rather than a change in nanoparticle size. These results establish ion implantation as a viable approach for integrating plasmonic nanostructures into Ga$_2$O$_3$.

</details>


### [131] [Open Quantum System Theory of Muon Spin Relaxation in Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23137)
*Elvis F. Arguelles,Osamu Sugino*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种非马尔可夫（non-Markovian）的μ子自旋弛豫理论，将植入的μ子视为与时间相关的局域磁场环境耦合的开放量子自旋。该理论超越了强碰撞近似，能够对零场和弱纵向场μSR谱进行全局定量分析，并在Li₀.₇₃CoO₂中识别出非马尔可夫特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有μ子自旋弛豫（μSR）理论主要基于马尔可夫近似或强碰撞近似，难以处理时间相关的局域磁场环境。需要发展超越这些近似的理论框架，以更精确地分析μSR实验数据，特别是对于复杂材料体系。

Method: 采用Schwinger-Keldysh影响泛函（influence-functional）表述，推导出自旋随机运动方程，其中有色涨落（colored fluctuations）和延迟记忆扭矩（retarded memory torque）处于同等地位。该理论在适当极限下可约化为标准的Kubo-Toyabe描述。

Result: 该理论能够对零场（ZF）和弱纵向场（LF）μSR谱进行超越强碰撞近似的全局定量分析。应用于Li₀.₇₃CoO₂时，成功分离了静态和锂驱动的组分，发现了中间温度窗口的热激活涨落速率，并在ZF/弱LF线形中识别出由延迟反作用/记忆核捕获的清晰非马尔可夫特征。

Conclusion: 该研究发展了一种处理μ子自旋弛豫的非马尔可夫理论框架，为分析复杂材料中的μSR数据提供了更精确的工具。理论能够识别传统方法可能忽略的非马尔可夫特征，在Li₀.₇₃CoO₂中的应用验证了其有效性。

Abstract: We present a non-Markovian theory of muon spin relaxation that treats the implanted muon as an open quantum spin coupled to a temporally correlated local magnetic environment. Using a Schwinger-Keldysh influence-functional formulation, we derive a spin stochastic equation of motion in which colored fluctuations and retarded memory torque appear on equal footing. In the appropriate limits, the theory reduces to standard Kubo-Toyabe descriptions. This enables quantitative, global analysis of zero-field (ZF) and weak longitudinal-field (LF) $μ$SR spectra beyond the strong-collision approximation. Applied to $\mathrm{Li}_{0.73}\mathrm{CoO}_2$ when the muon is frozen at the stopping site, the approach separates static and Li-driven components, finds a thermally activated fluctuation rate over the intermediate-temperature window, and identifies a clear non-Markovian signature in the ZF/weak-LF line shapes captured by a retarded backaction/memory kernel.

Abstract: Magnetic control of correlated spin systems is central to the development of next-generation spin-based technologies. Here, we show that the orientation of the applied magnetic field drives different magnetic phase transition sequences in NdFeO3 across a broad temperature range. Abstract: The performance of all-solid-state battery (ASSB) cathodes strongly depends on their microstructure. Optimizing the cathode morphology can therefore enhance effective macroscopic properties such as ionic and electronic conductivity. The search for optimized microstructures can be facilitated by virtual materials testing: By integrating image analysis and stochastic microstructure modeling to generate a wide range of realistic 3D microstructures and evaluate their effective macroscopic properties by means of numerical simulations, thereby reducing the need for extensive physical experiments. This approach allows for the investigation of structure-property relationships through parametric regression models that incorporate relevant geometrical descriptors of microstructures such as volume fractions, mean geodesic tortuosities, specific surface areas, and constrictivities. By linking these geometrical descriptors to macroscopic properties, virtual materials testing provides quantitative insight into how microstructure influences material performance. In the present paper, this framework is applied for ASSB cathodes. In addition, by systematically varying model parameters, a broad range of 3D microstructures can be generated, which remain close to the original cathode morphology while inducing targeted changes in selected geometrical descriptors. The resulting database enables the calibration of regression models whose predictive performance is assessed by comparing predicted and simulated effective properties such as the ionic and electronic conductivity, thereby quantifying how accurately combinations of geometrical descriptors can explain and predict variations in effective macroscopic properties.

### [134] [Experimental Insights into the Limiting Mechanism of Vacancy Transport in Sodium Metal Anodes for Solid State Batteries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23340)
*Ansgar Lowack,Rafael Anton,Bingchen Xue,Kristian Nikolowski,Cornelius Dirksen,Mareike Partsch,Alexander Michaelis*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了钠金属陶瓷固态电池在放电过程中电极脱层的机制，发现界面空位积累是限制因素，而非体相扩散。通过引入亲钠合金中间层可降低活化能，为开发稳定高倍率钠固态电池提供了关键路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 钠金属陶瓷固态电池（Na-SSBs）相比传统二次电池具有更高的安全性和能量密度，但放电过程中钠金属电极与陶瓷电解质界面的临界脱层现象尚未被充分理解。这一现象源于界面空位积累，阻碍了电池的稳定运行。

Method: 研究采用线性电流斜坡法，在两个被陶瓷固态电解质隔开的钠金属电极间施加电流，以诱发空位积累。通过分析临界电流密度$j_\mathrm{crit}(T)$与温度的关系，对三种固态电解质（$\mathrm{Na_{1.9}Al_{10.67}Li_{0.33}O_{17}}$、$\mathrm{Na_{3.4}Zr_2Si_{2.4}P_{0.6}O_{12}}$和$\mathrm{Na_5SmSi_4O_{12}}$）进行阿伦尼乌斯分析，并考察了锡-钠合金中间层的影响。

Result: 当电流密度超过临界值$j_\mathrm{crit}$时，阳极电压呈指数增长而非线性增加。三种电解质的活化能$E_\mathrm{A}$为0.13-0.15 eV，显著高于钠体相中空位扩散的活化能（0.053 eV）。活化能对阳极微观结构变化不敏感，排除了体相扩散作为传输瓶颈的可能性。引入薄锡-钠合金中间层可将$E_\mathrm{A}$降至$(0.10\pm0.01)$ eV。

Conclusion: 界面热力学而非体相扩散是钠金属陶瓷固态电池的速率限制步骤。亲钠（sodiophilic）、钠导电的中间层和低张力界面是实现稳定、高倍率钠固态电池的关键途径，特别是在实际堆叠压力下。

Abstract: Ceramic solid-state batteries with sodium (Na) metal electrodes promise enhanced safety and energy density compared to contemporary secondary batteries. However, the critical delamination of the Na metal electrode during discharge - when vacancies accumulate at the Na/ceramic interface - remains to be understood and avoided. The study investigates the underlying mechanism by applying a linear current ramp between two Na metal electrodes separated by a ceramic solid electrolyte to provoke vacancy buildup. Above a critical current density $j_\mathrm{crit}$ the anode voltage no longer increases linearly but in an exponential fashion. Arrhenius analysis of $j_\mathrm{crit}(T)$ for the three solid electrolytes $\mathrm{Na_{1.9}Al_{10.67}Li_{0.33}O_{17}}$, $\mathrm{Na_{3.4}Zr_2Si_{2.4}P_{0.6}O_{12}}$, and $\mathrm{Na_5SmSi_4O_{12}}$ yields an activation energy $E_\mathrm{A}$ of $0.13$ to $0.15\,\mathrm{eV}$. This exceeds the activation energy of $0.053\,\mathrm{eV}$ for the diffusive vacancy migration in bulk Na significantly. Further, $E_\mathrm{A}$ is insensitive to anode microstructure variation. Both observations rule out bulk diffusion as the transport bottleneck. A thin tin-sodium alloy interlayer lowers $E_\mathrm{A}$ to $(0.10\pm0.01)\,\mathrm{eV}$, implicating interfacial thermodynamics as rate-limiting. Sodiophilic, Na-conducting interlayers and low-tension interfaces emerge as key pathways to stable, high-rate Na-SSBs at practical stack pressures.

### [136] [AlphaDiffract: Automated Crystallographic Analysis of Powder X-ray Diffraction Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23367)
*Nina Andrejevic,Ming Du,Hemant Sharma,James P. Horwath,Aileen Luo,Xiangyu Yin,Michael Prince,Brian H. Toby,Mathew J. Cherukara*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: AlphaDiffract是一个深度学习框架，能够直接从粉末X射线衍射（PXRD）图谱中预测晶体系统、空间群和晶格参数，在实验数据上实现了最先进的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从粉末X射线衍射数据中进行材料识别和结构理解是材料科学中长期存在的挑战，而准确确定晶体晶格（包括晶格参数和晶体学对称性）是完整结构解析的先决条件。传统方法需要迭代且通常需要专家输入，而现有深度学习方法虽然显示出潜力，但缺乏从实验数据中全面确定晶格的稳健单次方法。

Method: AlphaDiffract采用ConvNeXt架构的一维适应版本，这是一种整合了transformer关键设计原则的现代卷积神经网络，并配备了针对每个晶体学特性的专用预测头。该模型在迄今为止最大的基于物理的数据集上进行训练，包含超过3100万个模拟衍射图谱，这些图谱通过增强来自ICSD和Materials Project数据库的312,267个精选结构生成。

Result: 该模型在实验数据上表现出强大的泛化能力，在RRUFF数据集上实现了81.7%的晶体系统准确率和66.2%的空间群准确率，同时还能预测所有六个晶格参数。这代表了利用深度学习进行高通量材料发现的重要进展。

Conclusion: 通过提供从PXRD数据中快速准确确定晶格的统一模型，AlphaDiffract代表了利用深度学习进行高通量材料发现的重要进展。

Abstract: Materials identification and structural understanding from powder X-ray diffraction (PXRD) data is a long-standing challenge in materials science, fundamental to discovering and characterizing novel materials. A prerequisite for full structure solution is the accurate determination of the crystal lattice, including lattice parameters and crystallographic symmetries. Traditional methods for this are iterative and typically require expert input, and while existing deep learning approaches have shown promise, a robust, single-shot method for comprehensive lattice determination from experimental data remains a key goal. Here, we introduce AlphaDiffract, a deep learning framework that achieves state-of-the-art performance in predicting the crystal system, space group, and lattice parameters directly from PXRD patterns. AlphaDiffract utilizes a 1D adaptation of the ConvNeXt architecture, a modern convolutional neural network that integrates key design principles from transformers, coupled with dedicated prediction heads for each crystallographic property. The model is trained on the largest-to-date physics-based dataset of over 31 million simulated diffraction patterns, generated by augmenting 312,267 curated structures from the ICSD and Materials Project databases. Crucially, it demonstrates strong generalization to experimental data, achieving 81.7% crystal system accuracy and 66.2% space group accuracy on the RRUFF dataset while additionally predicting all six lattice parameters. By providing a unified model for rapid and accurate lattice determination from PXRD data, AlphaDiffract represents a significant step forward in leveraging deep learning for high-throughput materials discovery.

### [137] [Ultrafast Sintering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23423)
*Jian Luo*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文综述了超快烧结（ultrafast sintering）领域的最新进展，评估了多种实现方法，并指出该技术在探索高熵陶瓷（high-entropy ceramics）等复杂材料体系方面的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在批判性评估超快烧结技术的最新进展，同时指出该领域尚未解决的科学问题和新出现的技术机遇。特别关注理解超快烧结的机制及其在复杂陶瓷材料合成中的应用潜力。

Method: 论文通过分析多种超快烧结方法来实现研究目标，包括快速热退火（rapid thermal annealing）、超快高温烧结（ultrafast high-temperature sintering）、黑光烧结（black light sintering）、大气压等离子体烧结（atmospheric-pressure plasma sintering）和感应超快烧结（induction ultrafast sintering）。这些方法分别采用不同的加热机制，如红外加热、石墨毡加热器、蓝激光或强紫外辐照等。

Result: 研究指出，闪烧（flash sintering）事件始于热-电耦合失控（coupled thermal and electrical runaway），而快速致密化则由超高加热速率和升高的烧结温度共同实现。基于这一理解，已通过多种途径实现了超快烧结，包括反应性超快合成与烧结（reactive ultrafast synthesis and sintering）。

Conclusion: 尽管已提出多种假设，但超快烧结的机制和动力学仍需进一步研究。特别是反应性超快合成与烧结在成分复杂陶瓷（compositionally complex ceramics）领域的应用具有科学意义和技术机遇。超快烧结方法的扩展为高通量材料发现提供了多功能平台，尤其在高熵陶瓷（high-entropy ceramics）等具有广阔成分空间的研究领域。

Abstract: This Perspective critically assesses recent advances in ultrafast sintering and highlights open scientific questions and emerging technological opportunities. Mechanistic studies of flash sintering indicate that the flash event initiates as a coupled thermal and electrical runaway, while rapid densification is enabled by ultrahigh heating rates and elevated sintering temperatures. Building on this understanding, ultrafast sintering has been realized through multiple approaches, including rapid thermal annealing (using intense infrared heating), ultrafast high-temperature sintering (in which specimens are sandwiched between graphite felt heaters), black light sintering (employing blue laser or intense ultraviolet irradiation), atmospheric-pressure plasma sintering, and induction ultrafast sintering (operating in either direct induction or susceptor-heating modes).Reactive ultrafast synthesis and sintering have also been demonstrated. Although several hypotheses have been proposed, the mechanisms governing ultrafast sintering and its kinetics warrant further investigation. In particular, reactive ultrafast synthesis and sintering of compositionally complex ceramics are scientifically intriguing to understand while also presenting technological opportunities. The expanding range of ultrafast sintering methods provides a versatile platform for high-throughput materials discovery, especially in the rapidly growing field of high-entropy and compositionally complex ceramics, which feature vast compositional spaces to explore.

</details>


### [138] [Ferromagnetic Spin Glass State and Anomalous Hall Effect in Topological Semimetal Candidate Mn2Sb2Te5](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23426)
*M. M. Sharma,Ankush Saxena,S. M. Huang,Santosh Karki Chhetri,Jin Hu,V. P. S. Awana*

TL;DR: 该研究通过磁化率、热容和电输运测量，揭示了Mn2Sb2Te5单晶中存在自旋玻璃态和场致铁磁性，并观察到反常霍尔效应，表明其作为磁性外尔半金属候选材料的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究的动机在于探索同时具有磁性和拓扑态的材料，这类材料是量子材料研究的关键前沿。Mn2(Bi/Sb)2Te5体系因其可能同时具有拓扑表面态和本征磁序而成为有前景的磁性外尔半金属（magnetic Weyl semimetal）候选材料。

Method: 研究方法包括对Mn2Sb2Te5单晶进行磁化率测量（magnetization measurements）、热容测量（heat capacity measurement）以及电输运性质表征，特别关注了反常霍尔效应（anomalous Hall effect）的观测。

Result: 磁化测量揭示了自旋玻璃态（spin glass state）和场致铁磁性（field-induced ferromagnetism）。热容测量表明不存在长程磁序，但Mn2Sb2Te5的本征磁化显著影响其电学性质，这通过反常霍尔效应得到证实。

Conclusion: 该工作为理解Mn2Sb2Te5的磁性和电子性质提供了重要见解，确立了Mn2(Bi/Sb)2Te5体系作为探索磁性与非平庸能带拓扑（non-trivial band topology）相互作用的理想平台，能够实现非磁性系统中无法获得的涌现量子相和新型输运响应。

Abstract: Materials that intrinsically possess both magnetism and topological states represent a key frontier of quantum materials research. Recently, Mn2(Bi/Sb)2Te5 has emerged as a promising candidate for hosting topological surface states coupled with intrinsic magnetic order, making it a potential magnetic Weyl semimetal. In this study, we investigate the magnetic and transport properties of Mn2Sb2Te5 single crystals. The magnetization measurements reveal a spin glass state with field-induced ferromagnetism. Although heat capacity measurement indicates the absence of long-range order, the intrinsic magnetization in Mn2Sb2Te5 significantly affects its electrical properties, as demonstrated by the anomalous Hall effect. This work provides valuable insights into the magnetism and the electronic properties of Mn2Sb2Te5, establishing Mn2(Bi/Sb)2Te5 system as a compelling platform for exploring the interplay between magnetism and non-trivial band topology, enabling emergent quantum phases and novel transport responses not accessible in non-magnetic systems.

### [139] [Structural Chart of Copper-Silver Nanoalloys through machine learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23442)
*Manoj Settem,Emanuele Telari,Antonio Tinti,Riccardo Ferrando,Alberto Giacomello*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纳米合金（或合金纳米颗粒）是一类重要的功能材料，但由于缺乏对其亚稳态和稳定结构的信息，设计合成方案以控制其结构和化学有序性具有挑战性。需要开发计算框架来探索纳米合金的结构空间。

Method: 研究开发了通用计算框架，以38原子AgCu纳米合金为模型系统。首先使用并行回火结合分子动力学（parallel tempering combined with molecular dynamics, PTMD）采样平衡结构分布，然后采用机器学习（machine learning, ML）方法将大量采样构型分类为不同结构类别，生成单一三维图谱可视化所有结构和成分。

Conclusion: 该框架为计算和映射多组分纳米颗粒的广阔结构和化学空间提供了有效途径，为功能纳米合金的理性设计铺平了道路。

Abstract: Nanoalloys (or alloy nanoparticles) are an important class of materials that are promising for their functional properties. However, designing synthesis protocols to control their structure and chemical ordering is rather challenging. Part of this difficulty stems from the lack of information on their metastable and stable structures. Here, we develop a general computational framework to construct a structural chart of nanoalloys using 38-atom AgCu nanoalloys as a model system. Initially, the equilibrium structural distribution is sampled using parallel tempering combined with molecular dynamics (PTMD). Using a machine learning (ML) based approach, the vast number of sampled configurations are classified into various structural classes. This ML approach produces a single three-dimensional map in which all structures and compositions can be visualized and discriminated. Finally, a finite-temperature structural chart is constructed which provides information on the dominant structures across the entire range of compositions and temperatures. In addition, the structural chart reveals significant differences in thermal stability between nanoalloys and bulk alloys. The presented framework provides an effective route to compute and map the vast structural and chemical space of multicomponent nanoparticles, paving the way to the rational design of functional nanoalloys.

### [140] [Quantum Saturation of the Electro-Optic Effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23486)
*Aiden Ross,Sankalpa Hazra,Albert Suceava,Dylan Sotir,Darrell G. Schlom,Venkatraman Gopalan,Long-Qing Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过利用量子涨落（quantum fluctuations）调控铁电相边界至0K，实现了在低温下（25K以下）保持大且温度不敏感的电光效应，为量子计算等低温应用提供了高性能电光材料设计原则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 未来量子计算架构需要能在低温下保持强而稳定性能的电光材料。传统电光材料的大电光系数通常局限于结构相变附近的狭窄温度窗口，温度微小变化会导致电光响应大幅波动。

Method: 采用热力学分析、相场模拟、实验生长和低温光学测量相结合的方法。通过应变（在BaTiO3中）或化学成分（在Ba1-xCaxTiO3中）调控铁电相边界至0K，利用量子涨落诱导饱和区域。

Result: 量子涨落诱导出饱和区域，使大电光响应在25K以下几乎不随温度变化。该低温电光效应与室温下块体BaTiO3相当，性能超过BaTiO3-on-Si一个数量级以上。

Conclusion: 这些发现为工程化高性能低温电光材料建立了通用设计原则，通过调控相边界至0K并利用量子涨落，可实现大且温度不敏感的电光响应。

Abstract: Future quantum computing architectures require electro-optic materials that maintain a strong, stable performance at cryogenic temperatures. In conventional electro-optic materials, large electro-optic coefficients are often confined to narrow temperature windows near structural phase transitions, where small changes in temperature lead to large changes in the electro-optic response. Using thermodynamic analysis, phase-field simulations, experimental growth and cryogenic optical measurements we show that quantum fluctuations can be harnessed to overcome this trade-off. By tuning the ferroelectric phase boundaries down to 0 K, quantum fluctuations induce a saturation regime in which a large electro-optic response becomes nearly temperature-independent below 25 K. We demonstrate that the phase boundaries can be tuned through either strain in BaTiO3 or through chemical composition in Ba1-xCaxTiO3, leading to a large, temperature insensitive, cryogenic electro-optic effect comparable to bulk BaTiO3 at room temperature; the performance exceeds BaTiO3-on-Si by over an order of magnitude. These findings establish a general design principle for engineering high-performance electro-optic materials for cryogenic applications.

</details>


### [141] [Active learning-enabled multi-objective design of thermally conductive and mechanically compliant polymers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23494)
*Yuhan Liu,Jiaxin Xu,Renzheng Zhang,Meng Jiang,Tengfei Luo*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究开发了一个基于多目标贝叶斯优化（MOBO）的主动学习（AL）框架，用于发现同时具备高热导率（TC）和低体积模量的聚合物材料，通过结合分子动力学（MD）模拟与机器学习方法，从大型未标记数据库中高效筛选出六个帕累托前沿候选材料。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 聚合物因其机械柔顺性和加工性在柔性电子和热界面材料中具有应用潜力，但传统聚合物热导率较低限制了其散热性能。同时实现高本征热导率和机械柔性的聚合物识别仍具挑战性。

Method: 开发了基于多目标贝叶斯优化（MOBO）的主动学习（AL）框架，首先通过高通量分子动力学（MD）流程生成初始数据集，训练独立的深度核学习（DKL）代理模型预测热导率和体积模量及其不确定性。使用并行噪声期望超体积改进（qNEHVI）采集函数迭代筛选大型未标记聚合物数据库，系统推荐新候选材料进行MD评估，并用新获取数据更新DKL模型。

Result: 最终在帕累托前沿（Pareto front）上识别出六个候选材料，代表了热导率与模量之间的最优权衡。可解释性分析揭示了与这些权衡相关的分子特征，可合成性评估支持了所选候选材料的实际相关性。

Conclusion: 通过结合分子动力学模拟与主动学习驱动的多目标贝叶斯优化，该工作流程缓解了数据稀缺问题，减少了开发时间，并为设计针对不同应用的多功能聚合物提供了可操作的指导。

Abstract: Polymers are attractive in applications like flexible electronics and thermal interface materials due to their mechanical compliance and processability. However, conventional polymers have low thermal conductivity (TC), limiting their heat dissipation performance. Identifying polymers that simultaneously achieve high intrinsic TC and mechanical flexibility (i.e., low modulus) remains a challenge. Here, we develop an active learning (AL) framework based on multi-objective Bayesian optimization (MOBO) to discover polymers exhibiting both high TC and low bulk modulus. Initially, a high-throughput molecular dynamics (MD) pipeline generated an initial dataset, and independent Deep Kernel Learning (DKL) surrogate models were trained for TC and bulk modulus to predict properties and uncertainties. Using the parallel noisy expected hypervolume improvement (qNEHVI) acquisition function, the framework iteratively screens a larger unlabeled polymer database, systematically recommends new polymer candidates for MD evaluation, and updates the DKL models with newly acquired data. Ultimately, six candidates were identified on the Pareto front, representing optimal trade-offs between TC and modulus. Interpretability analysis further revealed molecular features associated with these trade-offs, and synthesizability assessment supported the practical relevance of the selected candidates. By combining MD simulations with AL-enabled MOBO, our workflow mitigates data scarcity, reduces development time, and provides actionable guidance for designing multifunctional polymers tailored for different applications.

### [142] [Finite compressibility and strain hardening in elasto-plastic models of amorphous matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22684)
*A. Elgailani,D. Vandembroucq,C. E. Maloney*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过介观弹塑性模型探究非晶态物质在不同压缩模量比（K/μ）下的力学响应，揭示了Eshelby背应力在循环剪切和稳态剪切中的关键作用，以及硬化行为的自发涌现机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解非晶态物质（如非晶合金）中压缩模量与剪切模量比值（K/μ）变化对力学行为的影响，特别是在循环剪切和稳态剪切条件下。该参数可随成分、时效、淬火工艺或机械加工历史而变化。

Method: 采用介观弹塑性模型（mesoscopic elasto-plastic model）研究不同无量纲压缩模量（K/μ）的非晶态物质。研究包括振幅为Γ的循环剪切和正向稳态剪切两种加载模式。

Result: 在循环剪切中，随着Γ增加出现三种终端行为：弹性、滞回但微观可逆、扩散不可逆。Eshelby背应力（σ₀）决定了弹性到滞回的转变点Γ₀，该点与泊松比相关。较低K/μ（更可压缩）的系统具有更高的Γ₀和更宽的纯弹性区。在正向剪切中，较低K/μ导致更高的稳态流动应力σ_y。模型还自发涌现了复杂的硬化行为：在Γ₀处发生运动硬化到各向同性硬化的转变。

Conclusion: Eshelby背应力对泊松比的依赖性是非晶态物质塑性响应的关键机制，而非传统认为的自由体积过剩。该发现对K/μ可变的非晶金属合金或其他玻璃态系统具有重要启示，为理解其力学行为提供了新视角。

Abstract: We study a mesoscopic elasto-plastic model of amorphous matter with varying dimensionless compression modulus, $K/μ$, where $K$ and $μ$ are the compression and shear moduli. We study both cyclic shear with amplitude $Γ$ and forward steady shear. In cyclic shear, the terminal behavior is, in order of increasing $Γ$: i) trivially elastic, ii) hysteretic but with microscopically reversible limit cycles, iii) diffusive with no return to previously visited configurations. We show that the transition between i) and ii) at the onset point $Γ_0$ is determined by the Eshelby back stress, $σ_0$, which depends on the Poisson ratio. Systems with smaller $K/μ$ (more compressible) are effectively harder with a higher $Γ_0$ and a correspondingly larger purely elastic regime in cyclic loading. In forward shear, $σ_0$ plays a similar role where lower $K/μ$ results in a higher steady state flow stress, $σ_y$. We show that increasing $K/μ$ increases the amplitude of stress redistribution after a local yielding event without changing the net stress relaxation and relate this to the assumptions in mean-field descriptions of amorphous solids. A striking feature of the model is the emergence of a complex hardening behavior in the absence of any ad-hoc hardening parameters: a transition between a kinematic and an isotropic hardening behavior precisely at $Γ_0$ associated with the hysteresis transition. The enhanced plastic response for incompressible systems is also seen in amorphous alloys where it is usually attributed to excess free volume, while in the present model, it arises from the dependence of the Eshelby backstress on the Poisson ratio. Our results should have important implications for amorphous metallic alloys or other glassy systems where $K/μ$ can vary with composition, age, quench procedure, or mechanical processing history.

</details>


### [143] [Cooperative effect of local active stresses on the macroscopic contractility of elastic fiber networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22926)
*Abhinav Kumar,David A. Quint,Kinjal Dasbiswas*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了嵌入弹性生物聚合物网络中的主动收缩单元如何通过非线性方式增强网络宏观应力，发现不仅收缩单元数量，其局部几何构型也显著影响网络的硬化转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解嵌入弹性生物聚合物网络中的主动收缩单元集体行为如何调控网络宏观力学响应，特别是分子马达（molecular motors）在细胞骨架或粘附细胞在细胞外基质中通过局部调节主动力生成单元来调控网络尺度非线性弹性特性的物理机制。

Method: 采用模型弹性纤维网络，研究宏观边界应力如何依赖于嵌入收缩单元的数量和性质（每个单元施加各向同性力偶极子），以及纤维的弯曲刚度。通过有效介质理论（effective medium theory）将增强的收缩性与力偶极子施加约束导致的网络有效平均配位数增加联系起来。

Result: 宏观应力随偶极子数量非线性增加，源于初始柔软、弯曲主导网络的相互硬化。比较三种具有不同局部结构的力偶极子模型，发现主动单元约束网络的具体方式强烈影响硬化转变的开始和性质。

Conclusion: 不仅力生成单元的数量，其局部几何构型也关键决定宏观力学行为。该框架为理解生物系统如何通过局部调节主动力生成单元来调控网络尺度非线性弹性特性提供了物理基础。

Abstract: The collective action of actively contractile units embedded in elastic biopolymer networks plays a crucial role in regulating the network's macroscopic mechanical response. Here, we investigate how the macroscopic boundary stress in model elastic fiber networks depends on the number and nature of embedded contractile units, each exerting an isotropic force dipole, as well as on the bending stiffness of fibers. We find that the macroscopic stress increases nonlinearly with the number of dipoles due to mutual stiffening of initially soft, bending-dominated networks. Using effective medium theory, we relate this enhanced contractility to an increase in the effective average network coordination number due to constraints imposed by the force dipoles. By comparing three distinct force dipole models that differ in their local structures, we demonstrate that the specific manner in which an active unit constrains the network strongly influences the onset and nature of the stiffening transition. Our results highlight that not only the quantity but also the local geometry of force-generating units critically determines the macroscopic mechanical behavior. This framework provides a physical basis for understanding how biological systems-such as molecular motors in the cytoskeleton, or adherent cells in the extracellular matrix-can modulate network-scale nonlinear elastic properties through local tuning of active force-generating units.
