### [144] [Template-free fabrication of reconfigurable magnetic micropillars and filaments through controlled Nanoflower assembly and actuation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23102)
*Caterina Landi,Rosa Pérez-Garrido,Julio Marco Cuenca,Javier Tajuelo,Chantal Valeriani,Helena Gavilán,Fernando Martínez-Pedrero*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一种基于磁性纳米花（MNFs）的无模板自组装平台，通过调控粒子间相互作用、外加磁场和空间约束，实现了动态、场响应型微结构的可控制备，为微流控操作和生物微机器人应用提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁性纳米花（magnetic nanoflowers, MNFs）因其在临床相关交变磁场下具有大的固有磁损耗和高比吸收率，展现出作为磁热疗高效介质的巨大潜力。本研究旨在建立一个通用平台，通过无模板自组装策略创建基于MNFs的动态、场响应型微结构。

Method: 采用灵活、低成本的无模板自组装策略，通过调控粒子间相互作用、外加磁场和空间约束来实现微结构构建。通过控制离子强度、粒子覆盖率、表面电荷、粒子浓度和空间约束等参数，使MNFs在水溶液中自发组装成磁性微柱和微丝。使用L-多巴胺（L-DOPA）进行表面修饰，因其是提供儿茶酚、胺和羧酸盐基团的生物相容性配体。

Result: MNFs可在水溶液中自发组装成磁性微柱和微丝，低离子强度有利于可逆组装，中等盐浓度则产生稳定、不可逆结构。这些结构的尺寸、几何形状和动态响应可精确调控，实现纤毛样旋转、振荡等场诱导行为，以及微柱扭矩驱动脱离形成独立游动的微丝。MNFs@L-DOPA具有负表面电荷，在磁驱动下表现出与未涂层系统相似的组装行为。

Conclusion: 该研究为无模板设计仿生、功能性磁性和细长微结构建立了实用指导原则，突显了其在微流控操作和生物微机器人应用中的潜力。这些结果为构建动态响应型微系统提供了新的设计框架。

Abstract: Magnetic nanoflowers (MNFs), which exhibit large intrinsic magnetic losses and high specific absorption rates under clinically relevant alternating magnetic fields, highlight strong potential as efficient mediators for magnetic hyperthermia. In this work, we provide a versatile platform for creating dynamic, field-responsive microstructures based on MNFs through a flexible, low-cost, and template-free self-assembly strategy driven by tunable interparticle interactions, external magnetic fields, and spatial confinement. By controlling ionic strength, particle coverage, surface charge, particle concentration, and confinement, MNFs spontaneously assemble in aqueous solution into magnetic micropillars and microfilaments without predefined scaffolds, with low ionic strength favoring reversible assemblies and intermediate salt concentrations yielding stable, irreversible structures. The size, geometry, and dynamic response of these architectures can be precisely tuned, enabling field-induced behaviors such as cilia-like rotations, oscillations, and torque-driven detachment of micropillars into free-standing, swarming microfilaments. L-dopamine (L-DOPA) was used for surface modification in this work, as it is a biocompatible ligand offering catechol, amine, and carboxylate groups. Resulting MNFs@L-DOPA have negative surface charge and show assembly behavior qualitatively similar to the uncoated system under magnetic actuation. Together, these results establish practical guidelines for the template-free design of biomimetic, functional magnetic and elongated microarchitectures, highlighting their potential for microfluidic manipulation and bio-microrobotic applications.

</details>


### [145] [Where Humpty Dumpty Breaks: Geometry-Driven Fracture in Ellipsoidal Shells](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23349)
*Naoki Sekiya,Yuri Akiba,Kai Kageyama,Hokuto Nagatakiya,Ryuichi Tarumi,Tomohiko G. Sano*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了壳体曲率作为断裂形态的几何蓝图，通过内部加压双层球壳实验，证明了裂纹网络形态多样性取决于极地与赤道的曲率比，并建立了结构曲率与断裂之间的直接联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 断裂网络在自然界中普遍存在，但一个能够系统解释表面几何如何规定不同断裂形态之间转变的统一框架仍然缺乏。研究旨在探索壳体曲率如何作为断裂的几何蓝图，控制复杂裂纹网络的演化。

Method: 通过内部加压薄双层球壳（thin, bilayer spheroidal shells）进行实验，分析裂纹形态多样性如何依赖于极地与赤道的曲率比（curvature ratio）。研究将非线性几何与经典的格里菲斯（Griffith）和冯·米塞斯（von Mises）准则相结合。

Result: 研究发现丰富的裂纹形态多样性（横向、纵向和随机取向）取决于曲率比，这些模式源于壳体的非线性力学，可用于有效控制裂纹生长。在成熟的甜瓜和木卫二冰壳中观察到的不同断裂模式遵循相同的几何原理。

Conclusion: 研究建立了结构曲率与断裂之间的直接联系，提供了一个整合非线性几何与经典断裂准则的预测框架。这一对裂纹形态发生的统一理解将为抗断裂新型功能材料的设计原则提供信息，并为弯曲生物和地球物理结构的力学性能提供见解。

Abstract: Fracture networks are ubiquitous in nature, spanning scales from millimeter-sized cracks in botanical peels to hundred-kilometer-long lineae on planetary satellites. The propagation of a crack is a complex, nonlinear phenomenon governed by the interplay of mechanical properties, rheological behavior, and system geometry. While fracture mechanics has long addressed structural failure, the relationship among fracture, elasticity, and nonlinear geometry has recently revived as a focal point in condensed matter and biophysics. However, a unified framework that systematically explains how surface geometry prescribes the transition between disparate fracture morphologies remains elusive. Here we show that shell curvature provides a geometric blueprint for fracture, governing the evolution of complex crack networks through induced stress anisotropy. By internally pressurizing thin, bilayer spheroidal shells, we demonstrate that a rich diversity of crack morphologies across lateral, longitudinal, and random orientations depends on the curvature ratio between the pole and the equator. We find that these patterns arise from the nonlinear mechanics of the shell, which can be leveraged to effectively control crack growth. Our results establish a direct link between structural curvature and fractures, providing a predictive framework that integrates nonlinear geometry with the classical Griffith and von Mises criteria. Beyond our model system, we find that the disparate fracture patterns observed in ripening muskmelons and in the icy crust of Europa follow the same geometric principles. We expect that this unified understanding of crack morphogenesis will inform the design principles of novel functional materials that are resilient to fracture and provide insights into the mechanical performance of curved biological and geophysical architectures.

</details>


### [146] [Thickness effects in the electromechanical stability of charged biological membranes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23477)
*Sirui Ning,Yannick A. D. Omar,Karthik Shekhar,Kranthi K. Mandadapu*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种统一的理论框架，用于描述带电脂质双层膜在电场作用下的失稳机制，该框架同时考虑了有限膜厚度、表面电荷和体相电流体动力学效应，揭示了在生理条件下有限厚度效应的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解电场如何破坏生物膜对于电穿孔技术和生物电子界面至关重要，但现有理论描述存在碎片化问题。现有理论要么处理有限厚度膜的静电学，要么处理理想零厚度界面的电流体动力学，缺乏一个统一框架同时纳入有限膜厚度、表面电荷和体相电流体动力学效应。

Method: 应用最近开发的降维框架，该框架捕捉了控制带电脂质双层膜高度波动的耦合电流体动力学和力学效应。膜厚度为δ，电解质以德拜屏蔽长度λ表征，推导了电压和电荷依赖的有效表面张力和弯曲刚度的重整化，以及控制波动不稳定性的色散关系。

Result: 在生理屏蔽条件下（δ/λ∼4），有限厚度产生的牵引力矩贡献占总静电修正的70%以上。理论进一步揭示表面电荷在生理离子强度下可以稳定膜，增加有效张力，并以依赖于双层小叶间电荷不对称性的方式改变电穿孔阈值。

Conclusion: 该统一理论框架将先前众多理论结果作为其更一般理论的极限情况，当忽略有限厚度效应或屏蔽极强时。关键新贡献来自有限膜厚度产生的牵引力矩，这些在零厚度描述中不存在，对生理条件下的膜稳定性有重要影响。

Abstract: Understanding how electric fields destabilize biological membranes is important for electroporation-based technologies and bioelectronic interfaces. However, theoretical descriptions of this phenomenon remain fragmented. Existing theories treat either electrostatics in membranes of finite thickness or electrohydrodynamic flows at idealized zero-thickness interfaces, leaving unresolved a unified description that simultaneously incorporates finite membrane thickness, surface charge, and bulk electrohydrodynamics. Here, we apply a recently-developed, dimension-reduction framework that captures the coupled electrohydrodynamic and mechanical effects governing height fluctuations of a charged lipid bilayer of thickness $δ$ in an electrolyte characterized by Debye screening length $λ$. We derive voltage- and charge-dependent renormalizations of the effective surface tension and bending rigidity, along with a dispersion relation governing undulatory instabilities. A wide range of prior theoretical results arise as limiting cases of our more general theory when finite-thickness effects are neglected or screening is asymptotically strong. The key new contribution arises from traction moments generated across the finite membrane thickness, which are absent in zero-thickness descriptions. Under physiological screening ($δ/λ\sim 4$), these contributions account for more than $>70\%$ of the total electrostatic correction to both surface tension and bending rigidity. The theory further reveals that surface charges can stabilize the membrane at physiological ionic strengths, increasing the effective tension and shifting electroporation thresholds in a manner that depends on charge asymmetry between the leaflets.

### [147] [Path Integral Monte Carlo on a Sphere](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22338)
*Riccardo Fantoni*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究通过数值精确求解量子广义相对论的简化玩具模型，在恒定正曲率球面上研究量子多体系统的热平衡性质。采用路径积分蒙特卡洛方法测量了低温下球面上玻色子、费米子和任意子流体的动能、内能和静态结构，并分析了曲率对多体流体热力学和结构性质的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是数值精确求解量子广义相对论的简化玩具模型，更准确地说是弯曲空间上的路径积分。具体关注恒定正曲率球面上量子多体问题的热平衡性质，探索曲率对量子流体行为的影响。

Method: 采用路径积分蒙特卡洛（path integral Monte Carlo）方法测量低温下球面上玻色子、费米子和任意子流体的动能、内能和静态结构。对于费米子和任意子，使用受限路径积分（restricted path integral）方案克服符号问题（sign problem）。对于玻色子，还测量了超流分数。

Result: 计算机实验演化过程中多体路径构型的快照显示，由于庞加莱的"毛球定理"（hairy ball theorem），单粒子路径在极点附近的"速度"减慢。对于玻色子，将临界温度下的超流分数行为与Nelson和Kosterlitz在平直空间热力学极限下超流相变中预测的普适跳跃进行比较。研究了曲率对多体流体热力学和结构性质的影响。

Conclusion: 该研究成功数值求解了弯曲空间上的量子多体模型，揭示了曲率对量子流体行为的显著影响。受限路径积分方案对于非相互作用流体是精确的，但对于相互作用系统仅是一个近似，文中以低温电子气为例说明了这一点。

Abstract: We solve numerically exactly a simple toy model to quantum general relativity or more properly to path integral on a curved space. We consider the thermal equilibrium of a quantum many body problem on the sphere, the surface of constant positive curvature. We use path integral Monte Carlo to measure the kinetic energy, the internal energy and the static structure of a bosons, fermions and anyons fluid at low temperatures on the sphere. For bosons we also measure the superfluid fraction and compare its behavior at the critical temperature with the universal jump predicted by Nelson and Kosterlitz in flat space in the thermodynamic limit at the superfluid phase transition. For fermions and anyons it is necessary to use the restricted path integral recipe in order to overcome the sign problem. Even if this recipe is exact for the non interacting fluid it reduces to just an approximation for an interacting system. And we make the example of the electron gas at low temperature. Snapshots of the many body path configuration during the evolution of the computer experiment show that the ``speed'' of the single particle path near the poles slows down as a consequence of the ``hairy ball theorem'' of Poincaré. The influence of curvature on the thermodynamic and structural properties of the many body fluid is also studied.

</details>


### [148] [Transformation of the Talbot effect in response to phase disorder](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23026)
*Ilia Mosaki,A. V. Turlapov*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究分析了玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensates）链在自由膨胀时的干涉现象，揭示了初始相位无序（phase disorder）如何改变干涉图样并产生新的频谱峰，这些峰源于凝聚体对的干涉效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解初始相位无序对玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体链自由膨胀干涉现象的影响，特别是探究当初始相位不完全相同时，干涉图样如何变化以及新频谱峰的产生机制。

Method: 通过理论推导，建立了任意相位无序情况下空间密度分布频谱的解析表达式，并分析了新频谱峰与凝聚体对干涉产生的密度调制（wavelets）之间的对应关系。

Result: 研究发现，即使轻微的初始相位无序也会显著改变干涉图样，导致空间密度分布频谱出现新的峰值。这些新峰源于凝聚体对的干涉效应，其位置与这类干涉产生的密度调制波矢（wave vectors）一致。

Conclusion: 初始相位无序通过引入凝聚体对的干涉效应，在频谱中产生新的峰值；而当初始相位完全相同时，这些干涉产生的波列（wavelets）在叠加时相互抵消，导致相应峰值的缺失。

Abstract: Bose-Einstein condensates initially arranged in a long chain freely expand and interfere. If the initial phases of the condensates are identical, the initial density distribution is restored periodically during the expansion, giving rise to the Talbot effect. Even a slight disorder in the initial phases leads to a transformation of the interference pattern. In response to the phase disorder, the spectrum of the spatial density distribution acquires peaks that are absent in the case of identical phases. We derive an analytical expression for the spectrum of the spatial density distribution for an arbitrary phase disorder. We show that the new peaks emerging due to the phase disorder originate from pairwise interferences of the condensates. The positions of these peaks coincide with the wave vectors of the density modulations (wavelets) generated by such pairwise interferences. The absence of these peaks, when the initial phases are identical, is explained by the mutual destruction of the overlapping wavelets during their summation.

</details>


### [149] [Occupation-selective topological pumping from Floquet gauge fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23307)
*Wenjie Liu,Ching Hua Lee,Zhoutao Lei*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了占据数选择性拓扑泵浦（occupation-selective topological pumping）的新机制，其中密度依赖的隧穿动力学使双体束缚态（doublons）获得与单粒子不同的陈数（Chern numbers），从而在单粒子泵浦平凡时实现量子化输运。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统拓扑泵浦（topological pumping）受单粒子能带拓扑支配，本研究旨在探索当隧穿成为动力学、占据数依赖变量时，如何从根本上重塑这一范式，实现占据数选择性的拓扑响应。

Method: 采用周期性驱动的一维超晶格（one-dimensional superlattice）模型，其中隧穿具有密度依赖性（density-dependent hopping），通过分析双体束缚态（two-body bound states）的拓扑性质，并提出了基于超冷原子（ultracold atoms）的Floquet实现方案。

Result: 双体束缚态获得与单粒子不同的陈数，即使在单粒子泵浦平凡时也能展示量子化输运，包括反向传播响应；动力学规范场（dynamical-gauge-field）机制在束缚态能区诱导拓扑相变，并将贝里曲率（Berry curvature）集中到局域共振区域而不破坏绝热量子化。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了占据数选择性拓扑响应的新机制，该机制可扩展到更高占据数的束缚态，为拓扑物态调控提供了新途径，并提出了超冷原子实验实现方案。

Abstract: Topological pumping is conventionally governed by single-particle band topology. Here we show that promoting tunneling to a dynamical, occupation-conditioned variable fundamentally reshapes this paradigm, leading to occupation-selective topological pumping. In a periodically driven one-dimensional superlattice with density-dependent hopping, two-body bound states (doublons) acquire Chern numbers distinct from those of single particles and exhibit quantized transport even when the single-particle pump is trivial, including counter-propagating responses. We identify a dynamical-gauge-field mechanism that induces topological phase transitions in the bound-state sector absent from the single-particle spectrum. Furthermore, the gauge field concentrates Berry curvature into sharply localized resonant regions without compromising adiabatic quantization. A Floquet realization with ultracold atoms is proposed to realize such occupation-selective pumping. Our results reveal a mechanism for occupation-selective topological responses that can persist across higher-occupancy bound states.

</details>


### [150] [Intercavity phonons and dynamics in coupled polariton cavities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23479)
*Iliana Carmona-Moreno,Grover Andrade-Sánchez,Hugo A Lara-García,Giuseppe Pirruccio,Arturo Camacho-Guardian*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过共振驱动中间极化激元支（middle polariton branch），研究系统在包含相互作用情况下的动力学演化，分析其Bogoliubov激发模式。

Result: 共振驱动导致系统进入抑制相干拉比振荡（coherent Rabi oscillations）的独特动力学机制，系统单调演化至稳态。相互作用下，该机制支持低动量下具有类声子色散（phonon-like dispersion）的Bogoliubov激发。

Conclusion: 腔间极化激元在特定驱动条件下展现出独特的非振荡动力学，其集体激发模式既继承了激子分量的相互作用，又保持了准粒子的腔间本质特性。

Abstract: Intercavity polaritons, hybrid quasiparticles with spatially separated photonic and excitonic components, provide a platform to engineer structured light-matter states. We show that resonant driving of the middle polariton branch leads to a qualitatively distinct dynamical regime in which coherent Rabi oscillations are suppressed, and the system evolves monotonically toward its steady state. Including interactions, we demonstrate that this regime supports Bogoliubov excitations with a phonon-like dispersion at low momenta. These collective modes inherit interactions from the excitonic fraction, while preserving the intrinsically intercavity nature of the quasiparticles.

### [151] [Gaussian mixtures and non-parametric likelihoods through the lens of statistical mechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23196)
*Subhroshekhar Ghosh,Adityanand Guntuboyina,Satyaki Mukherjee,Hoang-Son Tran*

Main category: math.ST

TL;DR: 该研究从统计力学视角分析高斯混合模型（GMM）和非参数最大似然估计（NPMLE），建立了超越现有技术的稳定性保证，获得了NPMLE估计量与真实分布之间Kullback-Leibler散度的上界，并揭示了与统计力学中混沌和多谷现象的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于从统计力学（statistical mechanics）视角重新审视高斯混合模型（Gaussian Mixture Models, GMM）和非参数最大似然估计（non-parametric maximum likelihood estimation, NPMLE）问题。当前文献中NPMLE估计量与真实分布之间的Kullback-Leibler散度保证具有挑战性，需要建立超越现有技术的稳定性保证。

Method: 研究方法的核心是分析高斯混合密度对数的函数类复杂性（function class complexity），该方法能够处理其无界性。同时建立了NPMLE问题中的稳定性现象与统计力学模型中随机能量景观（random energy landscapes）的混沌（chaos）和多谷（multiple valleys）概念之间的对应关系。

Result: 研究获得了NPMLE与真实密度之间Kullback-Leibler散度的高概率上界，其阶为min{(log n)^{d+2}/n, log n/√n}，覆盖了n和d相对大小的广泛场景。对于NPMLE问题的近似解也获得了类似保证，解决了优化算法在有限时间内停止的现实情况。

Conclusion: 该研究建立的对应关系可能对统计学和机器学习中的各种随机优化问题具有广泛用途，特别是与这些模型的集中现象（concentration phenomena）和Langevin动力学的技术要素之间的联系。高斯混合密度对数函数类复杂性的分析具有更广泛的学术价值。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate Gaussian Mixture Models ({\it abbrv} GMM) and the related problem of non parametric maximum likelihood estimation ({\it abbrv} NPMLE) from the perspective of statistical mechanics. In particular, we establish stability guarantees for the NPMLE procedure that extend well beyond the state of the art. Crucially, we obtain guarantees on the Kullback-Leibler divergence between NPMLE estimators and the ground truth, a type of result which has been known to be challenging in the literature on this problem.
  In particular, we provide high probability upper bounds on the KL divergence between the NPMLE and the true density that are of the order of $\min\big\{\frac{(\log n)^{d+2}}{n} , \frac{\log n}{\sqrt n}\big\}$, which cover a wide range of scenarios for the comparative sizes of $n$ and $d$. We obtain similar guarantees for approximate solutions to the NPMLE problem, addressing realistic situations wherein optimization algorithms need to be stopped in finite time, allowing access only to approximations to the true NPMLE. A technical cornerstone of our approach is an analysis of the function class complexity of logarithms of gaussian mixture densities, which is able to handle their unboundedness, and could be of wider interest.
  We also establish correspondences between stability phenomena in the NPMLE problem and concepts from chaos and multiple valleys in random energy landscapes of statistical mechanics models. We believe that these correspondences may be useful for a wide variety of random optimization problems in statistics and machine learning, especially the connections to the the technical ingredients of concentration phenomena and Langevin dynamics for these models.

</details>

### [152] [Simultaneous measurement of pressure-dependent bulk and interfacial thermal properties in thermal interface materials using square-pulsed source thermoreflectance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22733)
*Tao Chen,Xin Qian,Puqing Jiang*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 本研究开发了一种方波脉冲源热反射（SPS）方法，能够同时测定热界面材料（TIMs）在机械载荷下的热导率（k）、体积热容（C）和界面热阻（ITR），解决了现有稳态或瞬态技术无法同时测量这些参数的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 热界面材料（thermal interface materials, TIMs）对电子芯片到散热器的热耗散至关重要，但其热导率、体积热容和界面热阻会随机械压力变化，现有稳态或瞬态技术无法同时测定这些参数。因此，体压缩（bulk compaction）和界面接触（interfacial contact）在TIM组件热传输中的耦合作用尚未得到充分解析。

Method: 本研究提出方波脉冲源热反射（square-pulsed source thermoreflectance, SPS）方法，在受控机械载荷下同时测定TIM堆栈的k、C和ITR。通过将方波调制频率（square-wave modulation frequencies）从1 Hz扩展到10 MHz，SPS能够探测广泛的穿透深度，从而区分TIM体热扩散和Al/TIM接触界面的热传输。

Result: 对导热凝胶（thermally conductive gel）、导热垫（thermal pad）和高真空脂（high-vacuum grease）在压缩-卸载循环中的测量揭示了不同的压力依赖性热传输机制。凝胶和垫表现出k和C增加、ITR降低以及显著的滞后现象，表明加载循环中体致密化（bulk densification）和持久界面顺应性（persistent interfacial conformity）的耦合作用。相比之下，润滑脂显示出几乎与压力无关的体特性，但ITR具有强烈的压力依赖性，符合界面主导响应（interface-dominated response）。

Conclusion: 这些结果解决了长期存在的挑战，即同时量化机械载荷TIM组件中的体和界面热传输，为电子封装中实验约束的热管理和可靠性分析提供了可能。

Abstract: Thermal interface materials (TIMs) critically regulate heat dissipation from electronic chips to heat spreaders, yet their thermal conductivity (k), volumetric heat capacity (C), and interfacial thermal resistance (ITR) evolve with mechanical pressure and cannot be determined simultaneously using existing steady-state or transient techniques. As a result, the coupled roles of bulk compaction and interfacial contact in governing heat transport in TIM assemblies remain poorly resolved. Here, we present a square-pulsed source (SPS) thermoreflectance method that enables simultaneous determination of k, C, and ITR in TIM stacks under controlled mechanical loading. By spanning square-wave modulation frequencies from 1 Hz to 10 MHz, SPS probes a broad range of thermal penetration depths, enabling distinction between heat diffusion in the TIM bulk and interfacial heat transfer at the Al/TIM contact. Measurements on a thermally conductive gel, a thermal pad, and a high-vacuum grease during compression-unloading cycles reveal distinct pressure-dependent thermal transport mechanisms. The gel and pad exhibit increases in k and C, reduced ITR, and pronounced hysteresis, indicating coupled bulk densification and persistent interfacial conformity during loading cycles. In contrast, the grease shows nearly pressure-independent bulk properties but a strong pressure dependence of ITR, consistent with an interface-dominated response. These results resolve the long-standing challenge of simultaneously quantifying bulk and interfacial thermal transport in mechanically loaded TIM assemblies, enabling experimentally constrained thermal management and reliability analysis in electronic packaging.

</details>


### [153] [Physics-Informed AI for Laser-Enhanced Contact Optimization in Silicon PV: Electrothermal Activation, Degradation Regimes, and Process Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23351)
*Donald Intal,Abasifreke U. Ebong*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 激光增强接触优化（LECO）是一种用于降低先进晶体硅太阳能电池接触电阻和恢复填充因子的方法，但其工业可转移性受到界面态动力学不稳定性的限制。本文提出了一种预测性工作流程，将瞬态电热建模与可靠性分类相结合，以区分稳定优化、边际激活和潜在损伤。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 激光增强接触优化（Laser-enhanced contact optimization, LECO）在先进晶体硅太阳能电池中应用日益广泛，但相同的局部激活在改善载流子传输的同时，也可能产生动力学不稳定的界面态，这限制了该技术的工业可转移性。

Method: 本文提出了一种耦合多物理场过程的预测性工作流程，包括：（i）将瞬态电热建模（transient electrothermal modeling）简化为状态指标；（ii）分析有效扩散深度和局部面能量密度；（iii）在配方空间中传播校准阈值。该方法使用瞬时状态图和时间依赖性漂移的可靠性分类。

Result: 该框架能够区分稳定优化、边际激活和潜在损伤，并解释了为什么细线缩放和含铜堆叠会通过电流局域化和扩散势垒约束来收紧稳定性裕度。该方法将微观结构证据与器件级特征联系起来。

Conclusion: 本文总结了一种下一代人工智能引导的优化数字孪生（AI guided optimization digital twin）框架，为激光增强接触优化提供了系统性的预测和可靠性评估方法。

Abstract: Laser-enhanced contact optimization (LECO) is increasingly used method to reduce contact resistance and recover fill factor in advanced crystalline silicon solar cells. However, the industrial transferability is limited because the same localized activation that improves carrier transport can also create kinetically unstable interface states. LECO can be viewed as a coupled Multiphysics process that links microstructural evidence to device-level signature that uses instantaneous regime map together with a reliability classification based on time-dependent drift. Thus, a predictive workflow is outlined in the review that couples (i) transient electrothermal modeling to reduced state metrics, (ii) effective diffusion depth and local areal energy density, and (iii) propagated calibrated thresholds across recipe space. The framework separates stable optimization from marginal activation and latent damage and explains why fine-line scaling and copper-containing stacks tighten stability margins through current localization and diffusion-barrier constraints. It sum up the next generation AI guided optimization digital twin.

### [154] [Casimir Geometry as a Probe of Short Range Forces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22413)
*Xiaolin Ma,Volodymyr Takhistov,Hideo Iizuka*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究证明卡西米尔几何构型可作为独立观测量，首次从球-球和板-板几何构型推导出对短程力的约束，完善了卡西米尔几何的标准集，为λ≲10⁻⁸米范围提供了最严格的约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 卡西米尔力（Casimir force）探测是研究短程相互作用最灵敏的实验手段之一，但现有约束几乎完全依赖单一几何构型。研究旨在证明几何构型可作为独立观测量，因为汤川型相互作用（Yukawa-type interactions）与卡西米尔背景在体力和表面量子效应方面具有不同的几何标度行为。

Method: 通过分析不同几何构型下力的标度行为，研究比较了球-球（sphere-sphere）和板-板（plate-plate）几何构型与现有单一几何构型的差异。该方法基于几何构型作为独立观测量的理论框架，推导出不同几何下的约束条件。

Result: 首次从球-球和板-板几何构型推导出对短程力的约束，从而完善了卡西米尔几何的标准集（canonical set of Casimir geometries）。在λ≲10⁻⁸米范围内获得了基于卡西米尔效应的最严格约束（most stringent Casimir-based bounds）。

Conclusion: 研究结果确立了几何构型作为系统搜索短程力的新手段（new handle），证明了不同几何构型可提供互补的约束信息，为未来实验设计提供了重要指导。

Abstract: Casimir force searches provide among the most sensitive laboratory probes of new short range interactions. Existing constraints rely almost exclusively on a single geometry. We show that Casimir geometry constitutes an independent observable, as Yukawa-type interactions and Casimir background exhibit different geometric scaling for bulk forces and surface quantum effects. We derive the first constraints from sphere-sphere and plate-plate geometries, thereby completing the canonical set of Casimir geometries, obtaining the most stringent Casimir-based bounds for $λ\lesssim 10^{-8}~\mathrm{m}$. Our results establish geometry as a new handle for systematic searches for short range forces.

### [155] [Power-Law Running of the Higgs Mass](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15081)
*Kang-Sin Choi*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出标量质量平方的重整化（renormalized scalar mass squared）随能量尺度呈幂次运行（power-runs），在大统一能标（M_GUT）和弱电能标（m_W）之间自然解释了28个数量级的差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在解释标量质量平方在大统一能标（M_GUT）和弱电能标（m_W）之间存在的28个数量级差异，这一差异在粒子物理标准模型（Standard Model）中是一个长期存在的问题。

Method: 通过分析重整化标量质量平方作为能量尺度的函数，发现其随能量尺度呈幂次运行（power-runs），并计算标准模型的圈修正因子（loop-correction factor），该修正由顶夸克汤川耦合（top quark Yukawa coupling）主导。

Result: 重整化标量质量平方在大统一能标处为O(M_GUT^2)，在弱电能标处为O(m_W^2)，28个数量级的差异可由标准模型的圈修正因子自然解释，该因子主要取决于顶夸克汤川耦合：16π^2/(N_c y_t^2 ln10)。

Conclusion: 标量质量平方的28个数量级差异可通过其随能量尺度的幂次运行行为自然解释，这一解释依赖于标准模型的圈修正，特别是顶夸克汤川耦合的主导作用。

Abstract: The renormalized scalar mass squared is a function of the energy scale and power-runs as its square: it is O$(M_{GUT}^2)$ at $M_{GUT}^2$ and O$(m_W^2)$ at $m_W^2$. The 28 orders of discrepancy is naturally explained by the loop-correction factor of the Standard Model, dominated by the top quark Yukawa coupling $16π^2/(N_c y_t^2 \ln10)$.

</details>


### [156] [CPT Violation, Mirror World and Implications for Baryon Asymmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22381)

Main category: hep-ph

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在为时间反转提供几何解释，而不依赖于初态-末态互换。通过构建全局CPT对称的宇宙对，可以自然地引入具有相反手性和反转微观时间坐标的镜像宇宙。

Method: 提出一个新颖模型，其中宇宙作为坐标反转的对应体对（coordinate-reversed counterparts）被创造，形成全局CPT对称系统。该框架允许在每个扇区内存在局部CPT破坏（local CPT violations），并研究这种破坏的后果。

Result: 局部CPT破坏导致真实暴胀子（real inflaton）和反暴胀子（anti-inflaton）场之间的质量差异。这种不对称性可以修改再加热温度（reheating temperatures），并在两个宇宙中自然地产生观测到的物质-反物质不对称性（matter-antimatter asymmetry）。

Conclusion: 该模型为时间反转提供了几何解释，并通过局部CPT破坏机制自然地解释了宇宙中观测到的物质-反物质不对称性，同时维持了全局的CPT对称性。

Abstract: We propose a novel model in which the Universe is created as a pair of coordinate-reversed counterparts, forming a globally CPT-symmetric system that permits local CPT violations within each sector. This framework naturally introduces a mirror universe with opposite chiralities and reversed microscopic time coordinates, providing a geometric interpretation of time reversal without relying on initial-final state interchange. We investigate the consequences of local CPT violation in each universe, which induces a mass difference between the real inflaton and anti-inflaton fields. Such an asymmetry can modify reheating temperatures and naturally generate the observed matter-antimatter asymmetry in both universes.

### [157] [Dark graviton sensing with magnetically levitated superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22647)
*Valentina Danieli,Paola C. M. Delgado,Federico R. Urban*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 悬浮传感器已成为探测轴子类粒子和暗光子等超轻暗物质的新前沿。本研究旨在探索磁悬浮超导体如何响应自旋2暗物质场（暗引力子），特别是在dHz至kHz频率范围内。

Method: 计算了暗引力子对超导体施加的作用力，分别考虑了物质耦合（matter coupling）和光耦合（light coupling）。物质耦合产生类似应变的潮汐加速度，而光耦合则诱导有效电流并产生振荡磁场。

Result: 研究发现，即使有显著实验改进，物质耦合的灵敏度仍无法与现有干涉仪或第五力实验竞争。然而，磁悬浮超导体可能成为暗引力子与电磁场耦合最灵敏的实验室探针之一，特别是在低频区域。

Conclusion: 磁悬浮超导体在探测暗引力子与电磁场的耦合方面具有独特潜力，尤其是在低频范围，前提是技术和读出噪声能得到有效控制。

Abstract: Levitated sensors have emerged as a new frontier to detect ultra-light dark matter such as axion-like particles and dark photons. In this work we study how a magnetically levitated superconductor responds to a spin-2 dark matter field, the dark graviton, in the dHz to kHz frequency range. To do so, we compute the forces that the dark graviton exerts on the superconductor, separately for matter and light couplings. The matter coupling produces a strain-like tidal acceleration between the superconductor and the readout pick-up loop in a way that is akin to a slow, continuous, massive gravitational wave. The light coupling instead induces an effective current that sources an oscillating magnetic field, thus driving the superdiamagnetic response of the superconductor. We find that, even with significant experimental improvements, the sensitivity reach for the matter coupling is not competitive with existing interferometers or fifth-force experiments. On the other hand, magnetically levitated superconductors could be among the most sensitive laboratory probes of the dark-graviton coupling to electromagnetism, especially at low frequencies, provided technical and readout noise can be kept under control.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究方法包括计算pp、pPb和Pb碰撞中通过光致光散射虚拟产生重轴子类粒子的微分和总截面。使用积分亮度分别为30 ab⁻¹、27 pb⁻¹和110 nb⁻¹的数据，建立了95%置信水平的排除极限以及3σ和5σ的发现极限。

Result: 研究结果显示，对于PbPb碰撞，当ALP质量m_a ≈ 250 GeV时获得最强的耦合常数限制；对于pp或pPb碰撞，当m_a ≈ 1 TeV时获得最强限制。这些结果与当前LHC限制进行了比较，表明FCC-hh具有显著优势。

Conclusion: 结论指出FCC-hh在搜索重轴子类粒子方面具有巨大的物理潜力。通过光致光散射过程，该对撞机能够提供比当前LHC更强的ALP耦合常数限制，特别是在特定质量区域。

Abstract: A virtual production of heavy axion-like particles (ALPs) via light-by-light scattering in pp, pPb and Pb collisions at the future 100 TeV collider FCC-hh is studied. Both differential and total cross sections are calculated. The 95\% C.L. exclusion limits, as well as $3σ$ and $5σ$ discovery limits on an ALP coupling constant versus ALP mass $m_a$ are given, using integrated luminosities of 30 ab$^{-1}$, 27 pb$^{-1}$ and 110 nb$^{-1}$. Our results are compared with the current LHC bounds. The strongest limit on the ALP coupling is obtained if $m_a \simeq 250$ GeV for the PbPb collisions, and if $m_a \simeq 1$ TeV for pp or pPb collisions. It allows us to conclude that the FCC-hh has a great physics potential of searching for the heavy ALPs.

### [159] [Light-by-light scattering at three loops in massless QCD and QED: amplitudes and cross sections](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22423)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用't Hooft-Veltman维度正规化方案（dimensional regularisation scheme）中的洛伦兹张量分解（Lorentz tensor decomposition）来简化计算复杂度，并计算三圈无质量QCD和QED螺旋度振幅（helicity amplitudes）。

Result: 获得的解析振幅结果非常紧凑，能够高效进行数值计算，并用于计算双光子（di-photon）系统不变质量和快度分布（rapidity distributions）的NNLO微分截面预测。

Conclusion: 计算得到的理论预测与ATLAS实验组在超周边重离子碰撞（ultra-peripheral heavy-ion collisions）中获得的数据相符合，验证了计算方法的有效性。

Abstract: We present the calculation of three-loop massless QCD and QED helicity amplitudes for light-by-light scattering. We make use of Lorentz tensor decomposition in the 't Hooft-Veltman dimensional regularisation scheme to reduce the complexity of the computation. Our analytic amplitude results are remarkably compact and can be efficiently evaluated numerically. We employ them to compute the corresponding NNLO differential cross-section predictions in the invariant mass and rapidity distributions of the di-photon system, for which we find agreement with the experimental ATLAS data from ultra-peripheral heavy-ion collisions.

### [160] [Cosmic Ray Boosted Dark Matter in COSINUS: Modeling and Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22971)
*G. Angloher,M. R. Bharadwaj,A. Böhmer,M. Cababie,I. Colantoni,I. Dafinei,N. Di Marco,C. Dittmar,F. Ferella,F. Ferroni,S. Fichtinger,A. Filipponi,T. Frank,M. Friedl,D. Fuchs,L. Gai,M. Gapp,M. Heikinheimo,M. N. Hughes,K. Huitu,M. Kellermann,R. Maji,M. Mancuso,L. Pagnanini,F. Petricca,S. Pirro,F. Pröbst,G. Profeta,A. Puiu,F. Reindl,K. Schäffner,J. Schieck,P. Schreiner,C. Schwertner,P. Settembri,K. Shera,M. Stahlberg,A. Stendahl,M. Stukel,C. Tresca,S. Yue,V. Zema,Y. Zhu,N. Zimmermann*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过增强暗物质（boosted dark matter）框架，利用高能宇宙射线或中微子散射使轻暗物质获得额外动能，从而克服传统直接探测实验对亚GeV暗物质的质量限制，为COSINUS实验提供了暗物质-核子散射截面的预测约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 亚GeV暗物质（sub-GeV dark matter）的直接探测面临挑战，因为轻暗物质粒子的动能较小。虽然专门设计的低阈值探测器已将探测下限推至几百MeV，但背景事件率而非能量阈值成为进一步改进的主要限制。增强暗物质框架为探测亚MeV质量暗物质提供了替代途径。

Method: 研究采用增强暗物质（boosted dark matter）框架，其中高能宇宙射线或中微子散射暗物质粒子，赋予其额外动能，使其速度超越非相对论性暗物质晕（dark matter halo）的典型预期。基于此框架，建立了暗物质-核子散射截面（dark matter - nucleon scattering cross sections）的目录，涵盖自旋0、1/2和1的暗物质，以及具有偶或奇宇称的标量和矢量媒介子（scalar and vector mediators）。

Result: 研究结果为COSINUS实验提供了暗物质-核子散射截面的预测约束，假设曝光量为100 kg·d。这些结果展示了COSINUS实验对亚GeV增强暗物质的潜在探测灵敏度，特别是在重媒介子极限（heavy mediator limit）下的各种暗物质和媒介子组合情况。

Conclusion: 增强暗物质框架能够克服传统直接探测实验对轻暗物质的质量限制，使具有较高能量阈值的实验也能探测亚GeV暗物质。COSINUS实验通过该框架有望对暗物质-核子相互作用截面设置新的约束，扩展对轻暗物质粒子的探测能力。

Abstract: Direct detection of nuclear recoils due to sub-GeV dark matter is challenging because of the small kinetic energy of the light dark matter particles. Although limits down to a few hundred MeV have been reached using specially designed low threshold detectors, further improvements are now constrained more by background event rates than by energy thresholds. However, constraints down to sub-MeV dark matter masses can still be obtained through the boosted dark matter framework. In this scenario, high-energy cosmic rays or neutrinos scatter off dark matter particles, imparting additional kinetic energy and boosting them beyond the typical velocities expected from the non-relativistic dark matter halo. These boosted dark matter particles can then be detected even by experiments with higher energy thresholds. In this work, we present a catalog of dark matter - nucleon scattering cross sections corresponding to a heavy mediator limit for spin zero, one half and one dark matter and for scalar and vector mediators with even or odd parity. Based on these results, we present projected constraints on the dark matter - nucleon cross section for the COSINUS experiment, assuming an exposure of 100 kg d, demonstrating the potential sensitivity to sub-GeV boosted dark matter.

</details>


### [161] [Dynamically assisted Schwinger pair production in differently polarized electric fields with the frequency chirping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22549)
*Abhinav Jangir,Anees Ahmed*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过实时狄拉克-海森堡-维格纳形式体系，分析了不同偏振电场中频率啁啾对电子-正电子对产生的增强效应。研究发现频率啁啾能显著增强动量分布的峰值，在动态辅助双色场中可将粒子数密度提高2-3个数量级，且随着啁啾参数增大，数密度对场偏振的敏感性逐渐减弱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索频率啁啾参数和场偏振对电子-正电子对产生过程的联合影响，为在有限场参数条件下最大化粒子产额提供理论指导。通过分析不同偏振电场中的动态辅助效应，寻求对产生过程的最优控制方法。

Method: 采用实时狄拉克-海森堡-维格纳形式体系（real-time Dirac-Heisenberg-Wigner formalism），研究单色场和动态辅助双色组合场中频率啁啾对电子-正电子对产生的影响。详细分析了啁啾参数和场偏振对动量分布和总粒子数密度的联合效应。

Result: 频率啁啾在单色场和双色组合场中均导致强烈的干涉效应，并显著增强了动量分布的峰值。在动态辅助情况下，当对强场和弱场都施加较大频率啁啾时，粒子数密度可提高2-3个数量级。此外，随着啁啾参数增大，数密度对场偏振的敏感性逐渐减弱。

Conclusion: 研究结果为电子-正电子对产生过程的最优控制提供了重要基础，为在有限场参数条件下最大化粒子产额提供了指导。频率啁啾技术可显著增强对产生效率，且随着啁啾参数增大，对场偏振的依赖性降低。

Abstract: We investigate the enhanced dynamically assisted electron-positron pair production in differently polarized electric fields with frequency chirps within the real-time Dirac-Heisenberg-Wigner formalism. The combined influence of the chirp parameter and the field polarization on the momentum distribution and the total number density of the created pairs is studied in detail for one-color field as well as dynamically assisted two-color combined fields. The frequency chirps lead to strong interference effects and significantly enhanced the peak values in the momentum distribution for both one-color field and two-color combined fields. In the dynamically assisted case, the number density can be enhanced significantly over 2-3 orders when large frequency chirp is applied to both strong and weak fields. Furthermore, we observe that sensitivity of the number density to field polarization progressively diminishes as the chirp parameter increases, a trend that holds for both one-color field and the assisted two-color combined fields. These results provide a valuable foundation for the optimal control of pair production, offering guidance for maximizing particle yield within a constrained set of field parameters.

### [162] [Five-flavor molecular pentaquarks in the $Ξ_b^{(\prime,\,*)} \bar D^{(*)}$ and $Ξ_c^{(\prime,\,*)} B^{(*)}$ systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23287)
*Fu-Lai Wang,Xiang Liu*

Main category: hep-ph

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 隐粲五夸克（hidden-charm pentaquarks）和开味四夸克（open-flavor tetraquarks）的发现激发了寻找更奇特强子构型的研究。本文旨在探索包含五种不同味道的真正奇异分子五夸克候选态。

Method: 采用单玻色子交换模型（one-boson-exchange model），结合S-D波混合（S-D wave mixing）和耦合道动力学（coupled-channel dynamics），系统研究Ξ_b^{(′,∗)}D̄^{(*)}和Ξ_c^{(′,∗)}B^{(*)}体系。

Abstract: The discovery of hidden-charm pentaquarks and open-flavor tetraquarks motivates the search for even more exotic hadron configurations. Employing the one-boson-exchange model with the $S$-$D$ wave mixing and coupled-channel dynamics, we identify the most promising molecular pentaquark candidates comprising five different flavors. Importantly, these loosely bound states exhibit pronounced spin splittings across different total angular momentum configurations after incorporating the spin-dependent interactions or the channel couplings. In addition, we identify several possible isovector molecular pentaquark candidates within the $Ξ_b^{(\prime,\,*)} \bar D^{(*)}$ and $Ξ_c^{(\prime,\,*)} B^{(*)}$ systems. Our predictions provide clear targets for experimental searches at facilities such as LHCb and Belle II, where the unique five-flavor quark configuration offers a distinctive experimental signature.

### [163] [Dark Matter Detection through Rydberg Atom Transducer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23337)
*J. F. Chen,Haokun Fu,Christina Gao,Jing Shu,Geng-Bo Wu,Peiran Yin,Yi-Ming Zhong,Ying Zuo*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种集成介电光晕镜（dielectric haloscope）、里德伯原子换能器（Rydberg-atom transducer）和超导纳米线单光子探测器（superconducting nanowire single-photon detector）的混合探测架构，用于探测meV质量范围的超轻玻色子暗物质（ultralight bosonic dark matter），在0.4 meV质量处对轴子-光子耦合（axion-photon coupling）的灵敏度可达g_aγγ ∼ 10⁻¹³ GeV⁻¹。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: meV质量范围的超轻玻色子暗物质（对应太赫兹康普顿频率）目前仍未被充分探索，主要障碍在于难以在太赫兹频率下同时实现高效信号转换和单光子敏感探测。这阻碍了对轴子（axion）和暗光子（dark photon）暗物质在太赫兹窗口的探测。

Method: 提出了一种统一低温平台（≲1 K）下的混合探测架构：介电光晕镜通过相位匹配共振增强将暗物质转换为太赫兹光子；冷⁸⁷Rb原子系综通过里德伯态间的六波混频（six-wave mixing）将太赫兹信号相干上转换至光学波段；最后使用超导纳米线单光子探测器进行探测。该过程具有固有方向性和窄带宽（Δν_atomic ∼ 1 MHz），可有效抑制各向同性热背景。

Result: 介电光晕镜实现了C ∼ 0.4的形状因子（form factor）和Q_L ∼ 10⁴的负载品质因子（loaded quality factor）。在0.3 K温度下进行10天积分后，预计在m_a ∼ 0.4 meV处对轴子-光子耦合的灵敏度可达g_aγγ ∼ 10⁻¹³ GeV⁻¹，达到QCD轴子带（QCD axion band）。

Conclusion: 该混合探测架构为太赫兹窗口的轴子和暗光子暗物质探测开辟了新途径，能够达到QCD轴子带的灵敏度，解决了太赫兹频率下信号转换与单光子探测的难题。

Abstract: Ultralight bosonic dark matter with masses in the meV range, corresponding to terahertz (THz) Compton frequencies, remains largely unexplored due to the difficulty of achieving both efficient signal conversion and single-photon-sensitive detection at THz frequencies. We propose a hybrid detection architecture that integrates a dielectric haloscope, Rydberg-atom transducer, and superconducting nanowire single-photon detection within a unified cryogenic platform operating at $\lesssim 1\,\text{K}$. The dielectric haloscope converts dark matter into THz photons via phase-matched resonant enhancement, achieving form factors $C \sim 0.4$ and loaded quality factors $Q_L \sim 10^4$. A cold $^{87}$Rb ensemble then coherently up-converts the THz signal to the optical domain through six-wave mixing among Rydberg states. The intrinsic directionality and narrow bandwidth ($Δν_{\mathrm{atomic}} \sim 1\,\text{MHz}$) of this process provide extra suppression of isotropic thermal backgrounds. With 10 days of integration at $0.3\,\text{K}$, we project sensitivity to the axion-photon coupling $g_{aγγ} \sim 10^{-13}\,\mathrm{GeV}^{-1}$ at $m_a \sim 0.4\,\text{meV}$, reaching the QCD axion band and opening the THz window for searches of both axion and dark photon dark matter.

### [164] [Relativistic quantum mechanics of massive neutrinos in a rotating frame](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22970)
*Alexander Breev,Maxim Dvornikov*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了中微子在旋转物质中的演化行为，基于狄拉克方程在共转非惯性系中的精确解，分析了电弱相互作用对中微子矢量流的影响，并推广了中微子味振荡在非静止物质中的描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究中微子在旋转物质中的演化行为，旨在理解电弱相互作用在非惯性系中的效应，特别是旋转物质对中微子动力学的影响，为天体物理应用提供理论基础。

Method: 采用狄拉克方程（Dirac equation）在共转非惯性系（corotating noninertial frame）中描述中微子，对于无质量中微子获得精确解，对于有质量粒子则考虑缓慢旋转物质的近似解。

Result: 发现沿旋转轴的矢量流（vector current）在无质量和有质量情况下均非零，类似于手征涡旋效应（chiral vortical effect）；推导出包含共振的跃迁概率，推广了非运动物质中的中微子味振荡（neutrino flavor oscillations）描述。

Conclusion: 该研究成功将中微子振荡理论推广到旋转物质环境，揭示了非惯性效应的重要影响，为相关天体物理现象的解释提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: We study the evolution of neutrinos electroweakly interacting with a rotating matter. The description of neutrinos is based on the Dirac equation in the corotating noninertial frame where matter is at rest. We find solution of this Dirac equation, where the matter angular velocity is accounted for exactly, for massless neutrinos. In case of massive particles, this solution is obtained for a slowly rotating matter. Our findings are compared with previous research. We consider two applications of our results. First, we compute the electroweak contribution to the vector current of neutrinos along the rotation axis, which is analogous to the chiral vortical effect. This current is shown to be nonzero for both massless and massive particles. Then, we take into account the nonzero mixing between different mass eigenstates. It allows us to study neutrino flavor oscillations in rotating matter and account for noninertial effects. We derive the transition probability which reveals the resonance. These findings generalize the description of neutrino oscillations in a nonmoving matter. Some astrophysical applications are briefly discussed.

### [165] [Unified description of Sivers and Boer-Mulders asymmetries from twist-3 correlations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23138)
*Zhimin Zhu,Jiangshan Lan,Chandan Mondal,Xingbo Zhao,James P. Vary,BLFQ Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 首次计算了质子和π介子的Efremov-Teryaev-Qiu-Sterman函数及相关twist-3夸克-胶子关联函数，基于光前有效哈密顿量对角化获得的光前波函数，预测结果与近期实验提取值定量一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机是首次计算质子和π介子的Efremov-Teryaev-Qiu-Sterman（ETQS）函数及相关twist-3夸克-胶子关联函数，这些函数对于理解强子自旋结构至关重要，特别是Sivers和Boer-Mulders不对称性。

Method: 方法基于光前有效哈密顿量（light-front effective Hamiltonian）在包含动态胶子的Fock空间截断内对角化获得光前波函数（light-front wave functions），计算硬极点区域（hard-pole region）的twist-3关联，并外推到软胶子极点极限（soft-gluon pole limit），最后进行标度演化（scale evolutions）。

Result: 计算结果显示，经过标度演化后的预测与近期实验提取值呈现定量一致性（quantitative consistency），为Sivers和Boer-Mulders不对称性提供了基于光前哈密顿量方法的统一描述。

Conclusion: 该研究成功实现了从第一性原理出发计算ETQS函数和twist-3夸克-胶子关联函数，其预测与实验数据一致，为理解强子自旋结构提供了重要的理论框架和数值基准。

Abstract: We present the first calculation of the Efremov-Teryaev-Qiu-Sterman functions and associated twist-3 quark-gluon correlation functions for both the proton and pion. These functions are determined using the light-front wave functions obtained by diagonalizing a light-front effective Hamiltonian within a Fock space truncated to include a dynamical gluon. We compute the twist-3 correlations in the hard-pole region and extrapolate them to the soft-gluon pole limit. After the scale evolutions, our predictions demonstrate quantitative consistency with recent experimental extractions, providing a unified description of the Sivers and Boer-Mulders asymmetries from a light-front Hamiltonian approach.

</details>

### [166] [GHz control of THz QCL band structure and gain by standing acoustic strain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22925)
*Alexander S. Kuznetsov,Valentino Pistore,Lutz Schrottke,Klaus Biermann,Xiang Lü*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于千兆赫兹体声波（BAW）直接调制太赫兹量子级联激光器（QCL）能带结构的新方法，用于实现主动频率梳生成和波形控制，避免了传统偏置调制的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 太赫兹（THz）领域的主动频率梳生成和波形控制是核心挑战。传统方法通过主动偏置调制（active bias modulation）实现，但会改变器件工作点并严重限制其灵活性。需要新的方法来克服这些限制。

Method: 提出基于千兆赫兹频率驻波体声波（standing bulk acoustic waves, BAWs）直接调制QCL能带结构的方法。在THz QCL顶部制造体声换能器（bulk acoustic transducer），在其有源区内激发GHz驻波BAWs。通过测量有源区光致发光（photoluminescence, PL）揭示BAW对能带结构的影响，并开发模型进行能带结构模拟预测BAW对QCL子带结构和增益的影响。

Result: 射频驱动换能器可在5-12 GHz频率范围内可调谐生成驻波BAWs，其波长与QCL周期长度相匹配。BAW应变导致PL能量在其非调制值周围产生高达数meV的显著调制。这是首次展示使用GHz声学应变在THz QCL中实现动态能带结构调制。

Conclusion: 该方法建立了QCL与BAWs之间的强大协同作用，为太赫兹领域的相干控制和频率梳工程引入了一种全新的范式，实现了对光学增益和色散的直接局部控制。

Abstract: Active frequency comb generation and waveform control are central challenges in the terahertz (THz) domain. In THz quantum cascade lasers (QCLs), these functions have typically been achieved through active bias modulation, which alters the operating point of the device and imposes severe limitations on its flexibility. To address these challenges, we propose an approach based on the direct modulation of the QCL bandstructure using GHz-frequency standing bulk acoustic waves (BAWs), promising direct and localized control of the optical gain and chromatic dispersion. To this end, we fabricated a bulk acoustic transducer on top of a THz QCL in order to excite GHz standing BAWs within its active region. We demonstrate that radio-frequency driving of the transducer leads to the tunable generation of standing BAWs in 5-12 GHz frequency range with wavelengths commensurate to the QCL period length. The effect of the BAW on the QCL bandstructure is revealed by measuring photoluminescence (PL) of the active region, where the BAW strain leads to a considerable modulation of the PL energy up to a few meV around its non-modulated value. We also develop a model and perform bandstructure simulations to predict the effect of the BAW on the QCL subband structure and gain. These results mark the first demonstration of dynamic bandstructure modulation in a THz QCL using GHz acoustic strain, introducing a fundamentally new paradigm that establishes a powerful synergy between QCLs and BAWs towards coherent control and frequency comb engineering in the THz domain.

</details>


### [167] [Ultrafast near-field imaging of an operating nanolaser using free electrons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23237)
*Cléo Santini,Thi Huong Ngo,Luiz H. G. Tizei,Aurélie Lloret,Tom Fraysse,Sebastien Weber,Adrien Teurtrie,Virginie Brändli,Sebastien Chenot,Denis Lefebvre,Stéphane Vézian,Hugo Lourenço-Martins,Christelle Brimont,Benjamin Damilano,Thierry Guillet,Sophie Meuret*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本研究通过同步电子近场与光子远场时间分辨光谱技术，突破了衍射极限，实现了纳米线激光器近场在纳米和亚皮秒尺度上的动态映射。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 集成光电子器件（integrated opto-electronic devices）有望革新信息处理，但实现紧凑功能器件的关键缺失单元是纳米尺度可调谐光源。虽然单晶生长的半导体纳米线激光器（nanowire lasers, NWLs）填补了这一空白，但其性能优化需要表征纳米尺度的近场及其动力学，这受到光衍射极限（diffraction limit）的限制。

Method: 采用同步电子近场与光子远场时间分辨光谱技术（synchronous electron near-field and photon far-field time-resolved spectroscopies），突破了衍射极限，实现了纳米尺度和亚皮秒时间分辨率的近场映射。

Result: 定量测量了纳米线激光器腔中受激光子绝对数量N₀(t)的演化，发现腔中同时存在高达4×10⁵个光子；映射了激光腔模的近场，显示回音壁模式（whispering gallery）和法布里-珀罗模式（Fabry-Perot）均可参与激光过程。

Conclusion: 研究展示了纳米线激光器在亚皮秒和纳米尺度下近场的演化过程，直接观测近场将有助于阐明材料异质性（缺陷、化学变化、污染物、界面粗糙度、应变）对纳米线激光器性能的影响。

Abstract: Integrated opto-electronic devices have the potential to revolutionize information processing, with substantial increase in compute speed, seamless information transfer and reduction of energy consumption. A key missing unit for the successful implementation of compact functional devices are nanometer scale modular and tunable light sources. Monotonically grown semiconducting nanowire lasers (NWLs) fills this gap. However, NWLs operation improvement and optimization require the characterization of their near-field and its dynamics at the nanometer scale, which is hindered due to the light diffraction limit. Here we show how synchronous electron near-field and photon far-field time-resolved spectroscopies surpass this limitation and map a NWLs near-field with nanometer and sub-picoseconds temporal resolution. We quantitatively measured the evolution of the absolute number of stimulated photons $N_0(t)$ in the NWL cavity, measuring that up to 4x10$^5$ are present simultaneously in the cavity. We mapped the lasing cavity mode's near-field, showing that both whispering gallery and Fabry-Perot modes can participate in the lasing. Our results demonstrate how the near-field of a NWL under operation evolves in the sub-picoseconds and the nanometer scales. We anticipate that a direct observation of the near-field will help to elucidate the influence of materials heterogeneities (defects, chemical changes, contaminants, interface roughness, strain) in NWL operation.

### [168] [Moment bounds and exclusion processes on random Delaunay triangulations with conductances](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22562)
*A. Faggionato,C. Tagliaferri*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 该论文研究平稳简单点过程的Voronoi剖分及其对偶Delaunay三角剖分上的随机游走和简单排斥过程。通过建立关于Palm分布的积分条件，确保加权度和相关矩的可积性，从而应用现有随机游走和电阻网络理论。对于非对称跳跃速率的情况，在有限依赖范围和一致有界传导率条件下，恢复了简单排斥过程的构造和性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究平稳简单点过程Voronoi剖分对偶图Delaunay三角剖分上随机权重（传导率）的积分性质。这些可积性条件对于应用随机游走、电阻网络和对称简单排斥过程（symmetric simple exclusion process）的现有理论至关重要，特别是当跳跃速率非对称时，需要确保过程的良好定义和性质。

Method: 引入Voronoi剖分及其对偶图Delaunay三角剖分，并为每条边分配随机权重（传导率）。建立关于Palm分布的充分条件，确保加权度和相关矩的可积性。对于非对称跳跃速率的情况，利用有限依赖范围和一致有界传导率条件，通过Bernoulli键渗流（Bernoulli bond percolation）分析恢复简单排斥过程的构造。

Result: 提供了确保加权度和相关矩关于Palm分布可积的充分条件，这些条件对于应用随机游走、电阻网络和对称简单排斥过程理论至关重要。对于非对称跳跃速率的情况，在点过程具有有限依赖范围且传导率一致有界时，成功恢复了简单排斥过程的构造和性质。

Conclusion: 论文建立了平稳简单点过程Voronoi剖分对偶图Delaunay三角剖分上随机传导率的积分理论框架。这些结果对于随机游走、电阻网络和简单排斥过程的应用具有重要意义，特别是在非对称跳跃速率情况下，为过程的良好定义和性质分析提供了理论基础。所有结果在整数平移平稳性条件下仍然有效。

Abstract: We consider the Voronoi tessellation associated to a stationary simple point process on $\mathbb{R}^d$ with finite and positive intensity. We introduce the Delaunay triangulation as its dual graph, i.e.~the graph with vertex set given by the point process and with edges between vertices whose Voronoi cells share a $(d-1)$-dimensional face. We also attach to each edge a random weight, called conductance. We provide sufficient conditions ensuring the integrability w.r.t. the Palm distribution of several quantities as weighted degrees and associated moments. These integrability properties are crucial in applications, as they allow to apply existing results on random walks, resistor networks and the symmetric simple exclusion processes with random conductances (cf. [1,11,12,13,14,15]). For the latter, while the moment bounds ensure its well definiteness and several properties, the same does not hold when the jump rates are not symmetric, i.e. for a generic simple exclusion process. In this case, by using a criterion from [13], we recover construction and properties of the simple exclusion process whenever the simple point process has finite range of dependence and the conductances are uniformly upper bounded. This last result relies on a suitable analysis of Bernoulli bond percolation on the Delaunay triangulation inspired by [2,3]. All the above results remain valid if the simple point process is stationary with respect to integer translations.

</details>


### [169] [On the Golomb-Dickman constant under Ewens sampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23175)
*José Ricardo G. Mendonça,Luis Jehiel Negret*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文定义了广义Golomb-Dickman常数λ_θ，作为Ewens测度下随机排列中最长循环比例在参数θ>0时的极限期望值，并给出了其显式积分表示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于将经典的Shepp和Lloyd计算扩展到Ewens测度（Ewens measure）设置，探索随机排列中最长循环比例在不同参数θ下的渐近行为。

Method: 方法基于Kingman泊松过程（Kingman's Poisson process）构造的泊松-狄利克雷分布（Poisson-Dirichlet distribution）的独立性性质，通过相对初等的手段获得λ_θ的显式积分表示。

Result: 获得了λ_θ关于指数积分（exponential integral）的显式积分表示，揭示了λ_θ对θ的依赖性反映了由长循环主导（小θ）和由许多小循环主导（大θ）两种机制之间的转变。

Conclusion: 该研究成功将经典计算扩展到Ewens设置，提供了λ_θ的数值表格和图示，为理解随机排列中最长循环的渐近行为提供了新的理论工具。

Abstract: We define a generalized Golomb-Dickman constant $λ_θ$ as the limiting expected proportion of the longest cycle in random permutations under the Ewens measure with parameter $θ> 0$. Exploiting the independence properties of Kingman's Poisson process construction of the Poisson-Dirichlet distribution, we obtain an explicit integral representation for $λ_θ$ in terms of the exponential integral. The dependence of $λ_θ$ on $θ$ reflects the transition between regimes dominated by long cycles (small $θ$) and those with many small cycles (large $θ$). Our result can be viewed as an extension of the classical calculations of Shepp and Lloyd to the Ewens setting by relatively elementary means. A figure and a table of numerical values of $λ_θ$ are included.

</details>

### [170] [Phases of itinerant anyons in Laughlin's quantum Hall states on a lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22389)
*Tevž Lotrič,Steven H. Simon*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期在范德华材料中观察到分数陈绝缘体附近的时间反演破缺超导性，促使理论界重新关注掺杂分数量子霍尔态在晶格上的行为，特别是"任意子超导性（anyon superconductivity）"这一概念。

Method: 采用有效部分子平均场理论进行解析分析，并结合变分蒙特卡洛（variational Monte Carlo）进行数值计算，比较了描述ν=1/m Laughlin序的U(1)和SU(m) Chern-Simons场理论框架。

Result: 在空穴掺杂ν=1/3费米子分数陈绝缘体的实验相关情景中，当能量最低的激发是基本1/3电荷任意子时，发现了形成半整数中心荷（half-integer central charge）任意子超导态的机制，无需这些任意子配对成电荷-2/3复合体。

Conclusion: 带Berry曲率与有效任意子色散的相互作用对实现何种任意子相具有决定性影响，为理解掺杂分数陈绝缘体中的任意子超导性提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: We study phases of itinerant anyons when hole-doping Laughlin-like states in fractional Chern insulators (FCIs). In light of the recent observation of time-reversal-broken superconductivity near FCIs in van der Waals materials, a theoretical understanding of doped fractional quantum Hall states on a lattice has been developed by Shi and Senthil [Phys. Rev. X 15, 031069], reviving old ideas about "anyon superconductivity". We test these ideas analytically within an effective parton mean-field theory and numerically with variational Monte Carlo, pointing out that the predicted state depends on whether the Laughlin order at $ν=1/m$ is described by a U(1), or an SU(m) Chern-Simons field, the latter implying a symmetry between the m parton species. Our results demonstrate that the interplay between band Berry curvature and effective anyon dispersion has crucial implications for which anyonic phase is realized. In the experimentally relevant scenario of hole-doping the $ν=1/3$ fermionic FCI, our results uncover a mechanism for the formation of an anyon superconducting state of half-integer central charge in the case when the energetically cheapest excitations are the fundamental 1/3 charge anyons, bypassing the need for these anyons to pair into charge-2/3 composites, which has generally been assumed in similar anyon superconductivity constructions.

### [171] [Discovery of BKT correlations in the quantum kagome compound Cs$_2$Cu$_3$SnF$_{12}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22481)
*M. S. Grbić,I. Jakovac,I. Kupčić,H. Tanaka,M. Horvatić*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究kagome化合物Cs₂Cu₃SnF₁₂的微观性质，特别是其量子自旋系统的独特行为，以理解该材料在量子磁性方面的特殊表现。

Method: 采用⁶³,⁶⁵Cu核四极共振（nuclear quadrupolar resonance, NQR）技术，分析低于奈尔温度（Néel temperature）T_N = 20 K的局域超精细场，并测量自旋-晶格弛豫率（spin-lattice relaxation rate）T₁⁻¹。

Result: 分析显示自旋结构与负矢量手性（negative vector chirality）的P2₁/n对称性一致；T₁⁻¹测量揭示了无隙基态（gapless ground state）和二维Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless（BKT）型关联，该关联在零磁场下延伸至约130 K的宽温区；NQR线宽增加与中子散射识别的短程手性序一致。

Conclusion: 研究结果确立了Cs₂Cu₃SnF₁₂作为展现BKT行为的独特量子kagome系统，其二维BKT型关联在宽温区内持续存在，揭示了该材料在量子磁性研究中的特殊地位。

Abstract: We investigate the microscopic properties of the kagome compound Cs$_2$Cu$_3$SnF$_{12}$ using $^{63,65}$Cu nuclear quadrupolar resonance (NQR). Analysis of the local hyperfine fields below the Néel temperature $T_N = 20$ K indicates a spin structure consistent with $P2_1/n$ symmetry of negative vector chirality. Measurements of the spin-lattice relaxation rate $T_1 ^{-1}$ reveal signatures of a gapless ground state and two-dimensional Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless (BKT)-type correlations above $T_N$, extending over a broad temperature range of approximately 130 K in zero magnetic field. Within the same temperature range, the observed increase in the NQR linewidth is consistent with short-range chiral order recently identified by neutron scattering. Our results establish Cs$_2$Cu$_3$SnF$_{12}$ as a unique quantum kagome system exhibiting BKT behavior.

### [172] [Symmetric Mass Generation Transition and its Nonequilibrium Critical Dynamics in a Bilayer Honeycomb Lattice Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22736)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对称质量生成（symmetric mass generation, SMG）相变违背了传统的朗道-金兹堡-威尔逊范式，在不发生自发对称性破缺或拓扑序的情况下打开多体能隙，在粒子物理和凝聚态物理领域引起了广泛关注。

Method: 采用无偏量子蒙特卡洛（quantum Monte Carlo）模拟研究双层蜂窝晶格（bilayer honeycomb lattice）模型中SMG相变的平衡和非平衡临界动力学，通过高精度提取临界指数分析临界行为。

Result: 明确确认在$J_{\text{c}}=2.584(8)$处存在SMG相变，将狄拉克半金属相与对称保持的SMG相分离；临界指数揭示了一个显著偏离平均场理论的新普适性类别；非平衡SMG相变尽管不满足基布尔-祖雷克机制的前提条件，但仍遵循广义有限时间标度。

Conclusion: 通过连接平衡临界性和非平衡动力学，本研究揭示了SMG相变的普适临界性质，为未来SMG物理的实验研究提供了坚实的理论基础。

Abstract: Symmetric mass generation (SMG) transitions defy the conventional Landau-Ginzburg-Wilson paradigm by opening a many-body gap without spontaneous symmetry breaking or topological order, attracting intense interest across particle physics and condensed matter physics. Here, we utilize unbiased quantum Monte Carlo simulations to investigate the equilibrium and nonequilibrium critical dynamics of the SMG transition in a bilayer honeycomb lattice model. We unambiguously confirm the existence of an SMG transition at $J_{\text{c}}=2.584(8)$ that separates the Dirac semimetal phase from a symmetry-preserving SMG phase. High-precision extraction of the critical exponents reveals a novel universality class that profoundly departs from mean-field theory. We then extend our study to the nonequilibrium regime, exploring the driven dynamics of the SMG transition. Notably, despite the breakdown of the prerequisites for the celebrated Kibble-Zurek mechanism, the nonequilibrium SMG transition still follows the generalized finite-time scaling. By bridging equilibrium criticality and nonequilibrium dynamics, our work uncovers the universal critical properties of SMG transitions, providing a solid theoretical basis for future experimental studies of SMG physics.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统二维Rokhsar-Kivelson二聚体模型在二分格子上通常局限于平移对称性破缺的二聚体晶体相。研究旨在突破这一限制，探索去禁闭的拓扑液体相。

Result: 确定了包含两个连续量子相变和一个一级相变的相图：Z₂液体与柱状/斑块价键固体（columnar/plaquette-VBS）之间的3D XY*相变，两个二聚体晶体之间的量子Lifshitz相变，以及交错晶体与Z₂液体之间的一级相变。

Abstract: Two-dimensional Rokhsar-Kivelson (RK) dimer models on bipartite lattices are generally limited to translation-symmetry-broken dimer crystals. We introduce a tensor-product regularisation of the dimer Hilbert space that yields a qubit Hamiltonian interpolating from the RK model to the $π$-flux toric code, thereby accessing a deconfined $\mathbb{Z}_2$ topological liquid. In this framework, the $\mathbb{Z}_2$ liquid descends from a multicritical $U(1)$ spin liquid through condensation of a charge-2 Higgs field, thus avoiding confinement. Using iDMRG together with low-energy field theory, we determine a phase diagram containing two continuous quantum phase transitions -- a $3\mathrm{D}$ XY$^{\ast}$ transition between the $\mathbb{Z}_2$ liquid and the columnar/plaquette-VBS, and a quantum Lifshitz transition between two dimer crystals -- alongside a first-order transition between the staggered crystal and the $\mathbb{Z}_2$ liquid. Our field theory suggests a deconfined multicritical point described by an Abelian Higgs model with dynamical critical exponent, $z=2$, where the three transitions meet, highlighting the interplay of fractionalisation and emergent gauge fluctuations.

### [174] [Dimensionality-Dependent Exciton Dispersion in a Single-Band Mott Insulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22695)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 激子带结构对研究激子动力学至关重要，理论上电子-空穴对之间的交换散射量子效应会显著调制激子色散，但需要实验验证维度变化对激子行为的影响。

Method: 采用高分辨率电子能量损失谱（high-resolution electron energy loss spectroscopy）直接观测单带Mott绝缘体（single-band Mott insulator）Nb3Cl8中的激子色散，对比分析高温相和低温相的维度依赖特性。

Result: 高温相中激子具有异常大的结合能，表现出清晰的准二维无质量线性色散；低温相中激子分裂为两个能带，均显示三维抛物线色散，这种色散的剧烈变化源于相变过程中层间耦合显著增强驱动的维度突变。

Conclusion: 该研究为激子行为如何随维度演化提供了清晰且典型的实例，揭示了维度突变对激子色散特性的决定性影响。

Abstract: Excitonic band structure is critical for investigating exciton dynamics. Theoretically, quantum effects from exchange scattering between electron-hole pairs significantly modulate exciton dispersion. Here, we report the direct observation of dimensionality-dependent exciton dispersion in a single-band Mott insulator Nb3Cl8 through high-resolution electron energy loss spectroscopy. In the high-temperature phase, the exciton in Nb3Cl8 hosts an exceptionally large binding energy, and exhibits clear quasi-two-dimensional massless linear dispersion. In contrast, in the low-temperature phase, the exciton splits into two bands, both displaying three-dimensional parabolic dispersion. These dramatic changes in the exciton dispersion stem from the dimensional mutation driven by a substantial enhancement of interlayer coupling across the phase transition. This Letter provides a clear and typical example of how exciton behavior evolves with dimensionality.

### [175] [Non-Hermitian skin effect in periodic, random, and quasiperiodic systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22919)
*F. Iwase*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过一维非厄米量子行走模型，系统比较了周期、随机和准周期（Fibonacci）结构对非厄米趋肤效应（NHSE）的影响。研究发现准周期结构能有效抑制大尺度边界积累，同时保持明确的拓扑能隙，为控制非厄米趋肤动力学提供了独特途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非厄米趋肤效应（non-Hermitian skin effect, NHSE）使体态向系统边界聚集，改变了体边对应关系，并使拓扑边缘模的识别复杂化。虽然已知破坏平移对称性会影响这一行为，但对不同结构类别的系统比较仍然有限。

Method: 研究采用一维非厄米量子行走模型（non-Hermitian quantum walk model），在拓扑非平庸区域匹配局部散射参数，以隔离空间结构在NHSE存在下的作用。系统比较了周期（periodic）、随机（random）和准周期（Fibonacci quasiperiodic）三种结构类型。

Result: 周期系统表现出显著的体态边界积累；随机系统通过安德森局域化（Anderson localization）抑制这种积累，但拓扑能隙被局域带隙态部分填充；而Fibonacci准周期系统在抑制大尺度边界积累的同时，保持了明确的拓扑能隙。波函数分析表明，准周期结构的层次性（hierarchical quasiperiodic structure）使体态在多个长度尺度上碎片化，从而缓解了NHSE。

Conclusion: 确定性准周期性（deterministic quasiperiodicity）构成了控制非厄米趋肤动力学和隔离拓扑边界模的独特结构体系。准周期结构通过其层次性特征有效抑制NHSE，同时保持拓扑能隙的完整性，为调控非厄米系统中的拓扑性质提供了新途径。

Abstract: The non-Hermitian skin effect (NHSE), which drives bulk states toward system boundaries, modifies bulk-boundary correspondence and complicates the identification of topological edge modes. Although breaking translational symmetry is known to influence this behavior, a systematic comparison of different structural classes remains limited. Here we investigate periodic, random, and quasiperiodic (Fibonacci) systems using a one-dimensional non-Hermitian quantum walk model. By matching the local scattering parameters in a topologically nontrivial regime, we isolate the role of spatial structure in the presence of the NHSE. We find that periodic systems exhibit pronounced boundary accumulation of bulk states. Random systems suppress this accumulation through Anderson localization, but the topological gap becomes partially filled with localized in-gap states. In contrast, the Fibonacci quasiperiodic system suppresses large-scale boundary accumulation while maintaining a well-defined topological gap. Analysis of the wave functions suggests that the hierarchical quasiperiodic structure fragments bulk states across multiple length scales, thereby mitigating the NHSE. These results identify deterministic quasiperiodicity as a distinct structural regime for controlling non-Hermitian skin dynamics and isolating topological boundary modes.

</details>


### [176] [Synergistic chemical and optical switching of chiral symmetry breaking in 1\textit{T}-TaS$_2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22921)
*Qingzheng Qiu,Mengxian Zhao,Roman Mankowsky,Henrik Till Lemke,Serhane Zerdane,Mathias Sander,Zihao Tao,Qizhi Li,Xiquan Zheng,Shilong Zhang,Qian Xiao,Xinyi Jiang,Yang Yang,Sheng Meng,Yingying Peng*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究展示了通过化学掺杂与飞秒光激发相结合，实现1T-TaS₂中手性电荷密度波（CDW）态的高效非热开关，揭示了其微观机制为声子介导的瞬态畴壁态过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光学控制对称性破缺量子相是量子材料研究的核心目标，但确定性开关常受限于单畴基态的稳定性。1T-TaS₂中的手性电荷密度波（chiral charge density wave, CDW）为此提供了天然平台，但原始材料被锁定在单一手性中。

Method: 结合化学掺杂（Ti替代）与飞秒光学激发（femtosecond optical excitation）。Ti掺杂稳定了共存手性畴的基态，为光学操控创造了可调谐的能量景观；飞秒光激发则诱导从主导手性畴到少数手性畴的不对称各向异性开关。

Result: 实现了手性CDW态的高效非热开关，其特征为面内畴生长和向非手性构型的重新分布。开关时间尺度与相干声子振荡（~2 THz）相当，揭示了通过瞬态畴壁态（transient domain-wall state）的声子介导路径。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了一种通过化学掺杂与超快光学调谐相结合来工程化和控制手性序参量的普适策略，为量子材料中对称性破缺相的光学操控提供了新途径。

Abstract: Optical control of symmetry-breaking quantum phases is a central goal in quantum materials, yet deterministic switching is often hindered by the stability of single-domain ground states. The chiral structure of the charge density wave (CDW) in 1T-TaS$_2$ provides a natural platform for such control, but the pristine material remains locked in a single chirality. Here we show that combining chemical doping with femtosecond optical excitation enables efficient and non-thermal switching of the chiral CDW state and reveal its microscopic mechanism. Ti substitution stabilizes a ground state with coexisting chiral domains, creating a tunable energy landscape for optical manipulation. Femtosecond photoexcitation then induces asymmetric and anisotropic switching from dominant to minority chiral domains, characterized by in-plane domain growth and a redistribution toward an achiral configuration. The switching occurs on a timescale comparable to a coherent phonon oscillation ($\sim$2 THz), revealing a phonon-mediated pathway that proceeds through a transient domain-wall state. Our results establish a broadly applicable strategy for engineering and controlling chiral order parameters through combined chemical and ultrafast optical tuning.

Method: 通过磁化率（magnetization）、比热（specific heat）和低至90 mK的中子衍射（neutron diffraction）测量，结合密度泛函理论（DFT）计算，对TbOF的磁性和结构性质进行了全面研究。

Abstract: We have identified TbOF as a unique frustrated and mixed-anion lattice, hosting unconventional magnetism. By means of magnetization, specific heat and neutron diffraction measurements down to 90 mK, as well as DFT calculations, we present a comprehensive study of the magnetic and structural properties of TbOF. We show that at 9.7 K, TbOF undergoes a structural phase transition accompanied by short-range magnetic correlations, in contrast to previously proposed long-range antiferromagnetic order. At lower temperatures, we observe two magnetic ordering transitions, consisting of incommensurate spin density waves and antiferromagnetic and ferromagnetic correlations. Furthermore, we observe metastable and hysteresis behavior below 2.0 K, highlighting the richness of complex magnetic interactions in TbOF. These results uniquely clarify the magnetic phase diagram of TbOF and highlight the intricate interplay between structure and magnetism in rare-earth oxyfluorides.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用SO(6) Majorana表示法描述各向同性Kitaev自旋液体中的自旋-3/2杂质算符，并对杂质相关项使用自洽平均场近似（self-consistent mean-field approximation）。通过分析杂质四极矩在通量扇区转变点的不连续跃迁，以及磁场下杂质间四极矩关联的指数衰减行为来研究通量构型。

Result: 基态通量扇区可以通过杂质四极矩在通量扇区转变点的不连续跃迁来识别。磁场下杂质间的四极矩关联呈现指数衰减，其衰减速率对通量扇区高度敏感。研究还讨论了与杂质结合的π通量（pi fluxes）相对于模型参数和内部通量构型的稳定性，并将发现与Lieb关于通量构型的猜想联系起来。

Abstract: Emergent fluxes play a central role in the low-energy properties of quantum spin liquids (QSLs), where they encode the underlying gauge structure and fractionalization of spins. Here, we show that the quadrupole moment of magnetic impurities provides a direct probe of these flux configurations in QSLs. Employing the SO(6) Majorana representation for spin-3/2 impurity operators in the isotropic Kitaev spin liquid together with a self-consistent mean-field approximation for impurity-related terms, we show that the ground-state flux sector can be identified by discontinuous jumps of the impurity quadrupole moment at the flux sector transition points. We also demonstrate that the quadrupole correlations between impurities under a magnetic field exhibit exponential decay, with decay rates that depend sensitively on the flux sector. Furthermore, we discuss the stability of pi fluxes bound to impurities with respect to model parameters and internal flux configurations, and relate our findings to Lieb's conjecture on flux configurations. These results establish the quadrupole moments of magnetic impurities as a sensitive tool to study fractionalized excitations and flux physics in Kitaev magnets.

### [179] [Open Quantum Cluster Embedding Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23163)
*Petar Brinić,Hugo U. R. Strand,Jakša Vučičević*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强关联电子系统的模拟面临严峻挑战，特别是某些实验相关的动力学响应函数计算存在有限尺寸效应和病态解析延拓（ill posed analytic continuation）问题。需要开发能够处理大晶格并避免解析延拓的方法。

Method: 提出量子簇嵌入理论，使用嵌入簇作为短程关联的代表，这些开放量子系统由Lindblad方程描述。从簇中提取的短程关联用于闭合晶格上费米子双线性算符和局域双占据数的运动方程，同时调整簇的马尔可夫浴使簇和晶格上的双线性算符及双占据期望值在两组方程伴随演化过程中保持一致。

Result: 该方法在非相互作用、原子极限和无限簇尺寸极限下数值精确，并满足总电荷和能量守恒定律。能够处理非常大的晶格，通过显式时间演化避免解析延拓。在方晶格Hubbard模型中计算电荷-电荷关联函数，与近期冷原子实验相比显示出良好的定性一致性。

Conclusion: 量子簇嵌入理论为解决强关联电子系统的动力学响应计算提供了有效框架，特别在处理大晶格和避免解析延拓方面具有优势，与实验结果的定性一致性验证了方法的有效性。

Abstract: The simulation of strongly correlated electron systems remains a formidable challenge. Certain experimentally relevant dynamical response functions are especially difficult to calculate, due to issues of finite-size effects and the ill posed analytic continuation. To address this we propose the quantum cluster embedding theory, an embedded cluster method aimed at computing the response of the system following an external perturbation; the frequency dependent dynamical susceptibility is obtained subsequently by means of inverse linear response theory. The embedded clusters, used within the method as representative of short range correlations, are open quantum systems governed by the Lindblad equation. The short-range correlations extracted from the clusters are used to close the equations of motion for the fermionic bilinear and the local double occupancy on the lattice. In turn, the clusters' Markovian baths are tuned to keep the bilinear and the double occupancy expectation values on the clusters and the lattice identical, throughout the concomitant evolution of the two sets of equations. The theory becomes numerically exact in the non-interacting, atomic and infinite cluster size limits, and it respects the total charge and energy conservation laws. We show that our approach can treat very large lattices while avoiding analytic continuation through the explicit time evolution. Finally we compute the charge-charge correlation function in the square lattice Hubbard model and compare with a recent cold atom experiment, finding good qualitative agreement.

Method: 采用描述CuO₂平面的标准Hubbard模型和t-J-U模型，将鲁棒的顺磁子能量与高温超导费米面性质（通过次近邻与最近邻跳跃积分比r ≡ t′/|t|）以及电荷转移能Δ_CT联系起来。

Abstract: Copper-oxide high-temperature (high-$T_c$) superconductors host robust paramagnon excitations whose propagation energies are insensitive to hole concentration and correlate with maximal measured superconducting transition temperatures. Employing canonical Hubbard- and $t$-$J$-$U$ models of a $\mathrm{CuO_2}$ plane, we relate robust paramagnon energies to high-$T_c$ fermiology (via the ratio $r \equiv t^\prime/|t|$ of next-nearest- to nearest-neighbor hopping integrals) and charge transfer energy, $Δ_\mathrm{CT}$. It is shown that variation of $r$ and $Δ_\mathrm{CT}$ between materials has an opposite effect on paramagnon energy, rationalizing comparable bandwidth of magnetic excitations across multiple cuprates. *Ryosuke Yoshii,Rio Oto*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究方法是分析具有变号质量项（sign-changing mass term）的一维狄拉克系统中的拓扑孤子，该孤子承载局域零模（localized zero mode），其空间扩展的波函数导致与巡游电子（itinerant electrons）的动量依赖交换耦合（momentum-dependent exchange coupling）。

Result: 结果表明，孤子波函数结构产生非平凡的形式因子（nontrivial form factor），抑制高能散射过程，导致能量依赖的有效近藤耦合（energy-dependent effective Kondo coupling），从而使孤子的实空间结构直接控制涌现的近藤能标。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一种机制，通过该机制拓扑缺陷通过其波函数结构控制多体能量标度，提出了通过拓扑工程调控多体能量标度的一般原理（general principle）。

Abstract: We study the Kondo effect induced by a topological soliton in a one-dimensional Dirac system with the sign-changing mass term. The soliton hosts a localized zero mode whose spatially extended wavefunction leads to a momentum-dependent exchange coupling with itinerant electrons. We show that this structure generates a nontrivial form factor that suppresses high-energy scattering processes, resulting in an energy-dependent effective Kondo coupling. As a consequence, the real-space structure of the soliton directly controls the emergent Kondo scale. This work establishes a mechanism by which topological defects control many-body energy scales through their wavefunction structure, suggesting a general principle for engineering many-body energy scales via topology.

### [183] [Perturbations of Dirac Operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23453)
*Steffen Schmidt*

Main category: math.RT

TL;DR: 本文研究了基本经典李超代数（basic classical Lie superalgebras）相对三次狄拉克算子（relative cubic Dirac operators）的扰动，利用彩色量子Weil代数（colour quantum Weil algebra）的统一形式体系，提出了三类互补的扰动方法和相应不变量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索基本经典李超代数相对三次狄拉克算子的扰动理论，通过彩色量子Weil代数的统一形式体系，系统性地构建不同类型的扰动方法及其不变量。

Method: 采用彩色量子Weil代数的统一形式体系，定义了三种互补的扰动方法：半单扰动（semisimple perturbations）、幂零扰动（nilpotent perturbations）以及通过Weil协变微分（Weil-covariant differential）实现的形变。

Result: 半单扰动为每个有限维单超模（finite-dimensional simple supermodule）分配有限个半单轨道和测量非典型性（atypicality）程度的向量空间；幂零扰动产生结合狄拉克上同调（Dirac cohomology）和Duflo-Serganova上同调（Duflo--Serganova cohomology）的上同调理论族；Weil协变微分形变产生陈型不变量（Chern-type invariant），为每个有限维模分配Weil复形上同调中的自然类。

Conclusion: 通过彩色量子Weil代数的统一框架，成功构建了相对三次狄拉克算子的三类互补扰动方法，分别产生半单轨道结构、上同调理论族和陈型不变量，为李超代数表示理论提供了新的不变量体系。

Abstract: We study perturbations of relative cubic Dirac operators for basic classical Lie superalgebras within the uniform formalism of the colour quantum Weil algebra. This perspective leads to three complementary classes of perturbations and resulting invariants. First, we define semisimple perturbations that assign to each finite-dimensional simple supermodule a finite collection of semisimple orbits, together with canonically defined vector spaces measuring the degree of atypicality. Second, we introduce nilpotent perturbations parametrized by the self-commuting variety of a quadratic Lie subsuperalgebra; the resulting family of cohomology theories combines Dirac cohomology and Duflo--Serganova cohomology. Third, we deform the cubic Dirac operator by a Weil-covariant differential built from the universal $1$-form in the colour quantum Weil algebra and the Weil differential, producing a Chern-type invariant that assigns to each finite-dimensional module a natural class in the cohomology of the Weil complex.

# cs.AI [[Back]](#toc)

### [184] [Intelligence Inertia: Physical Principles and Applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22347)
*Jipeng Han*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了智能惯性（intelligence inertia）的概念及其物理原理，用于量化智能系统的计算成本。研究发现，规则与状态之间的非对易性（non-commutativity）导致适应成本呈现类相对论的J型膨胀曲线，形成静态模型无法识别的"计算墙"。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典框架如兰道尔原理（Landauer's principle）和费舍尔信息（Fisher Information）仅在稀疏规则约束下有效近似，无法解释高级智能系统重构时维持符号可解释性所引发的超线性计算与能量成本。需要新的物理原理来量化智能的计算权重。

Method: 通过分析实际适应成本与静态信息理论估计之间的差异，推导出非线性成本公式，该公式类似于洛伦兹因子（Lorentz factor），表征了相对论性的J型膨胀曲线。通过三个决定性实验验证物理原理：J曲线膨胀与经典费舍尔信息模型的比较、神经网络架构演化的"Z字形"轨迹几何分析，以及实现考虑智能体物理抵抗变化的惯性感知调度器包装器。

Result: 研究揭示了规则与状态之间的基本非对易性（non-commutativity）是智能惯性的根源，导致适应成本呈现类相对论的J型膨胀曲线，形成"计算墙"。惯性感知调度器包装器通过尊重智能体对变化的物理抵抗，优化了深度网络的训练。

Conclusion: 智能惯性及其物理原理为结构适应成本提供了统一的物理描述，首次从第一性原理解释了智能体中的计算和可解释性维护开销。该框架超越了经典信息理论模型的局限性，揭示了智能系统重构中的基本物理约束。

Abstract: While Landauer's principle establishes the fundamental thermodynamic floor for information erasure and Fisher Information provides a metric for local curvature in parameter space, these classical frameworks function effectively only as approximations within regimes of sparse rule-constraints. They fail to explain the super-linear, and often explosive, computational and energy costs incurred when maintaining symbolic interpretability during the reconfiguration of advanced intelligent systems. This paper introduces the property of intelligence inertia and its underlying physical principles as foundational characteristics for quantifying the computational weight of intelligence. We demonstrate that this phenomenon is not merely an empirical observation but originates from the fundamental non-commutativity between rules and states, a root cause we have formally organized into a rigorous mathematical framework. By analyzing the growing discrepancy between actual adaptation costs and static information-theoretic estimates, we derive a non-linear cost formula that mirrors the Lorentz factor, characterizing a relativistic J-shaped inflation curve -- a "computational wall" that static models are blind to. The validity of these physical principles is examined through a trilogy of decisive experiments: (1) a comparative adjudication of this J-curve inflation against classical Fisher Information models, (2) a geometric analysis of the "Zig-Zag" trajectory of neural architecture evolution, and (3) the implementation of an inertia-aware scheduler wrapper that optimizes the training of deep networks by respecting the agent's physical resistance to change. Our results suggest a unified physical description for the cost of structural adaptation, offering a first-principle explanation for the computational and interpretability-maintenance overhead in intelligent agents.

</details>


<div id='physics.atom-ph'></div>

# physics.atom-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [185] [In-orbit Test of the Weak Equivalence Principle with Atom Interferometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22981)
*Dan-Fang Zhang,Jing-Ting Li,Wen-Zhang Wang,Wei-Hao Xu,Jia-Yi Wei,Xiao Li,Yi-Bo Wang,Dong-Feng Gao,Jia-Qi Zhong,Biao Tang,Lin Zhou,Run-Bing Li,Huan-Yao Sun,Qun-Feng Chen,Lei Qin,Mei-zhen An,Zong-Feng Li,Shu-Quan Wang,Xiao-Xiao Guo,Yao Tian,Xi-He Yu,Hong-En Zhong,Xi Chen,Jin Wang,Ming-Sheng Zhan*

Main category: physics.atom-ph

TL;DR: 本研究首次在轨实现了弱等效原理（Weak Equivalence Principle, WEP）的量子测试，利用中国空间站上的双物种（85Rb/87Rb）原子干涉仪，将微重力环境下原子干涉WEP测试精度提高了三个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 弱等效原理（Weak Equivalence Principle, WEP）是广义相对论的核心支柱，利用量子系统在太空环境中进行精确测试为探索新物理提供了独特窗口。

Method: 研究在中国空间站上实现了双物种（85Rb/87Rb）原子干涉仪（atom interferometer），开发了平台运动抑制、荧光检测切换和双光子失谐切换等方法，以消除相位噪声并提高测量精度。

Result: 基于280天的WEP测试数据获得了2.8×10⁻⁸的测试不确定度，经误差估计后得到(-3.1±4.6)×10⁻⁷的测试结果，将微重力环境下原子干涉WEP测试精度提高了三个数量级。

Conclusion: 这项工作为星载量子惯性传感器及其在未来太空基础物理中的应用铺平了道路。

Abstract: The Weak Equivalence Principle (WEP) is a central pillar of general relativity. Its precise test with quantum systems in space offers a unique window onto new physics. Here we report the first in-orbit quantum test of the WEP. A dual-species (85Rb/87Rb) atom interferometer is realized aboard the China Space Station. Methods of platform motion suppression, fluorescence detection switching, and two-photon detuning switching are developed to eliminate phase noise and improve measurement accuracy. A test uncertainty of 2.8*10-8 is obtained from 280 days of WEP test data, and a test result of (-3.1+/-4.6)*10-7 is achieved after error estimation. This improves prior atom-interferometric WEP tests in microgravity by three orders of magnitude. This work paves the way for space-borne quantum inertial sensors and their application to future fundamental physics in space.

</details>
